 <hr><center><h1>Shri Guru Granth Sahib: Raag Raamkalee</h1></center>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 001</h2></center>
  Raamkalee, First Mehl, First House, Chau-Padas:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. Truth Is The Name. Creative Being Personified. No Fear. No Hatred. Image Of The Undying. Beyond Birth. Self-Existent. By Guru's Grace:<br>
  Some read the Sanskrit scriptures, and some read the Puraanas.<br>
  Some meditate on the Naam, the Name of the Lord, and chant it on their malas, focusing on it in meditation.<br>
  I know nothing, now or ever; I recognize only Your One Name, Lord. ||1||<br>
  I do not know, Lord, what my condition shall be.<br>
  I am foolish and ignorant; I seek Your Sanctuary, God. Please, save my honor and my self-respect. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Sometimes, the soul soars high in the heavens, and sometimes it falls to the depths of the nether regions.<br>
  The greedy soul does not remain stable; it searches in the four directions. ||2||<br>
  With death pre-ordained, the soul comes into the world, gathering the riches of life.<br>
  I see that some have already gone, O my Lord and Master; the burning fire is coming closer! ||3||<br>
  No one has any friend, and no one has any brother; no one has any father or mother.<br>
  Prays Nanak, if You bless me with Your Name, it shall be my help and support in the end. ||4||1||<br>
  Raamkalee, First Mehl:<br>
  Your Light is prevailing everywhere.<br>
  Wherever I look, there I see the Lord. ||1||<br>
  Please rid me of the desire to live, O my Lord and Master.<br>
  My mind is entangled in the deep dark pit of Maya. How can I cross over, O Lord and Master? ||1||Pause||<br>
  He dwells deep within, inside the heart; how can He not be outside as well?<br>
  Our Lord and Master always takes care of us, and keeps us in His thoughts. ||2||<br>
  He Himself is near at hand, and He is far away.<br>
  He Himself is all-pervading, permeating everywhere.<br>
  Meeting the True Guru, the darkness is dispelled.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 002</h2></center>
  Wherever I look, there I see Him pervading. ||3||<br>
  There is doubt within me, and Maya is outside; it hits me in the eyes like an arrow.<br>
  Prays Nanak, the slave of the Lord's slaves: such a mortal suffers terribly. ||4||2||<br>
  Raamkalee, First Mehl:<br>
  Where is that door, where You live, O Lord? What is that door called? Among all doors, who can find that door?<br>
  For the sake of that door, I wander around sadly, detached from the world; if only someone would come and tell me about that door. ||1||<br>
  How can I cross over the world-ocean?<br>
  While I am living, I cannot be dead. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Pain is the door, and anger is the guard; hope and anxiety are the two shutters.<br>
  Maya is the water in the moat; in the middle of this moat, he has built his home. The Primal Lord sits in the Seat of Truth. ||2||<br>
  You have so many Names, Lord, I do not know their limit. There is no other equal to You.<br>
  Do not speak out loud - remain in your mind. The Lord Himself knows, and He Himself acts. ||3||<br>
  As long as there is hope, there is anxiety; so how can anyone speak of the One Lord?<br>
  In the midst of hope, remain untouched by hope; then, O Nanak, you shall meet the One Lord. ||4||<br>
  In this way, you shall cross over the world-ocean.<br>
  This is the way to remain dead while yet alive. ||1||Second Pause||3||<br>
  Raamkalee, First Mehl:<br>
  Awareness of the Shabad and the Teachings is my horn; the people hear the sound of its vibrations.<br>
  Honor is my begging-bowl, and the Naam, the Name of the Lord, is the charity I receive. ||1||<br>
  O Baba, Gorakh is the Lord of the Universe; He is always awake and aware.<br>
  He alone is Gorakh, who sustains the earth; He created it in an instant. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Binding together water and air, He infused the breath of life into the body, and made the lamps of the sun and the moon.<br>
  To die and to live, He gave us the earth, but we have forgotten these blessings. ||2||<br>
  There are so many Siddhas, seekers, Yogis, wandering pilgrims, spiritual teachers and good people.<br>
  If I meet them, I chant the Lord's Praises, and then, my mind serves Him. ||3||<br>
  Paper and salt, protected by ghee, remain untouched by water, as the lotus remains unaffected in water.<br>
  Those who meet with such devotees, O servant Nanak - what can death do to them? ||4||4||<br>
  Raamkalee, First Mehl:<br>
  Listen, Machhindra, to what Nanak says.<br>
  One who subdues the five passions does not waver.<br>
  One who practices Yoga in such a way,<br>
  saves himself, and saves all his generations. ||1||<br>
  He alone is a hermit, who attains such understanding.<br>
  Day and night, he remains absorbed in deepest Samaadhi. ||1||Pause||<br>
  He begs for loving devotion to the Lord, and lives in the Fear of God.<br>
  He is satisfied, with the priceless gift of contentment.<br>
  Becoming the embodiment of meditation, he attains the true Yogic posture.<br>
  He focuses his consciousness in the deep trance of the True Name. ||2||<br>
  Nanak chants the Ambrosial Bani.<br>
  Listen, O Machhindra: this is the insignia of the true hermit.<br>
  One who, in the midst of hope, remains untouched by hope,<br>
  shall truly find the Creator Lord. ||3||<br>
  Prays Nanak, I share the mysterious secrets of God.<br>
  The Guru and His disciple are joined together!<br>
  One who eats this food, this medicine of the Teachings,<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 003</h2></center>
  has the wisdom of the six Shaastras. ||4||5||<br>
  Raamkalee, First Mehl:<br>
  My boat is wobbly and unsteady; it is filled with sins. The wind is rising - what if it tips over?<br>
  As sunmukh, I have turned to the Guru; O my Perfect Master; please be sure to bless me with Your glorious greatness. ||1||<br>
  O Guru, my Saving Grace, please carry me across the world-ocean.<br>
  Bless me with devotion to the perfect, imperishable Lord God; I am a sacrifice to You. ||1||Pause||<br>
  He alone is a Siddha, a seeker, a Yogi, a wandering pilgrim, who meditates on the One Perfect Lord.<br>
  Touching the feet of the Lord Master, they are emancipated; they come to receive the Word of the Teachings. ||2||<br>
  I know nothing of charity, meditation, self-discipline or religious rituals; I only chant Your Name, God.<br>
  Nanak has met the Guru, the Transcendent Lord God; through the True Word of His Shabad, he is set free. ||3||6||<br>
  Raamkalee, First Mehl:<br>
  Focus your consciousness in deep absorption on the Lord.<br>
  Make your body a raft, to cross over.<br>
  Deep within is the fire of desire; keep it in check.<br>
  Day and night, that lamp shall burn unceasingly. ||1||<br>
  Float such a lamp upon the water;<br>
  this lamp will bring total understanding. ||1||Pause||<br>
  This understanding is good clay;<br>
  a lamp made of such clay is acceptable to the Lord.<br>
  So shape this lamp on the wheel of good actions.<br>
  In this world and in the next, this lamp shall be with you. ||2||<br>
  When He Himself grants His Grace,<br>
  then, as Gurmukh, one may understand Him.<br>
  Within the heart, this lamp is permanently lit.<br>
  It is not extinguished by water or wind.<br>
  Such a lamp will carry you across the water. ||3||<br>
  Wind does not shake it, or put it out.<br>
  Its light reveals the Divine Throne.<br>
  The Kh'shaatriyas, Brahmins, Soodras and Vaishyas<br>
  cannot find its value, even by thousands of calculations.<br>
  If any of them lights such a lamp,<br>
  O Nanak, he is emancipated. ||4||7||<br>
  Raamkalee, First Mehl:<br>
  To place one's faith in Your Name, Lord, is true worship.<br>
  With an offering of Truth, one obtains a place to sit.<br>
  If a prayer is offered with truth and contentment,<br>
  the Lord will hear it, and call him in to sit by Him. ||1||<br>
  O Nanak, no one returns empty-handed;<br>
  such is the Court of the True Lord. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The treasure I seek is the gift of Your Grace.<br>
  Please bless this humble beggar - this is what I seek.<br>
  Please, pour Your Love into the cup of my heart.<br>
  This is Your pre-determined value. ||2||<br>
  The One who created everything, does everything.<br>
  He Himself appraises His own value.<br>
  The Sovereign Lord King becomes manifest to the Gurmukh.<br>
  He does not come, and He does not go. ||3||<br>
  People curse at the beggar; by begging, he does not receive honor.<br>
  O Lord, You inspire me to speak Your Words, and tell the Story of Your Court. ||4||8||<br>
  Raamkalee, First Mehl:<br>
  The drop is in the ocean, and the ocean is in the drop. Who understands, and knows this?<br>
  He Himself creates the wondrous play of the world. He Himself contemplates it, and understands its true essence. ||1||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 004</h2></center>
  How rare are those who contemplate this spiritual wisdom.<br>
  Through this, the supreme state of liberation is attained. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The night is in the day, and the day is in the night. The same is true of hot and cold.<br>
  No one else knows His state and extent; without the Guru, this is not understood. ||2||<br>
  The female is in the male, and the male is in the female. Understand this, O God-realized being!<br>
  The meditation is in the music, and knowledge is in meditation. Become Gurmukh, and speak the Unspoken Speech. ||3||<br>
  The Light is in the mind, and the mind is in the Light. The Guru brings the five senses together, like brothers.<br>
  Nanak is forever a sacrifice to those who enshrine love for the One Word of the Shabad. ||4||9||<br>
  Raamkalee, First Mehl:<br>
  When the Lord God showered His Mercy,<br>
  egotism was eradicated from within me.<br>
  That humble servant who contemplates the Word of the Guru's Shabad, is very dear to the Lord. ||1||<br>
  That humble servant of the Lord is pleasing to his Lord God;<br>
  day and night, he performs devotional worship, day and night. Disregarding his own honor, he sings the Glorious Praises of the Lord. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The unstruck melody of the sound current resonates and resounds;<br>
  my mind is appeased by the subtle essence of the Lord.<br>
  Through the Perfect Guru, I am absorbed in Truth.<br>
  Through the Guru, I have found the Lord, the Primal Being. ||2||<br>
  Gurbani is the sound current of the Naad, the Vedas, everything.<br>
  My mind is attuned to the Lord of the Universe.<br>
  He is my sacred shrine of pilgrimage, fasting and austere self-discipline.<br>
  The Lord saves, and carries across, those who meet with the Guru. ||3||<br>
  One whose self-conceit is gone, sees his fears run away.<br>
  That servant grasps the Guru's feet.<br>
  The Guru, the True Guru, has expelled my doubts.<br>
  Says Nanak, I have merged into the Word of the Shabad. ||4||10||<br>
  Raamkalee, First Mehl:<br>
  He runs around, begging for clothes and food.<br>
  He burns with hunger and corruption, and will suffer in the world hereafter.<br>
  He does not follow the Guru's Teachings; through his evil-mindedness, he loses his honor.<br>
  Only through the Guru's Teachings will such a person become devoted. ||1||<br>
  The way of the Yogi is to dwell in the celestial home of bliss.<br>
  He looks impartially, equally upon all. He receives the charity of the Lord's Love, and the Word of the Shabad, and so he is satisfied. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The five bulls, the senses, pull the wagon of the body around.<br>
  By the Lord's power, one's honor is preserved.<br>
  But when the axle breaks, the wagon falls and crashes.<br>
  It falls apart, like a pile of logs. ||2||<br>
  Contemplate the Word of the Guru's Shabad, Yogi.<br>
  Look upon pain and pleasure as one and the same, sorrow and separation.<br>
  Let your food be contemplative meditation upon the Naam, the Name of the Lord, and the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  Your wall shall be permanent, by meditating on the Formless Lord. ||3||<br>
  Wear the loin-cloth of poise, and be free of entanglements.<br>
  The Guru's Word shall release you from sexual desire and anger.<br>
  In your mind, let your ear-rings be the Sanctuary of the Guru, the Lord.<br>
  O Nanak, worshipping the Lord in deep devotion, the humble are carried across. ||4||11||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 005</h2></center>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Raamkalee, Third Mehl, First House:<br>
  In the Golden Age of Sat Yuga, everyone spoke the Truth.<br>
  In each and every home, devotional worship was performed by the people, according to the Guru's Teachings.<br>
  In that Golden Age, Dharma had four feet.<br>
  How rare are those people who, as Gurmukh, contemplate this and understand. ||1||<br>
  In all four ages, the Naam, the Name of the Lord, is glory and greatness.<br>
  One who holds tight to the Naam is liberated; without the Guru, no one obtains the Naam. ||1||Pause||<br>
  In the Silver Age of Traytaa Yuga, one leg was removed.<br>
  Hypocrisy became prevalent, and people thought that the Lord was far away.<br>
  The Gurmukhs still understood and realized;<br>
  the Naam abided deep within them, and they were at peace. ||2||<br>
  In the Brass Age of Dwaapur Yuga, duality and double-mindedness arose.<br>
  Deluded by doubt, they knew duality.<br>
  In this Brass Age, Dharma was left with only two feet.<br>
  Those who became Gurmukh implanted the Naam deep within. ||3||<br>
  In the Iron Age of Kali Yuga, Dharma was left with only one power.<br>
  It walks on just one foot; love and emotional attachment to Maya have increased.<br>
  Love and emotional attachment to Maya bring total darkness.<br>
  If someone meets the True Guru, he is saved, through the Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||4||<br>
  Throughout the ages, there is only the One True Lord.<br>
  Among all, is the True Lord; there is no other at all.<br>
  Praising the True Lord, true peace is attained.<br>
  How rare are those, who as Gurmukh, chant the Naam. ||5||<br>
  Throughout all the ages, the Naam is the ultimate, the most sublime.<br>
  How rare are those, who as Gurmukh, understand this.<br>
  One who meditates on the Lord's Name is a humble devotee.<br>
  O Nanak, in each and every age, the Naam is glory and greatness. ||6||1||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fourth Mehl, First House:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  If someone is very fortunate, and is blessed with great high destiny, then he meditates on the Name of the Lord, Har, Har.<br>
  Chanting the Naam, the Name of the Lord, he finds peace, and merges in the Naam. ||1||<br>
  O mortal, as Gurmukh, worship the Lord in devotion forever.<br>
  Your heart shall be illumined; through the Guru's Teachings, lovingly attune yourself to the Lord. You shall merge in the Name of the Lord, Har, Har. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The Great Giver is filled with diamonds, emeralds, rubies and pearls;<br>
  one who has good fortune and great destiny inscribed upon his forehead, digs them out, by following the Guru's Teachings. ||2||<br>
  The Lord's Name is the jewel, the emerald, the ruby; digging it out, the Guru has placed it in your palm.<br>
  The unfortunate, self-willed manmukh does not obtain it; this priceless jewel remains hidden behind a curtain of straw. ||3||<br>
  If such pre-ordained destiny is written upon one's forehead, then the True Guru enjoins him to serve Him.<br>
  O Nanak, then he obtains the jewel, the gem; blessed, blessed is that one who follows the Guru's Teachings, and finds the Lord. ||4||1||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fourth Mehl:<br>
  Meeting with the humble servants of the Lord, I am in ecstasy; they preach the sublime sermon of the Lord.<br>
  The filth of evil-mindedness is totally washed away; joining the Sat Sangat, the True Congregation, one is blessed with understanding. ||1||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 006</h2></center>
  O humble servant of the Lord, follow the Guru's Teachings, and chant the Name of the Lord.<br>
  Whoever hears and speaks it is liberated; chanting the Lord's Name, one is embellished with beauty. ||1||Pause||<br>
  If someone has supremely high destiny written on his forehead, the Lord leads him to meet the humble servants of the Lord.<br>
  Be merciful, and grant me the Blessed Vision of the Saints' Darshan, which shall rid me of all poverty and pain. ||2||<br>
  The Lord's people are good and sublime; the unfortunate ones do not like them at all.<br>
  The more the Lord's exalted servants speak of Him, the more the slanderers attack and sting them. ||3||<br>
  Cursed, cursed are the slanderers who do not like the humble, the friends and companions of the Lord.<br>
  Those who do not like the honor and glory of the Guru are faithless, black-faced thieves, who have turned their backs on the Lord. ||4||<br>
  Have mercy, have mercy, please save me, Dear Lord. I am meek and humble - I seek Your protection.<br>
  I am Your child, and You are my father, God. Please forgive servant Nanak and merge him with Yourself. ||5||2||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fourth Mehl:<br>
  The friends of the Lord, the humble, Holy Saints are sublime; the Lord spreads out His protecting hands above them.<br>
  The Gurmukhs are the Holy Saints, pleasing to God; in His mercy, He blends them with Himself. ||1||<br>
  O Lord, my mind longs to meet with the humble servants of the Lord.<br>
  The sweet, subtle essence of the Lord is immortalizing ambrosia. Meeting the Saints, I drink it in. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The Lord's people are the most lofty and exalted. Meeting with them, the most exalted status is obtained.<br>
  I am the slave of the slave of the Lord's slaves; my Lord and Master is pleased with me. ||2||<br>
  The humble servant serves; one who enshrines love for the Lord in his heart, mind and body is very fortunate.<br>
  One who talks too much without love, speaks falsely, and obtains only false rewards. ||3||<br>
  Take pity on me, O Lord of the World, O Great Giver; let me fall at the feet of the Saints.<br>
  I would cut off my head, and cut it into pieces, O Nanak, and set it down for the Saints to walk upon. ||4||3||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fourth Mehl:<br>
  If I am blessed with supreme high destiny, I will meet the humble servants of the Lord, without delay.<br>
  The Lord's humble servants are pools of ambrosial nectar; by great good fortune, one bathes in them. ||1||<br>
  O Lord, let me work for the humble servants of the Lord.<br>
  I carry water, wave the fan and grind the corn for them; I massage and wash their feet. I apply the dust of their feet to my forehead. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The Lord's humble servants are great, very great, the greatest and most exalted; they lead us to meet the True Guru.<br>
  No one else is as great as the True Guru; meeting the True Guru, I meditate on the Lord, the Primal Being. ||2||<br>
  Those who seek the Sanctuary of the True Guru find the Lord. My Lord and Master saves their honor.<br>
  Some come for their own purposes, and sit before the Guru; they pretend to be in Samaadhi, like storks with their eyes closed. ||3||<br>
  Associating with the wretched and the lowly, like the stork and the crow, is like feeding on a carcass of poison.<br>
  Nanak: O God, unite me with the Sangat, the Congregation. United with the Sangat, I will become a swan. ||4||4||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 007</h2></center>
  Raamkalee, Fourth Mehl:<br>
  O True Guru, please be kind, and unite me with the Lord. My Sovereign Lord is the Beloved of my breath of life.<br>
  I am a slave; I fall at the Guru's feet. He has shown me the Path, the Way to my Lord God. ||1||<br>
  The Name of my Lord, Har, Har, is pleasing to my mind.<br>
  I have no friend except the Lord; the Lord is my father, my mother, my companion. ||1||Pause||<br>
  My breath of life will not survive for an instant, without my Beloved; unless I see Him, I will die, O my mother!<br>
  Blessed, blessed is my great, high destiny, that I have come to the Guru's Sanctuary. Meeting with the Guru, I have obtained the Blessed Vision of the Lord's Darshan. ||2||<br>
  I do not know or understand any other within my mind; I meditate and chant the Lord's Chant.<br>
  Those who lack the Naam, wander in shame; their noses are chopped off, bit by bit. ||3||<br>
  O Life of the World, rejuvenate me! O my Lord and Master, enshrine Your Name deep within my heart.<br>
  O Nanak, perfect is the Guru, the Guru. Meeting the True Guru, I meditate on the Naam. ||4||5||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fourth Mehl:<br>
  The True Guru, the Great Giver, is the Great, Primal Being; meeting Him, the Lord is enshrined within the heart.<br>
  The Perfect Guru has granted me the life of the soul; I meditate in remembrance on the Ambrosial Name of the Lord. ||1||<br>
  O Lord, the Guru has implanted the Name of the Lord, Har, Har, within my heart.<br>
  As Gurmukh, I have heard His sermon, which pleases my mind; blessed, blessed is my great destiny. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Millions, three hundred thirty millions of gods meditate on Him, but they cannot find His end or limitation.<br>
  With sexual urges in their hearts, they beg for beautiful women; stretching out their hands, they beg for riches. ||2||<br>
  One who chants the Praises of the Lord is the greatest of the great; the Gurmukh keeps the Lord clasped to his heart.<br>
  If one is blessed with high destiny, he meditates on the Lord, who carries him across the terrifying world-ocean. ||3||<br>
  The Lord is close to His humble servant, and His humble servant is close to the Lord; He keeps His humble servant clasped to His Heart.<br>
  O Nanak, the Lord God is our father and mother. I am His child; the Lord cherishes me. ||4||6||18||<br>
  Raag Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl, First House:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Have mercy on me, O Generous Giver, Lord of the meek; please do not consider my merits and demerits.<br>
  How can dust be washed? O my Lord and Master, such is the state of mankind. ||1||<br>
  O my mind, serve the True Guru, and be at peace.<br>
  Whatever you desire, you shall receive that reward, and you shall not be afflicted by pain any longer. ||1||Pause||<br>
  He creates and adorns the earthen vessels; He infuses His Light within them.<br>
  As is the destiny pre-ordained by the Creator, so are the deeds we do. ||2||<br>
  He believes the mind and body are all his own; this is the cause of his coming and going.<br>
  He does not think of the One who gave him these; he is blind, entangled in emotional attachment. ||3||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 008</h2></center>
  One who knows that God created him, reaches the Incomparable Mansion of the Lord's Presence.<br>
  Worshipping the Lord, I sing His Glorious Praises. Nanak is Your slave. ||4||1||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Place yourself beneath all men's feet, and you will be uplifted; serve Him in this way.<br>
  Know that all are above you, and you shall find peace in the Court of the Lord. ||1||<br>
  O Saints, speak that speech which purifies the gods and sanctifies the divine beings. As Gurmukh, chant the Word of His Bani, even for an instant. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Renounce your fraudulent plans, and dwell in the celestial palace; do not call anyone else false.<br>
  Meeting with the True Guru, you shall receive the nine treasures; in this way, you shall find the essence of reality. ||2||<br>
  Eradicate doubt, and as Gurmukh, enshrine love for the Lord; understand your own soul, O Siblings of Destiny.<br>
  Know that God is near at hand, and ever-present. How could you try to hurt anyone else? ||3||<br>
  Meeting with the True Guru, your path shall be clear, and you shall easily meet your Lord and Master.<br>
  Blessed, blessed are those humble beings, who, in this Dark Age of Kali Yuga, find the Lord. Nanak is forever a sacrifice to them. ||4||2||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Coming does not please me, and going does not bring me pain, and so my mind is not afflicted by disease.<br>
  I am in bliss forever, for I have found the Perfect Guru; my separation from the Lord is totally ended. ||1||<br>
  This is how I have joined my mind to the Lord.<br>
  Attachment, sorrow, disease and public opinion do not affect me, and so, I enjoy the subtle essence of the Lord, Har, Har, Har. ||1||Pause||<br>
  I am pure in the heavenly realm, pure on this earth, and pure in the nether regions of the underworld. I remain apart from the people of the world.<br>
  Obedient to the Lord, I enjoy peace forever; wherever I look, I see the Lord of glorious virtues. ||2||<br>
  There is no Shiva or Shakti, no energy or matter, no water or wind, no world of form there,<br>
  where the True Guru, the Yogi, dwells, where the Imperishable Lord God, the Unapproachable Master abides. ||3||<br>
  Body and mind belong to the Lord; all wealth belongs to the Lord; what glorious virtues of the Lord can I describe?<br>
  Says Nanak, the Guru has destroyed my sense of 'mine and yours'. Like water with water, I am blended with God. ||4||3||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  It is beyond the three qualities; it remains untouched. The seekers and Siddhas do not know it.<br>
  There is a chamber filled with jewels, overflowing with Ambrosial Nectar, in the Guru's Treasury. ||1||<br>
  This thing is wonderful and amazing! It cannot be described.<br>
  It is an unfathomable object, O Siblings of Destiny! ||1||Pause||<br>
  Its value cannot be estimated at all; what can anyone say about it?<br>
  By speaking and describing it, it cannot be understood; only one who sees it realizes it. ||2||<br>
  Only the Creator Lord knows it; what can any poor creature do?<br>
  Only He Himself knows His own state and extent. The Lord Himself is the treasure overflowing. ||3||<br>
  Tasting such Ambrosial Nectar, the mind remains satisfied and satiated.<br>
  Says Nanak, my hopes are fulfilled; I have found the Guru's Sanctuary. ||4||4||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 009</h2></center>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  God has made me His own, and vanquished all my enemies.<br>
  Those enemies who have plundered this world, have all been placed in bondage. ||1||<br>
  The True Guru is my Transcendent Lord.<br>
  I enjoy countless pleasures of power and tasty delights, chanting Your Name, and placing my faith in You. ||1||Pause||<br>
  I do not think of any other at all. The Lord is my protector, above my head.<br>
  I am carefree and independent, when I have the Support of Your Name, O my Lord and Master. ||2||<br>
  I have become perfect, meeting with the Giver of peace, and now, I lack nothing at all.<br>
  I have obtained the essence of excellence, the supreme status; I shall not forsake it to go anywhere else. ||3||<br>
  I cannot describe how You are, O True Lord, unseen, infinite,<br>
  immeasurable, unfathomable and unmoving Lord. O Nanak, He is my Lord and Master. ||4||5||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  You are wise; You are eternal and unchanging. You are my social class and honor.<br>
  You are unmoving - You never move at all. How can I be worried? ||1||<br>
  You alone are the One and only Lord;<br>
  You alone are the king.<br>
  By Your Grace, I have found peace. ||1||Pause||<br>
  You are the ocean, and I am Your swan; the pearls and rubies are in You.<br>
  You give, and You do not hesitate for an instant; I receive, forever enraptured. ||2||<br>
  I am Your child, and You are my father; You place the milk in my mouth.<br>
  I play with You, and You caress me in every way. You are forever the ocean of excellence. ||3||<br>
  You are perfect, perfectly all-pervading; I am fulfilled with You as well.<br>
  I am merged, merged, merged and remain merged; O Nanak, I cannot describe it! ||4||6||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Make your hands the cymbals, your eyes the tambourines, and your forehead the guitar you play.<br>
  Let the sweet flute music resound in your ears, and with your tongue, vibrate this song.<br>
  Move your mind like the rhythmic hand-motions; do the dance, and shake your ankle bracelets. ||1||<br>
  This is the rhythmic dance of the Lord.<br>
  The Merciful Audience, the Lord, sees all your make-up and decorations. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The whole earth is the stage, with the canopy of the sky overhead.<br>
  The wind is the director; people are born of water.<br>
  From the five elements, the puppet was created with its actions. ||2||<br>
  The sun and the moon are the two lamps which shine, with the four corners of the world placed between them.<br>
  The ten senses are the dancing girls, and the five passions are the chorus; they sit together within the one body.<br>
  They all put on their own shows, and speak in different languages. ||3||<br>
  In each and every home there is dancing, day and night; in each and every home, the bugles blow.<br>
  Some are made to dance, and some are whirled around; some come and some go, and some are reduced to dust.<br>
  Says Nanak, one who meets with the True Guru, does not have to dance the dance of reincarnation again. ||4||7||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 010</h2></center>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  He sings the song of the One Universal Creator; he sings the tune of the One Lord.<br>
  He lives in the land of the One Lord, shows the way to the One Lord, and remains attuned to the One Lord.<br>
  He centers his consciousness on the One Lord, and serves only the One Lord, who is known through the Guru. ||1||<br>
  Blessed and good is such a kirtanee, who sings such Praises.<br>
  He sings the Glorious Praises of the Lord,<br>
  and renounces the entanglements and pursuits of Maya. ||1||Pause||<br>
  He makes the five virtues, like contentment, his musical instruments, and plays the seven notes of the love of the Lord.<br>
  The notes he plays are the renunciation of pride and power; his feet keep the beat on the straight path.<br>
  He does not enter the cycle of reincarnation ever again; he keeps the One Word of the Shabad tied to the hem of his robe. ||2||<br>
  To play like Naarad, is to know that the Lord is ever-present.<br>
  The tinkling of the ankle bells is the shedding of sorrows and worries.<br>
  The dramatic gestures of acting are celestial bliss.<br>
  Such a dancer is not reincarnated again. ||3||<br>
  If anyone, out of millions of people, becomes pleasing to his Lord and Master, he sings the Lord's Praises in this way.<br>
  I have taken the Support of the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy.<br>
  Says Nanak, the Kirtan of the One Lord's Praises are sung there. ||4||8||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Some call Him, 'Raam, Raam', and some call Him, 'Khudaa-i'.<br>
  Some serve Him as 'Gusain', others as 'Allaah'. ||1||<br>
  He is the Cause of causes, the Generous Lord.<br>
  He showers His Grace and Mercy upon us. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Some bathe at sacred shrines of pilgrimage, and some make the pilgrimage to Mecca.|<br>
  Some perform devotional worship services, and some bow their heads in prayer. ||2||<br>
  Some read the Vedas, and some the Koran.<br>
  Some wear blue robes, and some wear white. ||3||<br>
  Some call themselves Muslim, and some call themselves Hindu.<br>
  Some yearn for paradise, and others long for heaven. ||4||<br>
  Says Nanak, one who realizes the Hukam of God's Will,<br>
  knows the secrets of his Lord and Master. ||5||9||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The wind merges into the wind.<br>
  The light blends into the light.<br>
  The dust becomes one with the dust.<br>
  What support is there for the one who is lamenting? ||1||<br>
  Who has died? O, who has died?<br>
  O God-realized beings, meet together and consider this. What a wondrous thing has happened! ||1||Pause||<br>
  No one knows what happens after death.<br>
  The one who is lamenting will also arise and depart.<br>
  Mortal beings are bound by the bonds of doubt and attachment.<br>
  When life becomes a dream, the blind man babbles and grieves in vain. ||2||<br>
  The Creator Lord created this creation.<br>
  It comes and goes, subject to the Will of the Infinite Lord.<br>
  No one dies; no one is capable of dying.<br>
  The soul does not perish; it is imperishable. ||3||<br>
  That which is known, does not exist.<br>
  I am a sacrifice to the one who knows this.<br>
  Says Nanak, the Guru has dispelled my doubt.<br>
  No one dies; no one comes or goes. ||4||10||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Meditate on the Lord of the Universe, the Beloved Lord of the World.<br>
  Meditating in remembrance on the Lord's Name, you shall live, and the Great Death shall not consume you ever again. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Through millions of incarnations, you have come, wandering, wandering, wandering.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 011</h2></center>
  By the highest destiny, you found the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy. ||1||<br>
  Without the Perfect Guru, no one is saved.<br>
  This is what Baba Nanak says, after deep reflection. ||2||11||<br>
  Raag Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl, Second House:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  The four Vedas proclaim it, but you don't believe them.<br>
  The six Shaastras also say one thing.<br>
  The eighteen Puraanas all speak of the One God.<br>
  Even so, Yogi, you do not understand this mystery. ||1||<br>
  The celestial harp plays the incomparable melody,<br>
  but in your intoxication, you do not hear it, O Yogi. ||1||Pause||<br>
  In the first age, the Golden Age, the village of truth was inhabited.<br>
  In the Silver Age of Traytaa Yuga, things began to decline.<br>
  In the Brass Age of Dwaapur Yuga, half of it was gone.<br>
  Now, only one leg of Truth remains, and the One Lord is revealed. ||2||<br>
  The beads are strung upon the one thread.<br>
  By means of many, various, diverse knots, they are tied, and kept separate on the string.<br>
  The beads of the mala are lovingly chanted upon in many ways.<br>
  When the thread is pulled out, the beads come together in one place. ||3||<br>
  Throughout the four ages, the One Lord made the body His temple.<br>
  It is a treacherous place, with several windows.<br>
  Searching and searching, one comes to the Lord's door.<br>
  Then, O Nanak, the Yogi attains a home in the Mansion of the Lord's Presence. ||4||<br>
  Thus, the celestial harp plays the incomparable melody;<br>
  hearing it, the Yogi's mind finds it sweet. ||1||Second Pause||1||12||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The body is a patch-work of threads.<br>
  The muscles are stitched together with the needles of the bones.<br>
  The Lord has erected a pillar of water.<br>
  O Yogi, why are you so proud? ||1||<br>
  Meditate on your Lord Master, day and night.<br>
  The patched coat of the body shall last for only a few days. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Smearing ashes on your body, you sit in a deep meditative trance.<br>
  You wear the ear-rings of 'mine and yours'.<br>
  You beg for bread, but you are not satisfied.<br>
  Abandoning your Lord Master, you beg from others; you should feel ashamed. ||2||<br>
  Your consciousness is restless, Yogi, as you sit in your Yogic postures.<br>
  You blow your horn, but still feel sad.<br>
  You do not understand Gorakh, your guru.<br>
  Again and again, Yogi, you come and go. ||3||<br>
  He, unto whom the Master shows Mercy<br>
  - unto Him, the Guru, the Lord of the World, I offer my prayer.<br>
  One who has the Name as his patched coat, and the Name as his robe,<br>
  O servant Nanak, such a Yogi is steady and stable. ||4||<br>
  One who meditates on the Master in this way, night and day,<br>
  finds the Guru, the Lord of the World, in this life. ||1||Second Pause||2||13||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  He is the Creator, the Cause of causes;<br>
  I do not see any other at all.<br>
  My Lord and Master is wise and all-knowing.<br>
  Meeting with the Gurmukh, I enjoy His Love. ||1||<br>
  Such is the sweet, subtle essence of the Lord.<br>
  How rare are those who, as Gurmukh, taste it. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The Light of the Ambrosial Name of the Lord is immaculate and pure.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 012</h2></center>
  Drinking it in, one becomes immortal and free of desire.<br>
  The body and mind are cooled and soothed, and the fire is extinguished.<br>
  Such a being is the embodiment of bliss, famous throughout the world. ||2||<br>
  What can I offer You, Lord? Everything belongs to You.<br>
  I am forever a sacrifice to You, hundreds of thousands of times.<br>
  You blessed me, and fashioned my body, mind and soul.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, this lowly being was exalted. ||3||<br>
  Opening the door, You summoned me to the Mansion of Your Presence.<br>
  As You are, so You have revealed Yourself to me.<br>
  Says Nanak, the screen is totally torn away;<br>
  I am Yours, and You are enshrined within my mind. ||4||3||14||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  He has linked His servant to His service.<br>
  The Divine Guru has poured the Ambrosial Naam, the Name of the Lord, into his mouth.<br>
  He has subdued all his anxiety.<br>
  I am forever a sacrifice to that Guru. ||1||<br>
  The True Guru has perfectly resolved my affairs.<br>
  The True Guru vibrates the unstruck melody of the sound current. ||1||Pause||<br>
  His Glory is profound and unfathomable.<br>
  One whom He blesses with patience becomes blissful.<br>
  One whose bonds are shattered by the Sovereign Lord<br>
  is not cast into the womb of reincarnation again. ||2||<br>
  One who is illuminated by the Lord's radiance within,<br>
  is not touched by pain and sorrow.<br>
  He holds in his robe the gems and jewels.<br>
  That humble being is saved, along with all his generations. ||3||<br>
  He has no doubt, double-mindedness or duality at all.<br>
  He worships and adores the One Immaculate Lord alone.<br>
  Wherever I look, I see the Merciful Lord.<br>
  Says Nanak, I have found God, the source of nectar. ||4||4||15||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  My self-conceit has been eliminated from my body.<br>
  The Will of God is dear to me.<br>
  Whatever He does, seems sweet to my mind.<br>
  And then, these eyes behold the wondrous Lord. ||1||<br>
  Now, I have become wise and my demons are gone.<br>
  My thirst is quenched, and my attachment is dispelled. The Perfect Guru has instructed me. ||1||Pause||<br>
  In His Mercy, the Guru has kept me under His protection.<br>
  The Guru has attached me to the Lord's Feet.<br>
  When the mind is totally held in check,<br>
  one sees the Guru and the Supreme Lord God as one and the same. ||2||<br>
  Whoever You have created, I am his slave.<br>
  My God dwells in all.<br>
  I have no enemies, no adversaries.<br>
  I walk arm in arm, like brothers, with all. ||3||<br>
  One whom the Guru, the Lord, blesses with peace,<br>
  does not suffer in pain any longer.<br>
  He Himself cherishes all.<br>
  Nanak is imbued with the love of the Lord of the World. ||4||5||16||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  You read the scriptures, and the commentaries,<br>
  but the Perfect Lord does not dwell in your heart.<br>
  You preach to others to have faith,<br>
  but you do not practice what you preach. ||1||<br>
  O Pandit, O religious scholar, contemplate the Vedas.<br>
  Eradicate anger from your mind, O Pandit. ||1||Pause||<br>
  You place your stone god before yourself,<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 013</h2></center>
  but your mind wanders in the ten directions.<br>
  You apply a ceremonial tilak mark to its forehead, and fall at its feet.<br>
  You try to appease the people, and act blindly. ||2||<br>
  You perform the six religious rituals, and sit wearing your loin-cloth.<br>
  In the homes of the wealthy, you read the prayer book.<br>
  You chant on your mala, and beg for money.<br>
  No one has ever been saved in this way, friend. ||3||<br>
  He alone is a Pandit, who lives the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  Maya, of the three qualities, leaves him.<br>
  The four Vedas are completely contained within the Lord's Name.<br>
  Nanak seeks His Sanctuary. ||4||6||17||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Millions of troubles do not come near him;<br>
  the many manifestations of Maya are his hand-maidens;<br>
  countless sins are his water-carriers;<br>
  he is blessed with the Grace of the Creator Lord. ||1||<br>
  One who has the Lord God as his help and support<br>
  - all his efforts are fulfilled. ||1||Pause||<br>
  He is protected by the Creator Lord; what harm can anyone do to him?<br>
  Even an ant can conquer the whole world.<br>
  His glory is endless; how can I describe it?<br>
  I am a sacrifice, a devoted sacrifice, to His feet. ||2||<br>
  He alone performs worship, austerities and meditation;<br>
  he alone is a giver to various charities;<br>
  he alone is approved in this Dark Age of Kali Yuga,<br>
  whom the Lord Master blesses with honor. ||3||<br>
  Joining the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy, I am enlightened.<br>
  I have found celestial peace, and my hopes are fulfilled.<br>
  The Perfect True Guru has blessed me with faith.<br>
  Nanak is the slave of His slaves. ||4||7||18||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Don't blame others, O people;<br>
  as you plant, so shall you harvest.<br>
  By your actions, you have bound yourself.<br>
  You come and go, entangled in Maya. ||1||<br>
  Such is the understanding of the Saintly people.<br>
  You shall be enlightened, through the Word of the Perfect Guru. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Body, wealth, spouse and ostentatious displays are false.<br>
  Horses and elephants will pass away.<br>
  Power, pleasures and beauty are all false.<br>
  Without the Naam, the Name of the Lord, everything is reduced to dust. ||2||<br>
  The egotistical people are deluded by useless doubt.<br>
  Of all this expanse, nothing shall go along with you.<br>
  Through pleasure and pain, the body is growing old.<br>
  Doing these things, the faithless cynics are passing their lives. ||3||<br>
  The Name of the Lord is Ambrosial Nectar in this Dark Age of Kali Yuga.<br>
  This treasure is obtained from the Holy.<br>
  O Nanak, whoever pleases the Guru,<br>
  the Lord of the Universe, beholds the Lord in each and every heart. ||4||8||19||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The Panch Shabad, the five primal sounds, echo the perfect sound current of the Naad.<br>
  The wondrous, amazing unstruck melody vibrates.<br>
  The Saintly people play there with the Lord.<br>
  They remain totally detached, absorbed in the Supreme Lord God. ||1||<br>
  It is the realm of celestial peace and bliss.<br>
  The Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy, sits and sings the Glorious Praises of the Lord. There is no disease or sorrow there, no birth or death. ||1||Pause||<br>
  There, they meditate only on the Naam, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  How rare are those who find this place of rest.<br>
  The love of God is their food, and the Kirtan of the Lord's Praise is their support.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 014</h2></center>
  They obtain a permanent seat in the infinite. ||2||<br>
  No one falls there, or wavers, or goes anywhere.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, some find this mansion.<br>
  They are not touched by doubt, fear, attachment or the traps of Maya.<br>
  They enter the deepest state of Samaadhi, through the kind mercy of God. ||3||<br>
  He has no end or limitation.<br>
  He Himself is unmanifest, and He Himself is manifest.<br>
  One who enjoys the taste of the Lord, Har, Har, deep within himself,<br>
  O Nanak, his wondrous state cannot be described. ||4||9||20||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Meeting with the Sangat, the Congregation, the Supreme Lord God has come into my consciousness.<br>
  In the Sangat, my mind has found contentment.<br>
  I touch my forehead to the feet of the Saints.<br>
  Countless times, I humbly bow to the Saints. ||1||<br>
  This mind is a sacrifice to the Saints;<br>
  holding tight to their support, I have found peace, and in their mercy, they have protected me. ||1||Pause||<br>
  I wash the feet of the Saints, and drink in that water.<br>
  Gazing upon the Blessed Vision of the Saints' Darshan, I live.<br>
  My mind rests its hopes in the Saints.<br>
  The Saints are my immaculate wealth. ||2||<br>
  The Saints have covered my faults.<br>
  By the Grace of the Saints, I am no longer tormented.<br>
  The Merciful Lord has blessed me with the Saints' Congregation.<br>
  The Compassionate Saints have become my help and support. ||3||<br>
  My consciousness, intellect and wisdom have been enlightened.<br>
  The Lord is profound, unfathomable, infinite, the treasure of virtue.<br>
  He cherishes all beings and creatures.<br>
  Nanak is enraptured, seeing the Saints. ||4||10||21||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Your home, power and wealth will be of no use to you.<br>
  Your corrupt worldly entanglements will be of no use to you.<br>
  Know that all your dear friends are fake.<br>
  Only the Name of the Lord, Har, Har, will go along with you. ||1||<br>
  Sing the Glorious Praises of the Lord's Name, O friend; remembering the Lord in meditation, your honor shall be saved.<br>
  Remembering the Lord in meditation, the Messenger of Death will not touch you. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Without the Lord, all pursuits are useless.<br>
  Gold, silver and wealth are just dust.<br>
  Chanting the Word of the Guru's Shabad, your mind shall be at peace.<br>
  Here and hereafter, your face shall be radiant and bright. ||2||<br>
  Even the greatest of the great worked and worked until they were exhausted.<br>
  None of them ever accomplished the tasks of Maya.<br>
  Any humble being who chants the Name of the Lord, Har, Har,<br>
  will have all his hopes fulfilled. ||3||<br>
  The Naam, the Name of the Lord, is the anchor and support of the Lord's devotees.<br>
  The Saints are victorious in this priceless human life.<br>
  Whatever the Lord's Saint does, is approved and accepted.<br>
  Slave Nanak is a sacrifice to him. ||4||11||22||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  You gather wealth by exploiting people.<br>
  It is of no use to you; it was meant for others.<br>
  You practice egotism, and act like a blind man.<br>
  In the world hereafter, you shall be tied to the leash of the Messenger of Death. ||1||<br>
  Give up your envy of others, you fool!<br>
  You only live here for a night, you fool!<br>
  You are intoxicated with Maya, but you must soon arise and depart.<br>
  You are totally involved in the dream. ||1||Pause||<br>
  In his childhood, the child is blind.<br>
  In the fullness of youth, he is involved in foul-smelling sins.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 015</h2></center>
  In the third stage of life, he gathers the wealth of Maya.<br>
  And when he grows old, he must leave all this; he departs regretting and repenting. ||2||<br>
  After a very long time, one obtains this precious human body, so difficult to obtain.<br>
  Without the Naam, the Name of the Lord, it is reduced to dust.<br>
  Worse than a beast, a demon or an idiot,<br>
  is that one who does not understand who created him. ||3||<br>
  Listen, O Creator Lord, Lord of the Universe, Lord of the World,<br>
  Merciful to the meek, forever compassionate<br>
  - If You emancipate the human, then his bonds are broken.<br>
  O Nanak, the people of world are blind; please, Lord, forgive them, and unite them with Yourself. ||4||12||23||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Joining the elements together, the robe of the body is fashioned.<br>
  The ignorant fool is engrossed in it.<br>
  He cherishes it, and constantly takes care of it.<br>
  But at the very last moment, he must arise and depart. ||1||<br>
  Without the Naam, the Name of the Lord, everything is false, O mortal.<br>
  Those who do not vibrate and meditate on the Lord of the Universe, but instead are imbued with other things, - all those mortals are plundered by Maya. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Bathing at sacred shrines of pilgrimage, filth is not washed off.<br>
  Religious rituals are all just egotistical displays.<br>
  By pleasing and appeasing people, no one is saved.<br>
  Without the Naam, they shall depart weeping. ||2||<br>
  Without the Lord's Name, the screen is not torn away.<br>
  I have studied all the Shaastras and Simritees.<br>
  He alone chants the Naam, whom the Lord Himself inspires to chant.<br>
  He obtains all fruits and rewards, and merges in peace. ||3||<br>
  O Savior Lord, please save me!<br>
  All peace and comforts are in Your Hand, God.<br>
  Whatever you attach me to, to that I am attached, O my Lord and Master.<br>
  O Nanak, the Lord is the Inner-knower, the Searcher of hearts. ||4||13||24||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Whatever He does makes me happy.<br>
  The ignorant mind is encouraged, in the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy.<br>
  Now, it does not waver at all; it has become stable and steady.<br>
  Receiving Truth, it is merged in the True Lord. ||1||<br>
  Pain is gone, and all illness is gone.<br>
  I have accepted the Will of God in my mind, associating with the Great Person, the Guru. ||1||Pause||<br>
  All is pure; all is immaculate.<br>
  Whatever exists is good.<br>
  Wherever He keeps me, that is the place of liberation for me.<br>
  Whatever He makes me chant, is His Name. ||2||<br>
  That is the sixty-eight sacred shrines of pilgrimage, where the Holy place their feet,<br>
  and that is heaven, where the Naam is chanted.<br>
  All bliss comes, when one obtains the Blessed Vision of the Lord's Darshan.<br>
  I sing continuously, continually, the Glorious Praises of the Lord. ||3||<br>
  The Lord Himself is pervading in each and every heart.<br>
  The glory of the Merciful Lord is radiant and manifest.<br>
  The shutters are opened, and doubts have run away.<br>
  Nanak has met with the Perfect Guru. ||4||14||25||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Millions of meditations and austerities rest in him,<br>
  along with wealth, wisdom, miraculous spiritual powers and angelic spiritual insight.<br>
  He enjoys the various shows and forms, pleasures and delicacies;<br>
  the Naam, the Name of the Lord, dwells within the heart of the Gurmukh. ||1||<br>
  Such is the glorious greatness of the Name of the Lord.<br>
  Its value cannot be described. ||1||Pause||<br>
  He alone is brave, patient and perfectly wise;<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 016</h2></center>
  he is intuitively in Samaadhi, profound and unfathomable.<br>
  He is liberated forever and all his affairs are perfectly resolved;<br>
  the Lord's Name abides within his heart. ||2||<br>
  He is totally peaceful, blissful and healthy;<br>
  he looks upon all impartially, and is perfectly detached.<br>
  He does not come and go, and he never wavers;<br>
  the Naam abides in his mind. ||3||<br>
  God is Merciful to the meek; He is the Lord of the World, the Lord of the Universe.<br>
  The Gurmukh meditates on Him, and his worries are gone.<br>
  The Guru has blessed Nanak with the Naam;<br>
  he serves the Saints, and works for the Saints. ||4||15||26||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Sing the Kirtan of the Lord's Praises, and the Beej Mantra, the Seed Mantra.<br>
  Even the homeless find a home in the world hereafter.<br>
  Fall at the feet of the Perfect Guru;<br>
  you have slept for so many incarnations - wake up! ||1||<br>
  Chant the Chant of the Lord's Name, Har, Har.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, it shall be enshrined within your heart, and you shall cross over the terrifying world-ocean. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Meditate on the eternal treasure of the Naam, the Name of the Lord, O mind,<br>
  and then, the screen of Maya shall be torn away.<br>
  Drink in the Ambrosial Nectar of the Guru's Shabad,<br>
  and then your soul shall be rendered immaculate and pure. ||2||<br>
  Searching, searching, searching, I have realized<br>
  that without devotional worship of the Lord, no one is saved.<br>
  So vibrate, and meditate on that Lord in the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy;<br>
  your mind and body shall be imbued with love for the Lord. ||3||<br>
  Renounce all your cleverness and trickery.<br>
  O mind, without the Lord's Name, there is no place of rest.<br>
  The Lord of the Universe, the Lord of the World, has taken pity on me.<br>
  Nanak seeks the protection and support of the Lord, Har, Har. ||4||16||27||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  In the Saints' Congregation, play joyfully with the Lord,<br>
  and you will not have to meet the Messenger of Death hereafter.<br>
  Your egotistical intellect shall be dispelled,<br>
  and your evil-mindedness will be totally taken away. ||1||<br>
  Sing the Glorious Praises of the Lord's Name, O Pandit.<br>
  Religious rituals and egotism are of no use at all. You shall go home with happiness, O Pandit. ||1||Pause||<br>
  I have earned the profit, the wealth of the Lord's praise.<br>
  All my hopes have been fulfilled.<br>
  Pain has left me, and peace has come to my home.<br>
  By the Grace of the Saints, my heart-lotus blossoms forth. ||2||<br>
  One who is blessed with the gift of the jewel of the Name,<br>
  obtains all treasures.<br>
  His mind becomes content, finding the Perfect Lord.<br>
  Why should he ever go begging again? ||3||<br>
  Hearing the Lord's sermon, he becomes pure and holy.<br>
  Chanting it with his tongue, he finds the way to salvation.<br>
  He alone is approved, who enshrines the Lord within his heart.<br>
  Nanak: such a humble being is exalted, O Siblings of Destiny. ||4||17||28||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  No matter how hard you try to grab it, it does not come into your hands.<br>
  No matter how much you may love it, it does not go along with you.<br>
  Says Nanak, when you abandon it,<br>
  then it comes and falls at your feet. ||1||<br>
  Listen, O Saints: this is the pure philosophy.<br>
  Without the Lord's Name, there is no salvation. Meeting with the Perfect Guru, one is saved. ||1||Pause||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 017</h2></center>
  When someone tries to appease her,<br>
  then she takes pride in herself.<br>
  But when someone puts her out of his thoughts,<br>
  then she serves him like a slave. ||2||<br>
  She seems to please, but in the end, she deceives.<br>
  She does not remain in any one place.<br>
  She has bewitched a great many worlds.<br>
  The Lord's humble servants cut her apart into pieces. ||3||<br>
  Whoever begs from her remains hungry.<br>
  Whoever is infatuated with her obtains nothing.<br>
  But one who renounces her, and joins the Society of the Saints,<br>
  by great good fortune, O Nanak, is saved. ||4||18||29||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  See the Lord, the Universal Soul, in all.<br>
  The One God is perfect, and all-pervading.<br>
  Know that the priceless jewel is within your own heart.<br>
  Realize that your essence is within your own self. ||1||<br>
  Drink in the Ambrosial Nectar, by the Grace of the Saints.<br>
  One who is blessed with high destiny, obtains it. Without a tongue, how can one know the taste? ||1||Pause||<br>
  How can a deaf person listen to the eighteen Puraanas and the Vedas?<br>
  The blind man cannot see even a million lights.<br>
  The beast loves grass, and remains attached to it.<br>
  One who has not been taught - how can he understand? ||2||<br>
  God, the Knower, knows all.<br>
  He is with His devotees, through and through.<br>
  Those who sing God's Praises with joy and delight,<br>
  O Nanak - the Messenger of Death does not even approach them. ||3||19||30||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Blessing me with His Name, He has purified and sanctified me.<br>
  The Lord's wealth is my capital. False hope has left me; this is my wealth.<br>
  Breaking my bonds, the Lord has linked me to His service.<br>
  I am a devotee of the Lord, Har, Har; I sing the Glorious Praises of the Lord. ||1||<br>
  The unstruck sound current vibrates and resounds.<br>
  The Lord's humble servants sing His Glorious Praises with love and delight; they are honored by the Divine Guru. ||1||Pause||<br>
  My pre-ordained destiny has been activated;<br>
  I have awakened from the sleep of countless incarnations.<br>
  In the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy, my aversion is gone.<br>
  My mind and body are imbued with love for the Lord. ||2||<br>
  The Merciful Savior Lord has saved me.<br>
  I have no service or work to my credit.<br>
  In His Mercy, God has taken pity on me;<br>
  He lifted me up and pulled me out, when I was suffering in pain. ||3||<br>
  Listening, listening to His Praises, joy has welled up within my mind.<br>
  Twenty-four hours a day, I sing the Glorious Praises of the Lord.<br>
  Singing, singing His Praises, I have obtained the supreme status.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, Nanak is lovingly focused on the Lord. ||4||20||31||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  In exchange for a shell, he gives up a jewel.<br>
  He tries to get what he must give up.<br>
  He collects those things which are worthless.<br>
  Enticed by Maya, he takes the crooked path. ||1||<br>
  You unfortunate man - have you no shame?<br>
  You do not remember in your mind the ocean of peace, the perfect Transcendent Lord God. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Nectar seems bitter to you, and poison is sweet.<br>
  Such is your condition, you faithless cynic, which I have seen with my own eyes.<br>
  You are fond of falsehood, fraud and egotism.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 018</h2></center>
  If you hear the Naam, the Name of the Lord, you feel like you have been stung by a scorpion. ||2||<br>
  You continually yearn for Maya,<br>
  and you never chant the Lord's Praises with your mouth.<br>
  The Lord is fearless and formless; He is the Great Giver.<br>
  But you do not love Him, you fool! ||3||<br>
  God, the True King, is above the heads of all kings.<br>
  He is the independent, perfect Lord King.<br>
  People are intoxicated by emotional attachment, entangled in doubt and family life.<br>
  Nanak: they are saved only by Your Mercy, Lord. ||4||21||32||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Night and day, I chant the Lord's Name.<br>
  Hereafter, I shall obtain a seat in the Court of the Lord.<br>
  I am in bliss forever; I have no sorrow.<br>
  The disease of ego never afflicts me. ||1||<br>
  O Saints of the Lord, seek out those who know God.<br>
  You shall be wonderstruck with wonder at the wonderful Lord; meditate in remembrance on the Lord, O mortal, and obtain the supreme status. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Calculating, measuring, and thinking in every way,<br>
  see that without the Naam, no one can be carried across.<br>
  Of all your efforts, none will go along with you.<br>
  You can cross over the terrifying world-ocean only through the love of God. ||2||<br>
  By merely washing the body, one's filth is not removed.<br>
  Afflicted by egotism, duality only increases.<br>
  That humble being who takes the medicine of the Name of the Lord, Har, Har<br>
  - all his diseases are eradicated. ||3||<br>
  Take pity on me, O merciful, Supreme Lord God;<br>
  let me never forget the Lord of the World from my mind.<br>
  Let me be the dust of the feet of Your slaves;<br>
  O God, please fulfill Nanak's hope. ||4||22||33||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  You are my Protection, O perfect Divine Guru.<br>
  There is no other than You.<br>
  You are all-powerful, O perfect Supreme Lord God.<br>
  He alone meditates on You, whose karma is perfect. ||1||<br>
  You Name, God, is the boat to carry us across.<br>
  My mind has grasped Your protection alone. Other than You, I have no place of rest at all. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Chanting, meditating on Your Name, I live,<br>
  and hereafter, I will obtain a seat in the Court of the Lord.<br>
  Pain and darkness are gone from my mind;<br>
  my evil-mindedness is dispelled, and I am absorbed in the Lord's Name. ||2||<br>
  I have enshrined love for the Lord's lotus feet.<br>
  The lifestyle of the Perfect Guru is immaculate and pure.<br>
  My fear has run away, and the fearless Lord dwells within my mind.<br>
  My tongue continually chants the Ambrosial Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||3||<br>
  The nooses of millions of incarnations are cut away.<br>
  I have obtained the profit of the true wealth.<br>
  This treasure is inexhaustible; it will never run out.<br>
  O Nanak, the devotees look beautiful in the Court of the Lord. ||4||23||34||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The Naam, the Name of the Lord, is a jewel, a ruby.<br>
  It brings Truth, contentment and spiritual wisdom.<br>
  The Lord entrusts the treasures of peace, intuition and kindness to His devotees. ||1||<br>
  This is the treasure of my Lord.<br>
  Consuming and expending it, it is never used up. The Lord has no end or limitation. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The Kirtan of the Lord's Praise is a priceless diamond.<br>
  It is the ocean of bliss and virtue.<br>
  In the Word of the Guru's Bani is the wealth of the unstruck sound current.<br>
  The Saints hold the key to it in their hands. ||2||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 019</h2></center>
  They sit there, in the cave of deep Samaadhi;<br>
  the unique, perfect Lord God dwells there.<br>
  God holds conversations with His devotees.<br>
  There is no pleasure or pain, no birth or death there. ||3||<br>
  One whom the Lord Himself blesses with His Mercy,<br>
  obtains the Lord's wealth in the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy.<br>
  Nanak prays to the merciful Primal Lord;<br>

  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The Vedas do not know His greatness.<br>
  Brahma does not know His mystery.<br>
  Incarnated beings do not know His limit.<br>
  The Transcendent Lord, the Supreme Lord God, is infinite. ||1||<br>
  Only He Himself knows His own state.<br>
  Others speak of Him only by hearsay. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Shiva does not know His mystery.<br>
  The gods gave grown weary of searching for Him.<br>
  The goddesses do not know His mystery.<br>
  Above all is the unseen, Supreme Lord God. ||2||<br>
  The Creator Lord plays His own plays.<br>
  He Himself separates, and He Himself unites.<br>
  Some wander around, while others are linked to His devotional worship.<br>
  By His actions, He makes Himself known. ||3||<br>
  Listen to the true story of the Saints.<br>
  They speak only of what they see with their eyes.<br>
  He is not involved with virtue or vice.<br>
  Nanak's God is Himself all-in-all. ||4||25||36||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  I have not tried to do anything through knowledge.<br>
  I have no knowledge, intelligence or spiritual wisdom.<br>
  I have not practiced chanting, deep meditation, humility or righteousness.<br>
  I know nothing of such good karma. ||1||<br>
  O my Beloved God, my Lord and Master,<br>
  there is none other than You. Even though I wander and make mistakes, I am still Yours, God. ||1||Pause||<br>
  I have no wealth, no intelligence, no miraculous spiritual powers; I am not enlightened.<br>
  I dwell in the village of corruption and sickness.<br>
  O my One Creator Lord God,<br>
  Your Name is the support of my mind. ||2||<br>
  Hearing, hearing Your Name, I live; this is my mind's consolation.<br>
  Your Name, God, is the Destroyer of sins.<br>
  You, O Limitless Lord, are the Giver of the soul.<br>
  He alone knows You, unto whom You reveal Yourself. ||3||<br>
  Whoever has been created, rests his hopes in You.<br>
  All worship and adore You, God, O treasure of excellence.<br>
  Slave Nanak is a sacrifice to You.<br>
  My merciful Lord and Master is infinite. ||4||26||37||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The Savior Lord is merciful.<br>
  Millions of incarnations are eradicated in an instant, contemplating the Lord.<br>
  All beings worship and adore Him.<br>
  Receiving the Guru's Mantra, one meets God. ||1||<br>
  My God is the Giver of souls.<br>
  The Perfect Transcendent Lord Master, my God, imbues each and every heart. ||1||Pause||<br>
  My mind has grasped His Support.<br>
  My bonds have been shattered.<br>
  Within my heart, I meditate on the Lord, the embodiment of supreme bliss.<br>
  My mind is filled with ecstasy. ||2||<br>
  The Lord's Sanctuary is the boat to carry us across.<br>
  The Lord's Feet are the embodiment of life itself.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 020</h2></center>
  They are the Support of the breath of life of the Saints.<br>
  God is infinite, the highest of the high. ||3||<br>
  That mind is excellent and sublime, which meditates in remembrance on the Lord.<br>
  In His Mercy, the Lord Himself bestows it.<br>
  Peace, intuitive poise and bliss are found in the Lord's Name.<br>
  Meeting with the Guru, Nanak chants the Name. ||4||27||38||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Abandon all your clever tricks.<br>
  Become His servant, and serve Him.<br>
  Totally erase your self-conceit.<br>

  Be awake and aware with your Guru.<br>
  Your hopes and desires shall be fulfilled, and you shall obtain all treasures from the Guru. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Let no one think that God and Guru are separate.<br>
  The True Guru is the Immaculate Lord.<br>

  Hold tight to the Support of the Guru, the Lord.<br>
  Give up all other hopes.<br>

  Meditate on the Lord, O Saints, and be in bliss.<br>
  Renounce your cleverness and all your tricks. Chant the Immaculate Chant of the Guru's Mantra. ||1||Pause||<br>

  Bow down to the Guru's Feet,<br>

  The Lord God is the Great Giver.<br>
  He has no end or limitation.<br>

  He will be your Saving Grace in the end. ||3||<br>
  Nanak has obtained this treasure,<br>

  Whoever chants it, is emancipated.<br>
  It is obtained only by His Grace. ||4||29||40||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Make this invaluable human life fruitful.<br>
  You shall not be destroyed when you go to the Lord's Court.<br>
  In this world and the next, you shall obtain honor and glory.<br>
  At the very last moment, He will save you. ||1||<br>
  Sing the Glorious Praises of the Lord.<br>
  In both this world and the next, you shall be embellished with beauty, meditating on the wondrous Primal Lord God. ||1||Pause||<br>
  While standing up and sitting down, meditate on the Lord,<br>
  and all your troubles shall depart.<br>
  All your enemies will become friends.<br>
  Your consciousness shall be immaculate and pure. ||2||<br>
  This is the most exalted deed.<br>
  Of all faiths, this is the most sublime and excellent faith.<br>
  Meditating in remembrance on the Lord, you shall be saved.<br>
  You shall be rid of the burden of countless incarnations. ||3||<br>
  Your hopes shall be fulfilled,<br>
  and the noose of the Messenger of Death will be cut away.<br>
  So listen to the Guru's Teachings.<br>
  O Nanak, you shall be absorbed in celestial peace. ||4||30||41||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 021</h2></center>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Honor the One, to whom everything belongs.<br>
  Leave your egotistical pride behind.<br>
  You belong to Him; everyone belongs to Him.<br>
  Worship and adore Him, and you shall be at peace forever. ||1||<br>
  Why do you wander in doubt, you fool?<br>
  Without the Naam, the Name of the Lord, nothing is of any use at all. Crying out, 'Mine, mine', a great many have departed, regretfully repenting. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Whatever the Lord has done, accept that as good.<br>
  Without accepting, you shall mingle with dust.<br>
  His Will seems sweet to me.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, He comes to dwell in the mind. ||2||<br>
  He Himself is carefree and independent, imperceptible.<br>
  Twenty-four hours a day, O mind, meditate on Him.<br>
  When He comes into the consciousness, pain is dispelled.<br>
  Here and hereafter, your face shall be radiant and bright. ||3||<br>
  Who, and how many have been saved, singing the Glorious Praises of the Lord?<br>
  They cannot be counted or evaluated.<br>
  Even the sinking iron is saved, in the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy,<br>
  O Nanak, as His Grace is received. ||4||31||42||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  In your mind, meditate on the Lord God.<br>
  This is the Teaching given by the Perfect Guru.<br>
  All fears and terrors are taken away,<br>
  and your hopes shall be fulfilled. ||1||<br>
  Service to the Divine Guru is fruitful and rewarding.<br>
  His value cannot be described; the True Lord is unseen and mysterious. ||1||Pause||<br>
  He Himself is the Doer, the Cause of causes.<br>
  Meditate on Him forever, O my mind, and continually serve Him.<br>
  You shall be blessed with truth, intuition and peace, O my friend. ||2||<br>
  My Lord and Master is so very great.<br>
  In an instant, He establishes and disestablishes.<br>
  There is no other than Him.<br>
  He is the Saving Grace of His humble servant. ||3||<br>
  Please take pity on me, and hear my prayer,<br>
  that Your servant may behold the Blessed Vision of Your Darshan.<br>
  Nanak chants the Chant of the Lord,<br>
  whose glory and radiance are the highest of all. ||4||32||43||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Reliance on mortal man is useless.<br>
  O God, my Lord and Master, You are my only Support.<br>
  I have discarded all other hopes.<br>
  I have met with my carefree Lord and Master, the treasure of virtue. ||1||<br>
  Meditate on the Name of the Lord alone, O my mind.<br>
  Your affairs shall be perfectly resolved; sing the Glorious Praises of the Lord, Har, Har, Har, O my mind. ||1||Pause||<br>
  You are the Doer, the Cause of causes.<br>
  Your lotus feet, Lord, are my Sanctuary.<br>
  I meditate on the Lord in my mind and body.<br>
  The blissful Lord has revealed His form to me. ||2||<br>
  I seek His eternal support;<br>
  He is the Creator of all beings.<br>
  Remembering the Lord in meditation, the treasure is obtained.<br>
  At the very last instant, He shall be your Savior. ||3||<br>
  Be the dust of all men's feet.<br>
  Eradicate self-conceit, and merge in the Lord.<br>
  Night and day, meditate on the Naam, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  O Nanak, this is the most rewarding activity. ||4||33||44||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  He is the Doer, the Cause of causes, the bountiful Lord.<br>
  The merciful Lord cherishes all.<br>
  The Lord is unseen and infinite.<br>
  God is great and endless. ||1||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 022</h2></center>
  I humbly pray to invoke the Universal Lord God, the Lord of the World.<br>
  The Creator Lord is all-pervading, everywhere. ||1||Pause||<br>
  He is the Lord of the Universe, the Life of the World.<br>
  Within your heart, worship and adore the Destroyer of fear.<br>
  The Master Rishi of the senses, Lord of the World, Lord of the Universe.<br>
  He is perfect, ever-present everywhere, the Liberator. ||2||<br>
  You are the One and only merciful Master,<br>
  spiritual teacher, prophet, religious teacher.<br>
  Master of hearts, Dispenser of justice,<br>
  more sacred than the Koran and the Bible. ||3||<br>
  The Lord is powerful and merciful.<br>
  The all-pervading Lord is the support of each and every heart.<br>
  The luminous Lord dwells everywhere.<br>
  His play cannot be known. ||4||<br>
  Be kind and compassionate to me, O Creator Lord.<br>
  Bless me with devotion and meditation, O Lord Creator.<br>
  Says Nanak, the Guru has rid me of doubt.<br>
  The Muslim God Allah and the Hindu God Paarbrahm are one and the same. ||5||34||45||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The sins of millions of incarnations are eradicated.<br>
