  When the Lord's lotus feet are enshrined in the mind,<br>
  all terrible evils are taken away from the body. ||1||<br>
  Sing the Praise of the Lord of the World, O mortal being.<br>
  The Unspoken Speech of the True Lord God is perfect. Dwelling upon it, one's light merges into the Light. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Hunger and thirst are totally quenched;<br>
  by the Grace of the Saints, meditate on the immortal Lord.<br>
  Night and day, serve God.<br>
  This is the sign that one has met with the Lord. ||2||<br>
  Worldly entanglements are ended, when God becomes merciful.<br>
  Gazing upon the Blessed Vision of the Guru's Darshan, I am enraptured.<br>
  My perfect pre-destined karma has been activated.<br>
  With my tongue, I continually sing the Glorious Praises of the Lord. ||3||<br>
  The Saints of the Lord are accepted and approved forever.<br>
  The foreheads of the Saintly people are marked with the Lord's insignia.<br>
  One who is blessed with the dust of the feet of the Lord's slave,<br>
  O Nanak, obtains the supreme status. ||4||35||46||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Let yourself be a sacrifice to the Blessed Vision of the Lord's Darshan.<br>
  Focus your heart's meditation on the Lord's lotus feet.<br>
  Apply the dust of the feet of the Saints to your forehead,<br>
  and the filthy evil-mindedness of countless incarnations will be washed off. ||1||<br>
  Meeting Him, egotistical pride is eradicated,<br>
  and you will come to see the Supreme Lord God in all. The Perfect Lord God has showered His Mercy. ||1||Pause||<br>
  This is the Guru's Praise, to chant the Name of the Lord.<br>
  This is devotion to the Guru, to sing forever the Glorious Praises of the Lord.<br>
  This is contemplation upon the Guru, to know that the Lord is close at hand.<br>
  Accept the Word of the Guru's Shabad as Truth. ||2||<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Teachings, look upon pleasure and pain as one and the same.<br>
  Hunger and thirst shall never afflict you.<br>
  The mind becomes content and satisfied through the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  Meditate on the Lord of the Universe, and He will cover all your faults. ||3||<br>
  The Guru is the Supreme Lord God; the Guru is the Lord of the Universe.<br>
  The Guru is the Great Giver, merciful and forgiving.<br>
  One whose mind is attached to the Guru's feet,<br>
  O slave Nanak, is blessed with perfect destiny. ||4||36||47||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 023</h2></center>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  What supports you in this world?<br>
  You ignorant fool, who is your companion?<br>
  The Lord is your only companion; no one knows His condition.<br>
  You look upon the five thieves as your friends. ||1||<br>
  Serve that home, which will save you, my friend.<br>
  Chant the Glorious Praises of the Lord of the Universe, day and night; in the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy, love Him in your mind. ||1||Pause||<br>
  This human life is passing away in egotism and conflict.<br>
  You are not satisfied; such is the flavor of sin.<br>
  Wandering and roaming around, you suffer terrible pain.<br>
  You cannot cross over the impassable sea of Maya. ||2||<br>
  You do the deeds which do not help you at all.<br>
  As you plant, so shall you harvest.<br>
  There is none other than the Lord to save you.<br>
  You will be saved, only if God grants His Grace. ||3||<br>
  Your Name, God, is the Purifier of sinners.<br>
  Please bless Your slave with that gift.<br>
  Please grant Your Grace, God, and emancipate me.<br>
  Nanak has grasped Your Sanctuary, God. ||4||37||48||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  I have found peace in this world.<br>
  I will not have to appear before the Righteous Judge of Dharma to give my account.<br>
  I will be respected in the Court of the Lord,<br>
  and I will not have to enter the womb of reincarnation ever again. ||1||<br>
  Now, I know the value of friendship with the Saints.<br>
  In His Mercy, the Lord has blessed me with His Name. My pre-ordained destiny has been fulfilled. ||1||Pause||<br>
  My consciousness is attached to the Guru's feet.<br>
  Blessed, blessed is this fortunate time of union.<br>
  I have applied the dust of the Saints' feet to my forehead,<br>
  and all my sins and pains have been eradicated. ||2||<br>
  Performing true service to the Holy,<br>
  the mortal's mind is purified.<br>
  I have seen the fruitful vision of the Lord's humble slave.<br>
  God's Name dwells within each and every heart. ||3||<br>
  All my troubles and sufferings have been taken away;<br>
  I have merged into the One, from whom I originated.<br>
  The Lord of the Universe, incomparably beautiful, has become merciful.<br>
  O Nanak, God is perfect and forgiving. ||4||38||49||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The tiger leads the cow to the pasture,<br>
  the shell is worth thousands of dollars,<br>
  and the elephant nurses the goat,<br>
  when God bestows His Glance of Grace. ||1||<br>
  You are the treasure of mercy, O my Beloved Lord God.<br>
  I cannot even describe Your many Glorious Virtues. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The cat sees the meat, but does not eat it,<br>
  and the great butcher throws away his knife;<br>
  the Creator Lord God abides in the heart;<br>
  the net holding the fish breaks apart. ||2||<br>
  The dry wood blossoms forth in greenery and red flowers;<br>
  in the high desert, the beautiful lotus flower blooms.<br>
  The Divine True Guru puts out the fire.<br>
  He links His servant to His service. ||3||<br>
  He saves even the ungrateful;<br>
  my God is forever merciful.<br>
  He is forever the helper and support of the humble Saints.<br>
  Nanak has found the Sanctuary of His lotus feet. ||4||39||50||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 024</h2></center>
  God killed the five tigers.<br>
  He has driven out the ten wolves.<br>
  The three whirl-pools have stopped spinning.<br>
  In the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy, the fear of reincarnation is gone. ||1||<br>
  Meditating, meditating in remembrance on the Lord of the Universe, I live.<br>
  In His Mercy, He protects His slave; the True Lord is forever and ever the forgiver. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The mountain of sin is burnt down, like straw,<br>
  by chanting and meditating on the Name, and worshipping God's feet.<br>
  God, the embodiment of bliss, becomes manifest everywhere.<br>
  Linked to His loving devotional worship, I enjoy peace. ||2||<br>
  I have crossed over the world-ocean, as if it were no bigger than a calf's footprint on the ground.<br>
  I shall never again have to endure suffering or grief.<br>
  The ocean is contained in the pitcher.<br>
  This is not such an amazing thing for the Creator to do. ||3||<br>
  When I am separated from Him, then I am consigned to the nether regions.<br>
  When He lifts me up and pulls me out, then I am enraptured by His Glance of Grace.<br>
  Vice and virtue are not under my control.<br>
  With love and affection, Nanak sings His Glorious Praises. ||4||40||51||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Neither your body nor your mind belong to you.<br>
  Attached to Maya, you are entangled in fraud.<br>
  You play like a baby lamb.<br>
  But suddenly, Death will catch you in its noose. ||1||<br>
  Seek the Sanctuary of the Lord's lotus feet, O my mind.<br>
  Chant the Name of the Lord, which will be your help and support. As Gurmukh, you shall obtain the true wealth. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Your unfinished worldly affairs will never be resolved.<br>
  You shall always regret your sexual desire, anger and pride.<br>
  You act in corruption in order to survive,<br>
  but not even an iota will go along with you, you ignorant fool! ||2||<br>
  You practice deception, and you know many tricks;<br>
  for the sake of mere shells, you throw dust upon your head.<br>
  You never even think of the One who gave you life.<br>
  The pain of false greed never leaves you. ||3||<br>
  When the Supreme Lord God becomes merciful,<br>
  this mind becomes the dust of the feet of the Holy.<br>
  With His lotus hands, He has attached us to the hem of His robe.<br>
  Nanak merges in the Truest of the True. ||4||41||52||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  I seek the Sanctuary of the Sovereign Lord.<br>
  I have become fearless, singing the Glorious Praises of the Lord of the Universe. In the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy, my pains have been taken away. ||1||Pause||<br>
  That person, within whose mind the Lord abides,<br>
  does not see the impassible world-ocean.<br>
  All one's affairs are resolved,<br>
  by chanting continually the Name of the Lord, Har, Har. ||1||<br>
  Why should His slave feel any anxiety? The Guru places His hand upon my forehead.<br>
  The fear of birth and death is dispelled;<br>
  I am a sacrifice to the Perfect Guru. ||2||<br>
  I am enraptured, meeting with the Guru, the Transcendent Lord.<br>
  He alone obtains the Blessed Vision of the Lord's Darshan, who is blessed by His Mercy.<br>
  One who is blessed by the Grace of the Supreme Lord God,<br>
  crosses over the terrifying world-ocean in the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy. ||3||<br>
  Drink in the Ambrosial Nectar, O Beloved Holy people.<br>
  Your face shall be radiant and bright in the Court of the Lord.<br>
  Celebrate and be blissful, and abandon all corruption.<br>
  O Nanak, meditate on the Lord and cross over. ||4||42||53||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 025</h2></center>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The fire runs away from the fuel.<br>
  The water runs away from the dust in all directions.<br>
  The feet are above, and the sky is beneath.<br>
  The ocean appears in the cup. ||1||<br>
  Such is our all-powerful dear Lord.<br>
  His devotees do not forget Him, even for an instant. Twenty-four hours a day, O mind, meditate on Him. ||1||Pause||<br>
  First comes the butter, and then the milk.<br>
  The dirt cleans the soap.<br>
  The fearless are afraid of fear.<br>
  The living are killed by the dead. ||2||<br>
  The visible body is hidden, and the etheric body is seen.<br>
  The Lord of the world does all these things.<br>
  The one who is cheated, is not cheated by the cheat.<br>
  With no merchandise, the trader trades again and again. ||3||<br>
  So join the Society of the Saints, and chant the Lord's Name.<br>
  So say the Simritees, Shaastras, Vedas and Puraanas.<br>
  Rare are those who contemplate and meditate on God.<br>
  O Nanak, they attain the supreme status. ||4||43||54||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Whatever pleases Him happens.<br>
  Forever and ever, I seek the Sanctuary of the Lord.There is none other than God. ||1||Pause||<br>
  You look upon your children, spouse and wealth; none of these will go along with you.<br>
  Eating the poisonous potion, you have gone astray. You will have to go, and leave Maya and your mansions. ||1||<br>
  Slandering others, you are totally ruined; because of your past actions, you shall be consigned to the womb of reincarnation.<br>
  Your past actions will not just go away; the most horrible Messenger of Death shall seize you. ||2||<br>
  You tell lies, and do not practice what you preach. Your desires are not satisfied - what a shame.<br>
  You have contracted an incurable disease; slandering the Saints, your body is wasting away; you are utterly ruined. ||3||<br>
  He embellishes those whom He has fashioned. He Himself gave life to the Saints.<br>
  O Nanak, He hugs His slaves close in His Embrace. Please grant Your Grace, O Supreme Lord God, and be kind to me as well. ||4||44||55||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Such is the Perfect Divine Guru, my help and support.<br>
  Meditation on Him is not wasted. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Gazing upon the Blessed Vision of His Darshan, I am enraptured.<br>
  The dust of His feet snaps the noose of Death.<br>
  His lotus feet dwell within my mind,<br>
  and so all the affairs of my body are arranged and resolved. ||1||<br>
  One upon whom He places His Hand, is protected.<br>
  My God is the Master of the masterless.<br>
  He is the Savior of sinners, the treasure of mercy.<br>
  Forever and ever, I am a sacrifice to Him. ||2||<br>
  One whom He blesses with His Immaculate Mantra,<br>
  renounces corruption; his egotistical pride is dispelled.<br>
  Meditate on the One Lord in the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy.<br>
  Sins are erased, through the love of the Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||3||<br>
  The Guru, the Transcendent Lord, dwells among all.<br>
  The treasure of virtue pervades and permeates each and every heart.<br>
  Please grant me the Blessed Vision of Your Darshan;<br>
  O God, I place my hopes in You. Nanak continually offers this true prayer. ||4||45||56||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 026</h2></center>
  Raag Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl, Second House, Du-Padas:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Sing the songs of Praise of the Lord.<br>
  Chanting the Naam, the Name of the Lord, total peace is obtained; coming and going is ended, my friend. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Singing the Glorious Praises of the Lord, one is enlightened,<br>
  and comes to dwell in His lotus feet. ||1||<br>
  In the Society of the Saints, one is saved.<br>
  O Nanak, he crosses over the terrifying world-ocean. ||2||1||57||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  My Guru is perfect, my Guru is perfect.<br>
  Chanting the Lord's Name, I am always at peace; all my illness and fraud is dispelled. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Worship and adore that One Lord alone.<br>
  In His Sanctuary, eternal peace is obtained. ||1||<br>
  One who feels hunger for the Naam sleeps in peace.<br>
  Meditating in remembrance on the Lord, all pains are dispelled. ||2||<br>
  Enjoy celestial bliss, O my Siblings of Destiny.<br>
  The Perfect Guru has eradicated all anxiety. ||3||<br>
  Twenty-four hours a day, chant God's Chant.<br>
  O Nanak, He Himself shall save you. ||4||2||58||<br>
  Raag Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl, Partaal, Third House:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  I humbly bow to the Lord, the Supreme Being.<br>
  The One, the One and Only Creator Lord permeates the water, the land, the earth and the sky. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Over and over again, the Creator Lord destroys, sustains and creates.<br>
  He has no home; He needs no nourishment. ||1||<br>
  The Naam, the Name of the Lord, is deep and profound, strong, poised, lofty, exalted and infinite.<br>
  He stages His plays; His Virtues are priceless. Nanak is a sacrifice to Him. ||2||1||59||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  You must abandon your beauty, pleasures, fragrances and enjoyments; beguiled by gold and sexual desire, you must still leave Maya behind. ||1||Pause||<br>
  You gaze upon billions and trillions of treasures and riches, which delight and comfort your mind,<br>
  but these will not go along with you. ||1||<br>
  Entangled with children, spouse, siblings and friends, you are enticed and fooled; these pass like the shadow of a tree.<br>
  Nanak seeks the Sanctuary of His lotus feet; He has found peace in the faith of the Saints. ||2||2||60||<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Raag Raamkalee, Ninth Mehl, Ti-Padas:<br>
  O mind, take the sheltering support of the Lord's Name.<br>
  Remembering Him in meditation, evil-mindedness is dispelled, and the state of Nirvaanaa is obtained. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Know that one who sings the Glorious Praises of the Lord is very fortunate.<br>
  The sins of countless incarnations are washed off, and he attains the heavenly realm. ||1||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 027</h2></center>
  At the very last moment, Ajaamal became aware of the Lord;<br>
  that state which even the supreme Yogis desire - he attained that state in an instant. ||2||<br>
  The elephant had no virtue and no knowledge; what religious rituals has he performed?<br>
  O Nanak, behold the way of the Lord, who bestowed the gift of fearlessness. ||3||1||<br>
  Raamkalee, Ninth Mehl:<br>
  Holy people: what way should I now adopt,<br>
  by which all evil-mindedness may be dispelled, and the mind may vibrate in devotional worship to the Lord? ||1||Pause||<br>
  My mind is entangled in Maya; it knows nothing at all of spiritual wisdom.<br>
  What is that Name, by which the world, contemplating it, might attain the state of Nirvaanaa? ||1||<br>
  When the Saints became kind and compassionate, they told me this.<br>
  Understand, that whoever sings the Kirtan of God's Praises, has performed all religious rituals. ||2||<br>
  One who enshrines the Lord's Name in his heart night and day - even for an instant<br>
  - has his fear of Death eradicated. O Nanak, his life is approved and fulfilled. ||3||2||<br>
  Raamkalee, Ninth Mehl:<br>
  O mortal, focus your thoughts on the Lord.<br>
  Moment by moment, your life is running out; night and day, your body is passing away in vain. ||1||Pause||<br>
  You have wasted your youth in corrupt pleasures, and your childhood in ignorance.<br>
  You have grown old, and even now, you do not understand, the evil-mindedness in which you are entangled. ||1||<br>
  Why have you forgotten your Lord and Master, who blessed you with this human life?<br>
  Remembering Him in meditation, one is liberated. And yet, you do not sing His Praises, even for an instant. ||2||<br>
  Why are you intoxicated with Maya? It will not go along with you.<br>
  Says Nanak, think of Him, remember Him in your mind. He is the Fulfiller of desires, who will be your help and support in the end. ||3||3||81||<br>
  Raamkalee, First Mehl, Ashtapadees:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  The same moon rises, and the same stars; the same sun shines in the sky.<br>
  The earth is the same, and the same wind blows. The age in which we dwell affects living beings, but not these places. ||1||<br>
  Give up your attachment to life.<br>
  Those who act like tyrants are accepted and approved - recognize that this is the sign of the Dark Age of Kali Yuga. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Kali Yuga has not been heard to have come to any country, or to be sitting at any sacred shrine.<br>
  It is not where the generous person gives to charities, nor seated in the mansion he has built. ||2||<br>
  If someone practices Truth, he is frustrated; prosperity does not come to the home of the sincere.<br>
  If someone chants the Lord's Name, he is scorned. These are the signs of Kali Yuga. ||3||<br>
  Whoever is in charge, is humiliated. Why should the servant be afraid,<br>
  when the master is put in chains? He dies at the hands of his servant. ||4||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 028</h2></center>
  Chant the Praises of the Lord; Kali Yuga has come.<br>
  The justice of the previous three ages is gone. One obtains virtue, only if the Lord bestows it. ||1||Pause||<br>
  In this turbulent age of Kali Yuga, Muslim law decides the cases, and the blue-robed Qazi is the judge.<br>
  The Guru's Bani has taken the place of Brahma's Veda, and the singing of the Lord's Praises are good deeds. ||5||<br>
  Worship without faith; self-discipline without truthfulness; the ritual of the sacred thread without chastity - what good are these?<br>
  You may bathe and wash, and apply a ritualistic tilak mark to your forehead, but without inner purity, there is no understanding. ||6||<br>
  In Kali Yuga, the Koran and the Bible have become famous.<br>
  The Pandit's scriptures and the Puraanas are not respected.<br>
  O Nanak, the Lord's Name now is Rehmaan, the Merciful.<br>
  Know that there is only One Creator of the creation. ||7||<br>
  Nanak has obtained the glorious greatness of the Naam, the Name of the Lord. There is no action higher than this.<br>
  If someone goes out to beg for what is already in his own home, then he should be chastised. ||8||1||<br>
  Raamkalee, First Mehl:<br>
  You preach to the world, and set up your house.<br>
  Abandoning your Yogic postures, how will you find the True Lord?<br>
  You are attached to possessiveness and the love of sexual pleasure.<br>
  You are not a renunciate, nor a man of the world. ||1||<br>
  Yogi, remain seated, and the pain of duality will run away from you.<br>
  You beg from door to door, and you don't feel ashamed. ||1||Pause||<br>
  You sing the songs, but you do not understand your own self.<br>
  How will the burning pain within be relieved?<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, let your mind be absorbed in the Lord's Love,<br>
  and you will intuitively experience the charity of contemplation. ||2||<br>
  You apply ashes to your body, while acting in hypocrisy.<br>
  Attached to Maya, you will be beaten by Death's heavy club.<br>
  Your begging bowl is broken; it will not hold the charity of the Lord's Love.<br>
  Bound in bondage, you come and go. ||3||<br>
  You do not control your seed and semen, and yet you claim to practice abstinence.<br>
  You beg from Maya, lured by the three qualities.<br>
  You have no compassion; the Lord's Light does not shine in you.<br>
  You are drowned, drowned in worldly entanglements. ||4||<br>
  You wear religious robes, and your patched coat assumes many disguises.<br>
  You play all sorts of false tricks, like a juggler.<br>
  The fire of anxiety burns brightly within you.<br>
  Without the karma of good actions, how can you cross over? ||5||<br>
  You make ear-rings of glass to wear in your ears.<br>
  But liberation does not come from learning without understanding.<br>
  You are lured by the tastes of the tongue and sex organs.<br>
  You have become a beast; this sign cannot be erased. ||6||<br>
  The people of the world are entangled in the three modes; the Yogis are entangled in the three modes.<br>
  Contemplating the Word of the Shabad, sorrows are dispelled.<br>
  Through the Shabad, one becomes radiant, pure and truthful.<br>
  One who contemplates the true lifestyle is a Yogi. ||7||<br>
  The nine treasures are with You, Lord; You are potent, the Cause of causes.<br>
  You establish and disestablish; whatever You do, happens.<br>
  One who practices celibacy, chastity, self-control, truth and pure consciousness<br>
  - O Nanak, that Yogi is the friend of the three worlds. ||8||2||<br>
  Raamkalee, First Mehl:<br>
  Above the six chakras of the body dwells the detached mind.<br>
  Awareness of the vibration of the Word of the Shabad has been awakened deep within.<br>
  The unstruck melody of the sound current resonates and resounds within; my mind is attuned to it.<br>
  Through the Guru's Teachings, my faith is confirmed in the True Name. ||1||<br>
  O mortal, through devotion to the Lord, peace is obtained.<br>
  The Lord, Har, Har, seems sweet to the Gurmukh, who merges in the Name of the Lord, Har, Har. ||1||Pause||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 029</h2></center>
  Eradicating attachment to Maya, one merges into the Lord.<br>
  Meeting with the True Guru, we unite in His Union.<br>
  The Naam, the Name of the Lord, is a priceless jewel, a diamond.<br>
  Attuned to it, the mind is comforted and encouraged. ||2||<br>
  The diseases of egotism and possessiveness do not afflict<br>
  one who worships the Lord. Fear of the Messenger of Death runs away.<br>
  The Messenger of Death, the enemy of the soul, does not touch me at all.<br>
  The Immaculate Name of the Lord illuminates my heart. ||3||<br>
  Contemplating the Shabad, we become Nirankaari - we come to belong to the Formless Lord God.<br>
  Awakening to the Guru's Teachings, evil-mindedness is taken away.<br>
  Remaining awake and aware night and day, lovingly focused on the Lord,<br>
  one becomes Jivan Mukta - liberated while yet alive. He finds this state deep within himself. ||4||<br>
  In the secluded cave, I remain unattached.<br>
  With the Word of the Shabad, I have killed the five thieves.<br>
  My mind does not waver or go to the home of any other.<br>
  I remain intuitively absorbed deep within. ||5||<br>
  As Gurmukh, I remain awake and aware, unattached.<br>
  Forever detached, I am woven into the essence of reality.<br>
  The world is asleep; it dies, and comes and goes in reincarnation.<br>
  Without the Word of the Guru's Shabad, it does not understand. ||6||<br>
  The unstruck sound current of the Shabad vibrates day and night.<br>
  The Gurmukh knows the state of the eternal, unchanging Lord God.<br>
  When someone realizes the Shabad, then he truly knows.<br>
  The One Lord is permeating and pervading everywhere in Nirvaanaa. ||7||<br>
  My mind is intuitively absorbed in the state of deepest Samaadhi;<br>
  renouncing egotism and greed, I have come to know the One Lord.<br>
  When the disciple's mind accepts the Guru,<br>
  O Nanak, duality is eradicated, and he merges in the Lord. ||8||3||<br>
  Raamkalee, First Mehl:<br>
  You calculate the auspicious days, but you do not understand<br>
  that the One Creator Lord is above these auspicious days.<br>
  He alone knows the way, who meets the Guru.<br>
  When one follows the Guru's Teachings, then he realizes the Hukam of God's Command. ||1||<br>
  Do not tell lies, O Pandit; O religious scholar, speak the Truth.<br>
  When egotism is eradicated through the Word of the Shabad, then one finds His home. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Calculating and counting, the astrologer draws the horoscope.<br>
  He studies it and announces it, but he does not understand reality.<br>
  Understand, that the Word of the Guru's Shabad is above all.<br>
  Do not speak of anything else; it is all just ashes. ||2||<br>
  You bathe, wash, and worship stones.<br>
  But without being imbued with the Lord, you are the filthiest of the filthy.<br>
  Subduing your pride, you shall receive the supreme wealth of God.<br>
  The mortal is liberated and emancipated, meditating on the Lord. ||3||<br>
  You study the arguments, but do not contemplate the Vedas.<br>
  You drown yourself - how will you save your ancestors?<br>
  How rare is that person who realizes that God is in each and every heart.<br>
  When one meets the True Guru, then he understands. ||4||<br>
  Making his calculations, cynicism and suffering afflict his soul.<br>
  Seeking the Sanctuary of the Guru, peace is found.<br>
  I sinned and made mistakes, but now I seek Your Sanctuary.<br>
  The Guru led me to meet the Lord, according to my past actions. ||5||<br>
  If one does not enter the Guru's Sanctuary, God cannot be found.<br>
  Deluded by doubt, one is born, only to die, and come back again.<br>
  Dying in corruption, he is bound and gagged at Death's door.<br>
  The Naam, the Name of the Lord, is not in his heart, and he does not act according to the Shabad. ||6||<br>
  Some call themselves Pandits, religious scholars and spiritual teachers.<br>
  Tinged with double-mindedness, they do not find the Mansion of the Lord's Presence.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 030</h2></center>
  One who takes the Support of the Naam, by Guru's Grace,<br>
  is a rare person, one among millions, incomparable. ||7||<br>
  One is bad, and another good, but the One True Lord is contained in all.<br>
  Understand this, O spiritual teacher, through the support of the True Guru:<br>
  rare indeed is that Gurmukh, who realizes the One Lord.<br>
  His comings and goings cease, and he merges in the Lord. ||8||<br>
  Those who have the One Universal Creator Lord within their hearts,<br>
  possess all virtues; they contemplate the True Lord.<br>
  One who acts in harmony with the Guru's Will,<br>
  O Nanak, is absorbed in the Truest of the True. ||9||4||<br>
  Raamkalee, First Mehl:<br>
  Practicing restraint by Hatha Yoga, the body wears away.<br>
  The mind is not softened by fasting or austerities.<br>
  Nothing else is equal to worship of the Lord's Name. ||1||<br>
  Serve the Guru, O mind, and associate with the humble servants of the Lord.<br>
  The tyrannical Messenger of Death cannot touch you, and the serpent of Maya cannot sting you, when you drink in the sublime essence of the Lord. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The world reads the arguments, and is softened only by music.<br>
  In the three modes and corruption, they are born and die.<br>
  Without the Lord's Name, they endure suffering and pain. ||2||<br>
  The Yogi draws the breath upwards, and opens the Tenth Gate.<br>
  He practices inner cleansing and the six rituals of purification.<br>
  But without the Lord's Name, the breath he draws is useless. ||3||<br>
  The fire of the five passions burns within him; how can he be calm?<br>
  The thief is within him; how can he taste the taste?<br>
  One who becomes Gurmukh conquers the body-fortress. ||4||<br>
  With filth within, he wanders around at places of pilgrimage.<br>
  His mind is not pure, so what is the use of performing ritual cleansings?<br>
  He carries the karma of his own past actions; who else can he blame? ||5||<br>
  He does not eat food; he tortures his body.<br>
  Without the Guru's wisdom, he is not satisfied.<br>
  The self-willed manmukh is born only to die, and be born again. ||6||<br>
  Go, and ask the True Guru, and associate with the Lord's humble servants.<br>
  Your mind shall merge into the Lord, and you shall not be reincarnated to die again.<br>
  Without the Lord's Name, what can anyone do? ||7||<br>
  Silence the mouse scurrying around within you.<br>
  Serve the Primal Lord, by chanting the Lord's Name.<br>
  O Nanak, God blesses us with His Name, when He grants His Grace. ||8||5||<br>
  Raamkalee, First Mehl:<br>
  The created Universe emanated from within You; there is no other at all.<br>
  Whatever is said to be, is from You, O God.<br>
  He is the True Lord and Master, throughout the ages.<br>
  Creation and destruction do not come from anyone else. ||1||<br>
  Such is my Lord and Master, profound and unfathomable.<br>
  Whoever meditates on Him, finds peace. The arrow of the Messenger of Death does not strike one who has the Name of the Lord. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The Naam, the Name of the Lord, is a priceless jewel, a diamond.<br>
  The True Lord Master is immortal and immeasurable.<br>
  That tongue which chants the True Name is pure.<br>
  The True Lord is in the home of the self; there is no doubt about it. ||2||<br>
  Some sit in the forests, and some make their home in the mountains.<br>
  Forgetting the Naam, they rot away in egotistical pride.<br>
  Without the Naam, what is the use of spiritual wisdom and meditation?<br>
  The Gurmukhs are honored in the Court of the Lord. ||3||<br>
  Acting stubbornly in egotism, one does not find the Lord.<br>
  Studying the scriptures, reading them to other people,<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 031</h2></center>
  and wandering around at places of pilgrimage, the disease is not taken away.<br>
  Without the Naam, how can one find peace? ||4||<br>
  No matter how much he tries, he cannot control his semen and seed.<br>
  His mind wavers, and he falls into hell.<br>
  Bound and gagged in the City of Death, he is tortured.<br>
  Without the Name, his soul cries out in agony. ||5||<br>
  The many Siddhas and seekers, silent sages and demi-gods<br>
  cannot satisfy themselves by practicing restraint through Hatha Yoga.<br>
  One who contemplates the Word of the Shabad, and serves the Guru<br>
  - his mind and body become immaculate, and his egotistical pride is obliterated. ||6||<br>
  Blessed with Your Grace, I obtain the True Name.<br>
  I remain in Your Sanctuary, in loving devotion.<br>
  Love for Your devotional worship has welled up within me.<br>
  As Gurmukh, I chant and meditate on the Lord's Name. ||7||<br>
  When one is rid of egotism and pride, his mind is drenched in the Lord's Love.<br>
  Practicing fraud and hypocrisy, he does not find God.<br>
  Without the Word of the Guru's Shabad, he cannot find the Lord's Door.<br>
  O Nanak, the Gurmukh contemplates the essence of reality. ||8||6||<br>
  Raamkalee, First Mehl:<br>
  As you come, so will you leave, you fool; as you were born, so will you die.<br>
  As you enjoy pleasures, so will you suffer pain. Forgetting the Naam, the Name of the Lord, you will fall into the terrifying world-ocean. ||1||<br>
  Gazing upon your body and wealth, you are so proud.<br>
  Your love for gold and sexual pleasures increases; why have you forgotten the Naam, and why do you wander in doubt? ||1||Pause||<br>
  You do not practice truth, abstinence, self-discipline or humility; the ghost within your skeleton has turned to dry wood.<br>
  You have not practiced charity, donations, cleansing baths or austerities. Without the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy, your life has gone in vain. ||2||<br>
  Attached to greed, you have forgotten the Naam. Coming and going, your life has been ruined.<br>
  When the Messenger of Death grabs you by your hair, you will be punished. You are unconscious, and have fallen into Death's mouth. ||3||<br>
  Day and night, you jealously slander others; in your heart, you have neither the Naam, nor compassion for all.<br>
  Without the Word of the Guru's Shabad, you will not find salvation or honor. Without the Lord's Name, you shall go to hell. ||4||<br>
  In an instant, you change into various costumes, like a juggler; you are entangled in emotional attachment and sin.<br>
  You gaze here and there upon the expanse of Maya; you are intoxicated with attachment to Maya. ||5||<br>
  You act in corruption, and put on ostentatious shows, but without awareness of the Shabad, you have fallen into confusion.<br>
  You suffer great pain from the disease of egotism. Following the Guru's Teachings, you shall be rid of this disease. ||6||<br>
  Seeing peace and wealth come to him, the faithless cynic become proud in his mind.<br>
  But He who owns this body and wealth, takes them back again, and then the mortal feels anxiety and pain deep within. ||7||<br>
  At the very last instant, nothing goes along with you; all is visible only by His Mercy.<br>
  God is our Primal and Infinite Lord; enshrining the Lord's Name in the heart, one crosses over. ||8||<br>
  You weep for the dead, but who hears you weeping? The dead have fallen to the serpent in the terrifying world-ocean.<br>
  Gazing upon his family, wealth, household and mansions, the faithless cynic is entangled in worthless worldly affairs. ||9||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 032</h2></center>
  He comes when the Lord sends him; when the Lord calls him back, he goes.<br>
  Whatever he does, the Lord is doing. The Forgiving Lord forgives him. ||10||<br>
  I seek to be with those who have tasted this sublime essence of the Lord.<br>
  Wealth, miraculous spiritual powers, wisdom and spiritual knowledge, are obtained from the Guru. The treasure of liberation is obtained in His Sanctuary. ||11||<br>
  The Gurmukh looks upon pain and pleasure as one and the same; he remains untouched by joy and sorrow.<br>
  Conquering his self-conceit, the Gurmukh finds the Lord; O Nanak, he intuitively merges into the Lord. ||12||7||<br>
  Raamkalee, Dakhanee, First Mehl:<br>
  Abstinence, chastity, self-control and truthfulness have been implanted within me; I am imbued with the sublime essence of the True Word of the Shabad. ||1||<br>
  My Merciful Guru remains forever imbued with the Lord's Love.<br>
  Day and night, He remains lovingly focused on the One Lord; gazing upon the True Lord, He is pleased. ||1||Pause||<br>
  He abides in the Tenth Gate, and looks equally upon all; He is imbued with the unstruck sound current of the Shabad. ||2||<br>
  Wearing the loin-cloth of chastity, He remains absorbed in the all-pervading Lord; His tongue enjoys the taste of God's Love. ||3||<br>
  The One who created the creation has met the True Guru; contemplating the Guru's lifestyle, He is pleased. ||4||<br>
  All are in the One, and the One is in all. This is what the True Guru has shown me. ||5||<br>
  He who created the worlds, solar systems and galaxies - that God cannot be known. ||6||<br>
  From the lamp of God, the lamp within is lit; the Divine Light illuminates the three worlds. ||7||<br>
  The Guru sits on the true throne in the true mansion; He is attuned, absorbed in the Fearless Lord. ||8||<br>
  The Guru, the detached Yogi, has enticed the hearts of all; He plays His harp in each and every heart. ||9||<br>
  O Nanak, in God's Sanctuary, one is emancipated; the True Guru becomes our true help and support. ||10||8||<br>
  Raamkalee, First Mehl:<br>
  He has made His home in the monastery of the heart; He has infused His power into the earth and the sky. ||1||<br>
  Through the Word of the Shabad, the Gurmukhs have saved so very many, O Saints. ||1||Pause||<br>
  He conquers attachment, and eradicates egotism, and sees Your Divine Light pervading the three worlds, Lord. ||2||<br>
  He conquers desire, and enshrines the Lord within his mind; he contemplates the Word of the True Guru's Shabad. ||3||<br>
  The horn of consciousness vibrates the unstruck sound current; Your Light illuminates each and every heart, Lord. ||4||<br>
  He plays the flute of the universe in his mind, and lights the fire of God. ||5||<br>
  Bringing together the five elements, day and night, the Lord's lamp shines with the Immaculate Light of the Infinite. ||6||<br>
  The right and left nostrils, the sun and the moon channels, are the strings of the body-harp; they vibrate the wondrous melody of the Shabad. ||7||<br>
  The true hermit obtains a seat in the City of God, the invisible, inaccessible, infinite. ||8||<br>
  The mind is the king of the city of the body; the five sources of knowledge dwell within it. ||9||<br>
  Seated in his home, this king chants the Shabad; he administers justice and virtue. ||10||<br>
  What can poor death or birth say to him? Conquering his mind, he remains dead while yet alive. ||11||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 033</h2></center>
  Brahma, Vishnu and Shiva are manifestations of the One God. He Himself is the Doer of deeds. ||12||<br>
  One who purifies his body, crosses over the terrifying world-ocean; he contemplates the essence of his own soul. ||13||<br>
  Serving the Guru, he finds everlasting peace; deep within, the Shabad permeates him, coloring him with virtue. ||14||<br>
  The Giver of virtue unites with Himself, one who conquers egotism and desire. ||15||<br>
  Eradicating the three qualities, dwell in the fourth state. This is the unparalleled devotional worship. ||16||<br>
  This is the Yoga of the Gurmukh: Through the Shabad, he understands his own soul, and he enshrines within his heart the One Lord. ||17||<br>
  Imbued with the Shabad, his mind becomes steady and stable; this is the most excellent action. ||18||<br>
  This true hermit does not enter into religious debates or hypocrisy; the Gurmukh contemplates the Shabad. ||19||<br>
  The Gurmukh practices Yoga - he is the true hermit; he practices abstinence and truth, and contemplates the Shabad. ||20||<br>
  One who dies in the Shabad and conquers his mind is the true hermit; he understands the Way of Yoga. ||21||<br>
  Attachment to Maya is the terrifying world-ocean; through the Shabad, the true hermit saves himself, and his ancestors as well. ||22||<br>
  Contemplating the Shabad, you shall be a hero throughout the four ages, O hermit; contemplate the Word of the Guru's Bani in devotion. ||23||<br>
  This mind is enticed by Maya, O hermit; contemplating the Shabad, you shall find release. ||24||<br>
  He Himself forgives, and unites in His Union; Nanak seeks Your Sanctuary, Lord. ||25||9||<br>
  Raamkalee, Third Mehl, Ashtapadees:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Make humility your ear-rings, Yogi, and compassion your patched coat.<br>
  Let coming and going be the ashes you apply to your body, Yogi, and then you shall conquer the three worlds. ||1||<br>
  Play that harp, Yogi,<br>
  which vibrates the unstruck sound current, and remain lovingly absorbed in the Lord. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Make truth and contentment your plate and pouch, Yogi; take the Ambrosial Naam as your food.<br>
  Make meditation your walking stick, Yogi, and make higher consciousness the horn you blow. ||2||<br>
  Make your stable mind the Yogic posture you sit in, Yogi, and then you shall be rid of your tormenting desires.<br>
  Go begging in the village of the body, Yogi, and then, you shall obtain the Naam in your lap. ||3||<br>
  This harp does not center you in meditation, Yogi, nor does it bring the True Name into your lap.<br>
  This harp does not bring you peace, Yogi, nor eliminate egotism from within you. ||4||<br>
  Make the Fear of God, and the Love of God, the two gourds of your lute, Yogi, and make this body its neck.<br>
  Become Gurmukh, and then vibrate the strings; in this way, your desires shall depart. ||5||<br>
  One who understands the Hukam of the Lord's Command is called a Yogi; he links his consciousness to the One Lord.<br>
  His cynicism is dispelled, and he becomes immaculately pure; this is how he finds the Way of Yoga. ||6||<br>
  Everything that comes into view shall be destroyed; focus your consciousness on the Lord.<br>
  Enshrine love for the True Guru, and then you shall obtain this understanding. ||7||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 034</h2></center>
  This is not Yoga, O Yogi, to abandon your family and wander around.<br>
  The Name of the Lord, Har, Har, is within the household of the body. By Guru's Grace, you shall find your Lord God. ||8||<br>
  This world is a puppet of clay, Yogi; the terrible disease, the desire for Maya is in it.<br>
  Making all sorts of efforts, and wearing religious robes, Yogi, this disease cannot be cured. ||9||<br>
  The Name of the Lord is the medicine, Yogi; the Lord enshrines it in the mind.<br>
  One who becomes Gurmukh understands this; he alone finds the Way of Yoga. ||10||<br>
  The Path of Yoga is very difficult, Yogi; he alone finds it, whom God blesses with His Grace.<br>
  Inside and outside, he sees the One Lord; he eliminates doubt from within himself. ||11||<br>
  So play the harp which vibrates without being played, Yogi.<br>
  Says Nanak, thus you shall be liberated, Yogi, and remain merged in the True Lord. ||12||1||10||<br>
  Raamkalee, Third Mehl:<br>
  The treasure of devotional worship is revealed to the Gurmukh; the True Guru has inspired me to understand this understanding. ||1||<br>
  O Saints, the Gurmukh is blessed with glorious greatness. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Dwelling always in Truth, celestial peace wells up; sexual desire and anger are eliminated from within. ||2||<br>
  Eradicating self-conceit, remain lovingly focused on the Naam, the Name of the Lord; through the Word of the Shabad, burn away possessiveness. ||3||<br>
  By Him we are created, and by Him we are destroyed; in the end, the Naam will be our only help and support. ||4||<br>
  He is ever-present; don't think that He is far away. He created the creation. ||5||<br>
  Deep within your heart, chant the True Word of the Shabad; remain lovingly absorbed in the True Lord. ||6||<br>
  The Priceless Naam is in the Society of the Saints; by great good fortune, it is obtained. ||7||<br>
  Do not be deluded by doubt; serve the True Guru, and keep your mind steady in one place. ||8||<br>
  Without the Name, everyone wanders around in confusion; they waste away their lives in vain. ||9||<br>
  Yogi, you have lost the Way; you wander around confused. Through hypocrisy, Yoga is not attained. ||10||<br>
  Sitting in Yogic postures in the City of God, through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, you shall find Yoga. ||11||<br>
  Restrain your restless wanderings through the Shabad, and the Naam will come to dwell in your mind. ||12||<br>
  This body is a pool, O Saints; bathe in it, and enshrine love for the Lord. ||13||<br>
  Those who cleanse themselves through the Naam, are the most immaculate people; through the Shabad, they wash off their filth. ||14||<br>
  Trapped by the three qualities, the unconscious person does not think of the Naam; without the Name, he wastes away. ||15||<br>
  The three forms of Brahma, Vishnu and Shiva are trapped in the three qualities, lost in confusion. ||16||<br>
  By Guru's Grace, this triad is eradicated, and one is lovingly absorbed in the fourth state. ||17||<br>
  The Pandits, the religious scholars, read, study and discuss the arguments; they do not understand. ||18||<br>
  Engrossed in corruption, they wander in confusion; who can they possibly instruct, O Siblings of Destiny? ||19||<br>
  The Bani, the Word of the humble devotee is the most sublime and exalted; it prevails throughout the ages. ||20||<br>
  One who is committed to this Bani is emancipated, and through the Shabad, merges in Truth. ||21||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 035</h2></center>
  One who searches the village of the body, through the Shabad, obtains the nine treasures of the Naam. ||22||<br>

  Let your eyes gaze upon the Wondrous Lord; let your consciousness be attached to the Unseen Lord. ||24||<br>

  I praise my Guru forever, who has inspired me to understand this true understanding. ||26||<br>

  Raamkalee, Third Mehl:<br>
  It is so hard to obtain that devotional worship of the Lord, O Saints. It cannot be described at all. ||1||<br>
  O Saints, as Gurmukh, find the Perfect Lord,<br>
  and worship the Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Without the Lord, everything is filthy, O Saints; what offering should I place before Him? ||2||<br>
  Whatever pleases the True Lord is devotional worship; His Will abides in the mind. ||3||<br>
  Everyone worships Him, O Saints, but the self-willed manmukh is not accepted or approved. ||4||<br>
  If someone dies in the Word of the Shabad, his mind become immaculate, O Saints; such worship is accepted and approved. ||5||<br>
  Sanctified and pure are those true beings, who enshrine love for the Shabad. ||6||<br>
  There is no worship of the Lord, other than the Name; the world wanders, deluded by doubt. ||7||<br>
  The Gurmukh understands his own self, O Saints; he lolvingly centers his mind on the Lord's Name. ||8||<br>
  The Immaculate Lord Himself inspires worship of Him; through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, it is accepted and approved. ||9||<br>
  Those who worship Him, but do not know the Way, are polluted with the love of duality. ||10||<br>
  One who becomes Gurmukh, knows what worship is; the Lord's Will abides within his mind. ||11||<br>
  One who accepts the Lord's Will obtains total peace, O Saints; in the end, the Naam will be our help and support. ||12||<br>
  One who does not understand his own self, O Saints, falsely flatters himself. ||13||<br>
  The Messenger of Death does not give up on those who practices hypocrisy; they are dragged away in disgrace. ||14||<br>
  Those who have the Shabad deep within, understand themselves; they find the way of salvation. ||15||<br>
  Their minds enter into the deepest state of Samaadhi, and their light is absorbed into the Light. ||16||<br>
  The Gurmukhs listen constantly to the Naam, and chant it in the True Congregation. ||17||<br>
  The Gurmukhs sing the Lord's Praises, and erase self-conceit; they obtain true honor in the Court of the Lord. ||18||<br>
  True are their words; they speak only the Truth; they lovingly focus on the True Name. ||19||<br>
  My God is the Destroyer of fear, the Destroyer of sin; in the end, He is our only help and support. ||20||<br>
  He Himself pervades and permeates everything; O Nanak, glorious greatness is obtained through the Naam. ||21||3||12||<br>
  Raamkalee, Third Mehl:<br>
  I am filthy and polluted, proud and egotistical; receiving the Word of the Shabad, my filth is taken away. ||1||<br>
  O Saints, the Gurmukhs are saved through the Naam, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  The True Name abides deep within their hearts. The Creator Himself embellishes them. ||1||Pause||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 036</h2></center>
  Touching the philosopher's stone, they themselves become the philosopher's stone; the Dear Lord Himself blesses them with His Mercy. ||2||<br>
  Some wear religious robes, and wander around in pride; they lose their life in the gamble. ||3||<br>
  Some worship the Lord in devotion, night and day; day and night, they keep the Lord's Name enshrined in their hearts. ||4||<br>
  Those who are imbued with Him night and day, are spontaneously intoxicated with Him; they intuitively conquer their ego. ||5||<br>
  Without the Fear of God, devotional worship is never performed; through the Love and the Fear of God, devotional worship is embellished. ||6||<br>
  The Shabad burns away emotional attachment to Maya, and then one contemplates the essence of spiritual wisdom. ||7||<br>
  The Creator Himself inspires us to act; He Himself blesses us with His treasure. ||8||<br>
  The limits of His virtues cannot be found; I sing His Praises and contemplate the Word of the Shabad. ||9||<br>
  I chant the Lord's Name, and praise my Dear Lord; egotism is eradicated from within me. ||10||<br>
  The treasure of the Naam is obtained from the Guru; the treasures of the True Lord are inexhaustible. ||11||<br>
  He Himself is pleased with His devotees; by His Grace, He infuses His strength within them. ||12||<br>
  They always feel hunger for the True Name; they sing and contemplate the Shabad. ||13||<br>
  Soul, body and everything are His; it is so difficult to speak of, and contemplate Him. ||14||<br>
  Those humble beings who are attached to the Shabad are saved; they cross over the terrifying world-ocean. ||15||<br>
  Without the True Lord, no one can cross over; how rare are those who contemplate and understand this. ||16||<br>
  We obtain only that which is pre-ordained; receiving the Lord's Shabad, we are embellished. ||17||<br>
  Imbued with the Shabad, the body becomes golden, and loves only the True Name. ||18||<br>
  The body is then filled to overflowing with Ambrosial Nectar, obtained by contemplating the Shabad. ||19||<br>
  Those who seek God, find Him; others burst and die from their own egotism. ||20||<br>
  The debaters waste away, while the servants serve, with love and affection for the Guru. ||21||<br>
  He alone is a Yogi, who contemplates the essence of spiritual wisdom, and conquers egotism and thirsty desire. ||22||<br>
  The True Guru, the Great Giver, is revealed to those upon whom You bestow Your Grace, O Lord. ||23||<br>
  Those who do not serve the True Guru, and who are attached to Maya, are drowned; they die in their own egotism. ||24||<br>
  As long as there is breath within you, so long you should serve the Lord; then, you will go and meet the Lord. ||25||<br>
  Night and day, she remains awake and aware, day and night; she is the darling bride of her Beloved Husband Lord. ||26||<br>
  I offer my body and mind in sacrifice to my Guru; I am a sacrifice to Him. ||27||<br>
  Attachment to Maya will end and go away; only by contemplating the Shabad will you be saved. ||28||<br>
  They are awake and aware, whom the Lord Himself awakens; so contemplate the Word of the Guru's Shabad. ||29||<br>
  O Nanak, those who do not remember the Naam are dead. The devotees live in contemplative meditation. ||30||4||13||<br>
  Raamkalee, Third Mehl:<br>
  Receiving the treasure of the Naam, the Name of the Lord, from the Guru, I remain satisfied and fulfilled. ||1||<br>
  O Saints, the Gurmukhs attain the state of liberation.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 037</h2></center>
  The One Name abides deep within my heart; such is the glorious greatness of the Perfect Lord. ||1||Pause||<br>
  He Himself is the Creator, and He Himself is the Enjoyer. He Himself gives sustenance to all. ||2||<br>
  Whatever He wants to do, He is doing; no one else can do anything. ||3||<br>
  He Himself fashions and creates the creation; He links each and every person to their task. ||4||<br>
  If you serve Him, then you will find peace; the True Guru will unite you in His Union. ||5||<br>
  The Lord Himself creates Himself; the Unseen Lord cannot be seen. ||6||<br>
  He Himself kills, and brings back to life; He does not have even an iota of greed. ||7||<br>
  Some are made givers, and some are made beggars; He Himself inspires us to devotional worship. ||8||<br>
  Those who know the One Lord are very fortunate; they remain absorbed in the True Lord. ||9||<br>
  He Himself is beautiful, He Himself is wise and clever; His worth cannot be expressed. ||10||<br>
  He Himself infuses pain and pleasure; He Himself makes them wander around in doubt. ||11||<br>
  The Great Giver is revealed to the Gurmukh; without the Guru, the world wanders in darkness. ||12||<br>
  Those who taste, enjoy the flavor; the True Guru imparts this understanding. ||13||<br>
  Some, the Lord causes to forget and lose the Name; others become Gurmukh, and are granted this understanding. ||14||<br>
  Forever and ever, praise the Lord, O Saints; how glorious is His greatness! ||15||<br>
  There is no other King except Him; He administers justice, as He has made it. ||16||<br>
  His justice is always True; how rare are those who accept His Command. ||17||<br>
  O mortal, meditate forever on the Lord, who has made the Gurmukh in His making. ||18||<br>
  That humble being who meets with the True Guru is fulfilled; the Naam abides in his heart. ||19||<br>
  The True Lord is Himself forever True; He announces His Bani, the Word of His Shabad. ||20||<br>
  Nanak is wonderstruck, hearing and seeing His Lord; my God is all-pervading, everywhere. ||21||5||14||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl, Ashtapadees:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Some make a big show of their worldly influence.<br>
  Some make a big show of devotional worship.<br>
  Some practice inner cleansing teahniques, and control the breath through Kundalini Yoga.<br>
  I am meek; I worship and adore the Lord, Har, Har. ||1||<br>
  I place my faith in You alone, O Beloved Lord.<br>
  I do not know any other way. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Some abandon their homes, and live in the forests.<br>
  Some put themselves on silence, and call themselves hermits.<br>
  Some claim that they are devotees of the One Lord alone.<br>
  I am meek; I seek the shelter and support of the Lord, Har, Har. ||2||<br>
  Some say that they live at sacred shrines of pilgrimage.<br>
  Some refuse food and become Udaasis, shaven-headed renunciates.<br>
  Some have wandered all across the earth.<br>
  I am meek; I have fallen at the door of the Lord, Har, Har. ||3||<br>
  Some say that they belong to great and noble families.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 038</h2></center>
  Some say that they have the arms of their many brothers to protect them.<br>
  Some say that they have great expanses of wealth.<br>
  I am meek; I have the support of the Lord, Har, Har. ||4||<br>
  Some dance, wearing ankle bells.<br>
  Some fast and take vows, and wear malas.<br>
  Some apply ceremonial tilak marks to their foreheads.<br>
  I am meek; I meditate on the Lord, Har, Har, Har. ||5||<br>
  Some work spells using the miraculous spiritual powers of the Siddhas.<br>
  Some wear various religious robes and establish their authority.<br>
  Some perform Tantric spells, and chant various mantras.<br>
  I am meek; I serve the Lord, Har, Har, Har. ||6||<br>
  One calls himself a wise Pandit, a religious scholar.<br>
  One performs the six rituals to appease Shiva.<br>
  One maintains the rituals of pure lifestyle, and does good deeds.<br>
  I am meek; I seek the Sanctuary of the Lord, Har, Har, Har. ||7||<br>
  I have studied the religions and rituals of all the ages.<br>
  Without the Name, this mind is not awakened.<br>
  Says Nanak, when I found the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy,<br>
  my thirsty desires were satisfied, and I was totally cooled and soothed. ||8||1||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  He created you out of this water.<br>
  From clay, He fashioned your body.<br>
  He blessed you with the light of reason and clear consciousness.<br>
  In your mother's womb, He preserved you. ||1||<br>
  Contemplate your Savior Lord.<br>
  Give up all others thoughts, O mind. ||1||Pause||<br>
  He gave you your mother and father;<br>
  he gave you your charming children and siblings;<br>
  he gave you your spouse and friends;<br>
  enshrine that Lord and Master in your consciousness. ||2||<br>
  He gave you the invaluable air;<br>
  He gave you the priceless water;<br>
  He gave you burning fire;<br>
  let your mind remain in the Sanctuary of that Lord and Master. ||3||<br>
  He gave you the thirty-six varieties of tasty foods;<br>
  He gave you a place within to hold them;<br>
  He gave you the earth, and things to use;<br>
  enshrine in your consciousness the feet of that Lord and Master. ||4||<br>
  He gave you eyes to see, and ears to hear;<br>
  He gave you hands to work with, and a nose and a tongue;<br>
  He gave you feet to walk upon, and the crowning glory of your head;<br>
  O mind, worship the Feet of that Lord and Master. ||5||<br>
  He transformed you from impure to pure;<br>
  He installed you above the heads of all creatures;<br>
  now, you may fulfill your destiny or not;<br>
  Your affairs shall be resolved, O mind, meditating on God. ||6||<br>
  Here and there, only the One God exists.<br>
  Wherever I look, there You are.<br>
  My mind is reluctant to serve Him;<br>
  forgetting Him, I cannot survive, even for an instant. ||7||<br>
  I am a sinner, without any virtue at all.<br>
  I do not serve You, or do any good deeds.<br>
  By great good fortune, I have found the boat - the Guru.<br>
  Slave Nanak has crossed over, with Him. ||8||2||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Some pass their lives enjoying pleasures and beauty.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 039</h2></center>
  Some pass their lives with their mothers, fathers and children.<br>
  Some pass their lives in power, estates and trade.<br>
  The Saints pass their lives with the support of the Lord's Name. ||1||<br>
  The world is the creation of the True Lord.<br>
  He alone is the Master of all. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Some pass their lives in arguments and debates about scriptures.<br>
  Some pass their lives tasting flavors.<br>
  Some pass their lives attached to women.<br>
  The Saints are absorbed only in the Name of the Lord. ||2||<br>
  Some pass their lives gambling.<br>
  Some pass their lives getting drunk.<br>
  Some pass their lives stealing the property of others.<br>
  The humble servants of the Lord pass their lives meditating on the Naam. ||3||<br>
  Some pass their lives in Yoga, strict meditation, worship and adoration.<br>
  Some, in sickness, sorrow and doubt.<br>
  Some pass their lives practicing control of the breath.<br>
  The Saints pass their lives singing the Kirtan of the Lord's Praises. ||4||<br>
  Some pass their lives walking day and night.<br>
  Some pass their lives on the fields of battle.<br>
  Some pass their lives teaching children.<br>
  The Saints pass their lives singing the Lord's Praise. ||5||<br>
  Some pass their lives as actors, acting and dancing.<br>
  Some pass their lives taking the lives of others.<br>
  Some pass their lives ruling by intimidation.<br>
  The Saints pass their lives chanting the Lord's Praises. ||6||<br>
  Some pass their lives counseling and giving advice.<br>
  Some pass their lives forced to serve others.<br>
  Some pass their lives exploring life's mysteries.<br>
  The Saints pass their lives drinking in the sublime essence of the Lord. ||7||<br>
  As the Lord attaches us, so we are attached.<br>
  No one is foolish, and no one is wise.<br>
  Nanak is a sacrifice, a sacrifice to those who are blessed by His Grace to receive His Name. ||8||3||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Even in a forest fire, some trees remain green.<br>
  The infant is released from the pain of the mother's womb.<br>
  Meditating in remembrance on the Naam, the Name of the Lord, fear is dispelled.<br>
  Just so, the Sovereign Lord protects and saves the Saints. ||1||<br>
  Such is the Merciful Lord, my Protector.<br>
  Wherever I look, I see You cherishing and nurturing. ||1||Pause||<br>
  As thirst is quenched by drinking water;<br>
  as the bride blossoms forth when her husband comes home;<br>
  as wealth is the support of the greedy person<br>
  - just so, the humble servant of the Lord loves the Name of the Lord, Har, Har. ||2||<br>
  As the farmer protects his fields;<br>
  as the mother and father show compassion to their child;<br>
  as the lover merges on seeing the beloved;<br>
  just so does the Lord hug His humble servant close in His Embrace. ||3||<br>
  As the blind man is in ecstasy, when he can see again;<br>
  and the mute, when he is able to speak and sing songs;<br>
  and the cripple, being able to climb over the mountain<br>
  - just so, the Name of the Lord saves all. ||4||<br>
  As cold is dispelled by fire,<br>
  sins are driven out in the Society of the Saints.<br>
  As cloth is cleaned by soap,<br>
  just so, by chanting the Naam, all doubts and fears are dispelled. ||5||<br>
  As the chakvi bird longs for the sun,<br>
  as the rainbird thirsts for the rain drop,<br>
  as the deer's ears are attuned to the sound of the bell,<br>
  the Lord's Name is pleasing to the mind of the Lord's humble servant. ||6||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 040</h2></center>
  By Your Grace, we love You.<br>
  When You show Mercy, then You come into our minds.<br>
  When the Support of the earth granted His Grace,<br>
  then I was released from my bonds. ||7||<br>
  I have seen all places with my eyes wide open.<br>
  There is no other than Him.<br>
  Doubt and fear are dispelled, by Guru's Grace.<br>
  Nanak sees the wondrous Lord everywhere. ||8||4||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  All beings and creatures that are seen, God, depend on Your Support. ||1||<br>
  This mind is saved through the Name of the Lord. ||1||Pause||<br>
  In an instant, He establishes and disestablishes, by His Creative Power. All is the Creation of the Creator. ||2||<br>
  Sexual desire, anger, greed, falsehood and slander are banished in the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy. ||3||<br>
  Chanting the Naam, the Name of the Lord, the mind becomes immaculate, and life is passed in absolute peace. ||4||<br>
  That mortal who enters the Sanctuary of the devotees, does not lose out, here or hereafter. ||5||<br>
  Pleasure and pain, and the condition of this mind, I place before You, Lord. ||6||<br>
  You are the Giver of all beings; You cherish what You have made. ||7||<br>
  So many millions of times, Nanak is a sacrifice to Your humble servants. ||8||5||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl, Ashtapadee:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Receiving the Blessed Vision of His Darshan, all sins are erased, and He unites me with the Lord. ||1||<br>
  My Guru is the Transcendent Lord, the Giver of peace.<br>
  He implants the Naam, the Name of the Supreme Lord God within us; in the end, He is our help and support. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The source of all pain within is destroyed; I apply the dust of the feet of the Saints to my forehead. ||2||<br>
  In an instant, He purifies the sinners, and dispels the darkness of ignorance. ||3||<br>
  The Lord is all-powerful, the Cause of causes. Nanak seeks His Sanctuary. ||4||<br>
  Shattering the bonds, the Guru implants the Lord's lotus feet within, and lovingly attunes us to the One Word of the Shabad. ||5||<br>
  He has lifted me up, and pulled me out of the deep, dark pit of sin; I am attuned to the True Shabad. ||6||<br>
  The fear of birth and death is taken away; I shall never wander again. ||7||<br>
  This mind is imbued with the sublime elixir of the Naam; drinking in the Ambrosial Nectar, it is satisfied. ||8||<br>
  Joining the Society of the Saints, I sing the Kirtan of the Lord's Praises; I dwell in the eternal, unchanging place. ||9||<br>
  The Perfect Guru has given me the perfect teachings; there is nothing except the Lord, O Siblings of Destiny. ||10||<br>
  I have obtained the treasure of the Naam, by great good fortune; O Nanak, I shall not fall into hell. ||11||<br>
  Clever tricks have not worked for me; I shall act according to the Instructions of the Perfect Guru. ||12||<br>
  He is chanting, intense meditation, austere self-discipline and purification. He Himself acts, and causes us to act. ||13||<br>
  In the midst of children and spouse, and utter corruption, the True Guru has carried me across. ||14||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 041</h2></center>
  You Yourself take care of Your beings; You Yourself attach them to the hem of Your robe. ||15||<br>
  I have built the boat of true Dharmic faith, to cross over the terrifying world-ocean. ||16||<br>
  The Lord Master is unlimited and endless; Nanak is a sacrifice, a sacrifice to Him. ||17||<br>
  Being of Immortal Manifestation, He is not born; He is self-existent; He is the Light in the darkness of Kali Yuga. ||18||<br>
  He is the Inner-knower, the Searcher of hearts, the Giver of souls; gazing upon Him, I am satisfied and fulfilled. ||19||<br>
  He is the One Universal Creator Lord, immaculate and fearless; He is permeating and pervading all the water and the land. ||20||<br>
  He blesses His devotees with the Gift of devotional worship; Nanak longs for the Lord, O my mother. ||21||1||6||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl,<br>
  Shalok:<br>
  Study the Word of the Shabad, O beloveds. It is your anchoring support in life and in death.<br>
  Your face shall be radiant, and you will be at peace forever, O Nanak, meditating in remembrance on the One Lord. ||1||<br>
  My mind and body are imbued with my Beloved Lord; I have been blessed with loving devotion to the Lord, O Saints. ||1||<br>
  The True Guru has approved my cargo, O Saints.<br>
  He has blessed His slave with the profit of the Lord's Name; all my thirst is quenched, O Saints. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Searching and searching, I have found the One Lord, the jewel; I cannot express His value, O Saints. ||2||<br>
  I focus my meditation on His Lotus Feet; I am absorbed in the True Vision of His Darshan, O Saints. ||3||<br>
  Singing, singing His Glorious Praises, I am enraptured; meditating in remembrance on the Lord, I am satisfied and fulfilled, O Saints. ||4||<br>
  The Lord, the Supreme Soul, is permeating within all; what comes, and what goes, O Saints? ||5||<br>
  At the very beginning of time, and throughout the ages, He is, and He shall always be; He is the Giver of peace to all beings, O Saints. ||6||<br>
  He Himself is endless; His end cannot be found. He is totally pervading and permeating everywhere, O Saints. ||7||<br>
  Nanak: the Lord is my friend, companion, wealth, youth, son, father and mother, O Saints. ||8||2||7||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  In thought, word and deed, I contemplate the Lord's Name.<br>
  The horrible world-ocean is very treacherous; O Nanak, the Gurmukh is carried across. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Inwardly, peace, and outwardly, peace; meditating on the Lord, evil tendencies are crushed. ||1||<br>
  He has rid me of what was clinging to me; my Dear Lord God has blessed me with His Grace. ||2||<br>
  The Saints are saved, in His Sanctuary; the very egotistical people rot away and die. ||3||<br>
  In the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy, I have obtained this fruit, the Support of the One Name alone. ||4||<br>
  No one is strong, and no one is weak; all are manifestations of Your Light, Lord. ||5||<br>

  Who can estimate Your value, O Creator Lord? God has no end or limitation. ||7||<br>
  Please bless Nanak with the glorious greatness of the gift of the Naam, and the dust of the feet of Your Saints. ||8||3||8||22||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 042</h2></center>
  Raamkalee, Third Mehl, Anand ~ The Song Of Bliss:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  I am in ecstasy, O my mother, for I have found my True Guru.<br>
  I have found the True Guru, with intuitive ease, and my mind vibrates with the music of bliss.<br>
  The jewelled melodies and their related celestial harmonies have come to sing the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  The Lord dwells within the minds of those who sing the Shabad.<br>
  Says Nanak, I am in ecstasy, for I have found my True Guru. ||1||<br>
  O my mind, remain always with the Lord.<br>
  Remain always with the Lord, O my mind, and all sufferings will be forgotten.<br>
  He will accept You as His own, and all your affairs will be perfectly arranged.<br>
  Our Lord and Master is all-powerful to do all things, so why forget Him from your mind?<br>
  Says Nanak, O my mind, remain always with the Lord. ||2||<br>
  O my True Lord and Master, what is there which is not in Your celestial home?<br>
  Everything is in Your home; they receive, unto whom You give.<br>
  Constantly singing Your Praises and Glories, Your Name is enshrined in the mind.<br>
  The divine melody of the Shabad vibrates for those, within whose minds the Naam abides.<br>
  Says Nanak, O my True Lord and Master, what is there which is not in Your home? ||3||<br>
  The True Name is my only support.<br>
  The True Name is my only support; it satisfies all hunger.<br>
  It has brought peace and tranquility to my mind; it has fulfilled all my desires.<br>
  I am forever a sacrifice to the Guru, who possesses such glorious greatness.<br>
  Says Nanak, listen, O Saints; enshrine love for the Shabad.<br>
  The True Name is my only support. ||4||<br>
  The Panch Shabad, the five primal sounds, vibrate in that blessed house.<br>
  In that blessed house, the Shabad vibrates; He infuses His almighty power into it.<br>
  Through You, we subdue the five demons of desire, and slay Death, the torturer.<br>
  Those who have such pre-ordained destiny are attached to the Lord's Name.<br>
  Says Nanak, they are at peace, and the unstruck sound current vibrates within their homes. ||5||<br>
  Without the true love of devotion, the body is without honor.<br>
  The body is dishonored without devotional love; what can the poor wretches do?<br>
  No one except You is all-powerful; please bestow Your Mercy, O Lord of all nature.<br>
  There is no place of rest, other than the Name; attached to the Shabad, we are embellished with beauty.<br>
  Says Nanak, without devotional love, what can the poor wretches do? ||6||<br>
  Bliss, bliss - everyone talks of bliss; bliss is known only through the Guru.<br>
  Eternal bliss in known only through the Guru, when the Beloved Lord grants His Grace.<br>
  Granting His Grace, He cuts away our sins; He blesses us with the healing ointment of spiritual wisdom.<br>
  Those who eradicate attachment from within themselves, are adorned with the Shabad, the Word of the True Lord.<br>
  Says Nanak, this alone is bliss - bliss which is known through the Guru. ||7||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 043</h2></center>
  O Baba, he alone receives it, unto whom You give it.<br>
  He alone receives it, unto whom You give it; what can the other poor wretched beings do?<br>
  Some are deluded by doubt, wandering in the ten directions; some are adorned with attachment to the Naam.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, the mind becomes immaculate and pure, for those who follow God's Will.<br>
  Says Nanak, he alone receives it, unto whom You give it, O Beloved Lord. ||8||<br>
  Come, Beloved Saints, let us speak the Unspoken Speech of the Lord.<br>
  How can we speak the Unspoken Speech of the Lord? Through which door will we find Him?<br>
  Surrender body, mind, wealth, and everything to the Guru; obey the Order of His Will, and you will find Him.<br>
  Obey the Hukam of the Guru's Command, and sing the True Word of His Bani.<br>
  Says Nanak, listen, O Saints, and speak the Unspoken Speech of the Lord. ||9||<br>
  O fickle mind, through cleverness, no one has found the Lord.<br>
  Through cleverness, no one has found Him; listen, O my mind.<br>
  This Maya is so fascinating; because of it, people wander in doubt.<br>
  This fascinating Maya was created by the One who has administered this potion.<br>
  I am a sacrifice to the One who has made emotional attachment sweet.<br>
  Says Nanak, O fickle mind, no one has found Him through cleverness. ||10||<br>
  O beloved mind, contemplate the True Lord forever.<br>
  This family which you see shall not go along with you.<br>
  They shall not go along with you, so why do you focus your attention on them?<br>
  Don't do anything that you will regret in the end.<br>
  Listen to the Teachings of the True Guru - these shall go along with you.<br>
  Says Nanak, O beloved mind, contemplate the True Lord forever. ||11||<br>
  O inaccessible and unfathomable Lord, Your limits cannot be found.<br>
  No one has found Your limits; only You Yourself know.<br>
  All living beings and creatures are Your play; how can anyone describe You?<br>
  You speak, and You gaze upon all; You created the Universe.<br>
  Says Nanak, You are forever inaccessible; Your limits cannot be found. ||12||<br>
  The angelic beings and the silent sages search for the Ambrosial Nectar; this Amrit is obtained from the Guru.<br>
  This Amrit is obtained, when the Guru grants His Grace; He enshrines the True Lord within the mind.<br>
  All living beings and creatures were created by You; only some come to see the Guru, and seek His blessing.<br>
  Their greed, avarice and egotism are dispelled, and the True Guru seems sweet.<br>
  Says Nanak, those with whom the Lord is pleased, obtain the Amrit, through the Guru. ||13||<br>
  The lifestyle of the devotees is unique and distinct.<br>
  The devotees' lifestyle is unique and distinct; they follow the most difficult path.<br>
  They renounce greed, avarice, egotism and desire; they do not talk too much.<br>
  The path they take is sharper than a two-edged sword, and finer than a hair.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 044</h2></center>
  By Guru's Grace, they shed their selfishness and conceit; their hopes are merged in the Lord.<br>
  Says Nanak, the lifestyle of the devotees, in each and every age, is unique and distinct. ||14||<br>
  As You make me walk, so do I walk, O my Lord and Master; what else do I know of Your Glorious Virtues?<br>
  As You cause them to walk, they walk - You have placed them on the Path.<br>
  In Your Mercy, You attach them to the Naam; they meditate forever on the Lord, Har, Har.<br>
  Those whom You cause to listen to Your sermon, find peace in the Gurdwara, the Guru's Gate.<br>
  Says Nanak, O my True Lord and Master, you make us walk according to Your Will. ||15||<br>
  This song of praise is the Shabad, the most beautiful Word of God.<br>
  This beauteous Shabad is the everlasting song of praise, spoken by the True Guru.<br>
  This is enshrined in the minds of those who are so pre-destined by the Lord.<br>
  Some wander around, babbling on and on, but none obtain Him by babbling.<br>
  Says Nanak, the Shabad, this song of praise, has been spoken by the True Guru. ||16||<br>
  Those humble beings who meditate on the Lord become pure.<br>
  Meditating on the Lord, they become pure; as Gurmukh, they meditate on Him.<br>
  They are pure, along with their mothers, fathers, family and friends; all their companions are pure as well.<br>
  Pure are those who speak, and pure are those who listen; those who enshrine it within their minds are pure.<br>
  Says Nanak, pure and holy are those who, as Gurmukh, meditate on the Lord, Har, Har. ||17||<br>
  By religious rituals, intuitive poise is not found; without intuitive poise, skepticism does not depart.<br>
  Skepticism does not depart by contrived actions; everybody is tired of performing these rituals.<br>
  The soul is polluted by skepticism; how can it be cleansed?<br>
  Wash your mind by attaching it to the Shabad, and keep your consciousness focused on the Lord.<br>
  Says Nanak, by Guru's Grace, intuitive poise is produced, and this skepticism is dispelled. ||18||<br>
  Inwardly polluted, and outwardly pure.<br>
  Those who are outwardly pure and yet polluted within, lose their lives in the gamble.<br>
  They contract this terrible disease of desire, and in their minds, they forget about dying.<br>
  In the Vedas, the ultimate objective is the Naam, the Name of the Lord; but they do not hear this, and they wander around like demons.<br>
  Says Nanak, those who forsake Truth and cling to falsehood, lose their lives in the gamble. ||19||<br>
  Inwardly pure, and outwardly pure.<br>
  Those who are outwardly pure and also pure within, through the Guru, perform good deeds.<br>
  Not even an iota of falsehood touches them; their hopes are absorbed in the Truth.<br>
  Those who earn the jewel of this human life, are the most excellent of merchants.<br>
  Says Nanak, those whose minds are pure, abide with the Guru forever. ||20||<br>
  If a Sikh turns to the Guru with sincere faith, as sunmukh<br>
  - if a Sikh turns to the Guru with sincere faith, as sunmukh, his soul abides with the Guru.<br>
  Within his heart, he meditates on the lotus feet of the Guru; deep within his soul, he contemplates Him.<br>
  Renouncing selfishness and conceit, he remains always on the side of the Guru; he does not know anyone except the Guru.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 045</h2></center>
  Says Nanak, listen, O Saints: such a Sikh turns toward the Guru with sincere faith, and becomes sunmukh. ||21||<br>
  One who turns away from the Guru, and becomes baymukh - without the True Guru, he shall not find liberation.<br>
  He shall not find liberation anywhere else either; go and ask the wise ones about this.<br>
  He shall wander through countless incarnations; without the True Guru, he shall not find liberation.<br>
  But liberation is attained, when one is attached to the feet of the True Guru, chanting the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  Says Nanak, contemplate this and see, that without the True Guru, there is no liberation. ||22||<br>
  Come, O beloved Sikhs of the True Guru, and sing the True Word of His Bani.<br>
  Sing the Guru's Bani, the supreme Word of Words.<br>
  Those who are blessed by the Lord's Glance of Grace - their hearts are imbued with this Bani.<br>
  Drink in this Ambrosial Nectar, and remain in the Lord's Love forever; meditate on the Lord, the Sustainer of the world.<br>
  Says Nanak, sing this True Bani forever. ||23||<br>
  Without the True Guru, other songs are false.<br>
  The songs are false without the True Guru; all other songs are false.<br>
  The speakers are false, and the listeners are false; those who speak and recite are false.<br>
  They may continually chant, 'Har, Har' with their tongues, but they do not know what they are saying.<br>
  Their consciousness is lured by Maya; they are just reciting mechanically.<br>
  Says Nanak, without the True Guru, other songs are false. ||24||<br>
  The Word of the Guru's Shabad is a jewel, studded with diamonds.<br>
  The mind which is attached to this jewel, merges into the Shabad.<br>
  One whose mind is attuned to the Shabad, enshrines love for the True Lord.<br>
  He Himself is the diamond, and He Himself is the jewel; one who is blessed, understands its value.<br>
  Says Nanak, the Shabad is a jewel, studded with diamonds. ||25||<br>
  He Himself created Shiva and Shakti, mind and matter; the Creator subjects them to His Command.<br>
  Enforcing His Order, He Himself sees all. How rare are those who, as Gurmukh, come to know Him.<br>
  They break their bonds, and attain liberation; they enshrine the Shabad within their minds.<br>
