  Those whom the Lord Himself makes Gurmukh, lovingly focus their consciousness on the One Lord.<br>
  Says Nanak, He Himself is the Creator; He Himself reveals the Hukam of His Command. ||26||<br>
  The Simritees and the Shaastras discriminate between good and evil, but they do not know the true essence of reality.<br>
  They do not know the true essence of reality without the Guru; they do not know the true essence of reality.<br>
  The world is asleep in the three modes and doubt; it passes the night of its life sleeping.<br>
  Those humble beings remain awake and aware, within whose minds, by Guru's Grace, the Lord abides; they chant the Ambrosial Word of the Guru's Bani.<br>
  Says Nanak, they alone obtain the essence of reality, who night and day remain lovingly absorbed in the Lord; they pass the night of their life awake and aware. ||27||<br>
  He nourished us in the mother's womb; why forget Him from the mind?<br>
  Why forget from the mind such a Great Giver, who gave us sustenance in the fire of the womb?<br>
  Nothing can harm one, whom the Lord inspires to embrace His Love.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 046</h2></center>
  He Himself is the love, and He Himself is the embrace; the Gurmukh contemplates Him forever.<br>
  Says Nanak, why forget such a Great Giver from the mind? ||28||<br>
  As is the fire within the womb, so is Maya outside.<br>
  The fire of Maya is one and the same; the Creator has staged this play.<br>
  According to His Will, the child is born, and the family is very pleased.<br>
  Love for the Lord wears off, and the child becomes attached to desires; the script of Maya runs its course.<br>
  This is Maya, by which the Lord is forgotten; emotional attachment and love of duality well up.<br>
  Says Nanak, by Guru's Grace, those who enshrine love for the Lord find Him, in the midst of Maya. ||29||<br>
  The Lord Himself is priceless; His worth cannot be estimated.<br>
  His worth cannot be estimated, even though people have grown weary of trying.<br>
  If you meet such a True Guru, offer your head to Him; your selfishness and conceit will be eradicated from within.<br>
  Your soul belongs to Him; remain united with Him, and the Lord will come to dwell in your mind.<br>
  The Lord Himself is priceless; very fortunate are those, O Nanak, who attain to the Lord. ||30||<br>
  The Lord is my capital; my mind is the merchant.<br>
  The Lord is my capital, and my mind is the merchant; through the True Guru, I know my capital.<br>
  Meditate continually on the Lord, Har, Har, O my soul, and you shall collect your profits daily.<br>
  This wealth is obtained by those who are pleasing to the Lord's Will.<br>
  Says Nanak, the Lord is my capital, and my mind is the merchant. ||31||<br>
  O my tongue, you are engrossed in other tastes, but your thirsty desire is not quenched.<br>
  Your thirst shall not be quenched by any means, until you attain the subtle essence of the Lord.<br>
  If you do obtain the subtle essence of the Lord, and drink in this essence of the Lord, you shall not be troubled by desire again.<br>
  This subtle essence of the Lord is obtained by good karma, when one comes to meet with the True Guru.<br>
  Says Nanak, all other tastes and essences are forgotten, when the Lord comes to dwell within the mind. ||32||<br>
  O my body, the Lord infused His Light into you, and then you came into the world.<br>
  The Lord infused His Light into you, and then you came into the world.<br>
  The Lord Himself is your mother, and He Himself is your father; He created the created beings, and revealed the world to them.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, some understand, and then it's a show; it seems like just a show.<br>
  Says Nanak, He laid the foundation of the Universe, and infused His Light, and then you came into the world. ||33||<br>
  My mind has become joyful, hearing of God's coming.<br>
  Sing the songs of joy to welcome the Lord, O my companions; my household has become the Lord's Mansion.<br>
  Sing continually the songs of joy to welcome the Lord, O my companions, and sorrow and suffering will not afflict you.<br>
  Blessed is that day, when I am attached to the Guru's feet and meditate on my Husband Lord.<br>
  I have come to know the unstruck sound current and the Word of the Guru's Shabad; I enjoy the sublime essence of the Lord, the Lord's Name.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 047</h2></center>
  Says Nanak, God Himself has met me; He is the Doer, the Cause of causes. ||34||<br>
  O my body, why have you come into this world? What actions have you committed?<br>
  And what actions have you committed, O my body, since you came into this world?<br>
  The Lord who formed your form - you have not enshrined that Lord in your mind.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, the Lord abides within the mind, and one's pre-ordained destiny is fulfilled.<br>
  Says Nanak, this body is adorned and honored, when one's consciousness is focused on the True Guru. ||35||<br>
  O my eyes, the Lord has infused His Light into you; do not look upon any other than the Lord.<br>
  Do not look upon any other than the Lord; the Lord alone is worthy of beholding.<br>
  This whole world which you see is the image of the Lord; only the image of the Lord is seen.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, I understand, and I see only the One Lord; there is no one except the Lord.<br>
  Says Nanak, these eyes were blind; but meeting the True Guru, they became all-seeing. ||36||<br>
  O my ears, you were created only to hear the Truth.<br>
  To hear the Truth, you were created and attached to the body; listen to the True Bani.<br>
  Hearing it, the mind and body are rejuvenated, and the tongue is absorbed in Ambrosial Nectar.<br>
  The True Lord is unseen and wondrous; His state cannot be described.<br>
  Says Nanak, listen to the Ambrosial Naam and become holy; you were created only to hear the Truth. ||37||<br>
  The Lord placed the soul to the cave of the body, and blew the breath of life into the musical instrument of the body.<br>
  He blew the breath of life into the musical instrument of the body, and revealed the nine doors; but He kept the Tenth Door hidden.<br>
  Through the Gurdwara, the Guru's Gate, some are blessed with loving faith, and the Tenth Door is revealed to them.<br>
  There are many images of the Lord, and the nine treasures of the Naam; His limits cannot be found.<br>
  Says Nanak, the Lord placed the soul to the cave of the body, and blew the breath of life into the musical instrument of the body. ||38||<br>
  Sing this true song of praise in the true home of your soul.<br>
  Sing the song of praise in your true home; meditate there on the True Lord forever.<br>
  They alone meditate on You, O True Lord, who are pleasing to Your Will; as Gurmukh, they understand.<br>
  This Truth is the Lord and Master of all; whoever is blessed, obtains it.<br>
  Says Nanak, sing the true song of praise in the true home of your soul. ||39||<br>
  Listen to the song of bliss, O most fortunate ones; all your longings shall be fulfilled.<br>
  I have obtained the Supreme Lord God, and all sorrows have been forgotten.<br>
  Pain, illness and suffering have departed, listening to the True Bani.<br>
  The Saints and their friends are in ecstasy, knowing the Perfect Guru.<br>
  Pure are the listeners, and pure are the speakers; the True Guru is all-pervading and permeating.<br>
  Prays Nanak, touching the Guru's Feet, the unstruck sound current of the celestial bugles vibrates and resounds. ||40||1||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 048</h2></center>
  Raamkalee, Sadd ~ The Call Of Death:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  He is the Great Giver of the Universe, the Lover of His devotees, throughout the three worlds.<br>
  One who is merged in the Word of the Guru's Shabad does not know any other.<br>
  Dwelling upon the Word of the Guru's Shabad, he does not know any other; he meditates on the One Name of the Lord.<br>
  By the Grace of Guru Nanak and Guru Angad, Guru Amar Das obtained the supreme status.<br>
  And when the call came for Him to depart, He merged in the Name of the Lord.<br>
  Through devotional worship in this world, the imperishable, immovable, immeasurable Lord is found. ||1||<br>
  The Guru gladly accepted the Lord's Will, and so the Guru easily reached the Lord God's Presence.<br>
  The True Guru prays to the Lord, "Please, save my honor. This is my prayer".<br>
  Please save the honor of Your humble servant, O Lord; please bless him with Your Immaculate Name.<br>
  At this time of final departure, it is our only help and support; it destroys death, and the Messenger of Death.<br>
  The Lord God heard the prayer of the True Guru, and granted His request.<br>
  The Lord showered His Mercy, and blended the True Guru with Himself; He said, "Blessed! Blessed! Wonderful!"||2||<br>
  Listen O my Sikhs, my children and Siblings of Destiny; it is my Lord's Will that I must now go to Him.<br>
  The Guru gladly accepted the Lord's Will, and my Lord God applauded Him.<br>
  One who is pleased with the Lord God's Will is a devotee, the True Guru, the Primal Lord.<br>
  The unstruck sound current of bliss resounds and vibrates; the Lord hugs him close in His embrace.<br>
  O my children, siblings and family, look carefully in your minds, and see.<br>
  The pre-ordained death warrant cannot be avoided; the Guru is going to be with the Lord God. ||3||<br>
  The True Guru, in His Own Sweet Will, sat up and summoned His family.<br>
  Let no one weep for me after I am gone. That would not please me at all.<br>
  When a friend receives a robe of honor, then his friends are pleased with his honor.<br>
  Consider this and see, O my children and siblings; the Lord has given the True Guru the robe of supreme honor.<br>
  The True Guru Himself sat up, and appointed the successor to the Throne of Raja Yoga, the Yoga of Meditation and Success.<br>
  All the Sikhs, relatives, children and siblings have fallen at the Feet of Guru Ram Das. ||4||<br>
  Finally, the True Guru said, "When I am gone, sing Kirtan in Praise of the Lord, in Nirvaanaa."<br>
  Call in the long-haired scholarly Saints of the Lord, to read the sermon of the Lord, Har, Har.<br>
  Read the sermon of the Lord, and listen to the Lord's Name; the Guru is pleased with love for the Lord.<br>
  Do not bother with offering rice-balls on leaves, lighting lamps, and other rituals like floating the body out on the Ganges; instead, let my remains be given up to the Lord's Pool.<br>
  The Lord was pleased as the True Guru spoke; he was blended then with the all-knowing Primal Lord God.<br>
  The Guru then blessed the Sodhi Ram Das with the ceremonial tilak mark, the insignia of the True Word of the Shabad. ||5||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 049</h2></center>
  And as the True Guru, the Primal Lord spoke, and the Gursikhs obeyed His Will.<br>
  His son Mohri turned sunmukh, and become obedient to Him; he bowed, and touched Ram Das' feet.<br>
  Then, everyone bowed and touched the feet of Ram Das, into whom the Guru infused His essence.<br>
  And any that did not bow then because of envy - later, the True Guru brought them around to bow in humility.<br>
  It pleased the Guru, the Lord, to bestow glorious greatness upon Him; such was the pre-ordained destiny of the Lord's Will.<br>
  Says Sundar, listen, O Saints: all the world fell at His feet. ||6||1||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl, Chhant:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Friend, my Friend - standing so near to me is my Friend!<br>
  Beloved, the Lord my Beloved - with my eyes, I have seen the Lord, my Beloved!<br>
  With my eyes I have seen Him, sleeping upon the bed within each and every heart; my Beloved is the sweetest ambrosial nectar.<br>
  He is with all, but he cannot be found; the fool does not know His taste.<br>
  Intoxicated with the wine of Maya, the mortal babbles on about trivial affairs; giving in to the illusion, he cannot meet the Lord.<br>
  Says Nanak, without the Guru, he cannot understand the Lord, the Friend who is standing near everyone. ||1||<br>
  God, my God - the Support of the breath of life is my God.<br>
  Merciful Lord, my Merciful Lord - the Giver of gifts is my Merciful Lord.<br>
  The Giver of gifts is infinite and unlimited; deep within each and every heart, He is so beautiful!<br>
  He created Maya, His slave, so powerfully pervasive - she has enticed all beings and creatures.<br>
  One whom the Lord saves, chants the True Name, and contemplates the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  Says Nanak, one who is pleasing to God - God is very dear to him. ||2||<br>
  I take pride, I take pride in God; I take pride in my God.<br>
  Wise, God is wise; my Lord and Master is all-wise, and all-knowing.<br>
  All-wise and all-knowing, and forever supreme; the Name of the Lord is Ambrosial Nectar.<br>
  Those who have such pre-ordained destiny recorded upon their foreheads, taste it, and are satisfied with the Lord of the Universe.<br>
  They meditate on Him, and find Him; they place all their pride in Him.<br>
  Says Nanak, He is seated on His eternal throne; True is His royal court. ||3||<br>
  The song of joy, the Lord's song of joy; listen to the song of joy of my God.<br>
  The wedding song, God's wedding song; the unstruck sound current of His wedding song resounds.<br>
  The unstruck sound current vibrates, and the Word of the Shabad resounds; there is continuous, continual rejoicing.<br>
  Meditating on that God, everything is obtained; He does not die, or come or go.<br>
  Thirst is quenched, and hopes are fulfilled; the Gurmukh meets with the absolute, unmanifest Lord.<br>
  Says Nanak, in the Home of my God, the songs of joy are continuously, continually heard. ||4||1||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 050</h2></center>
  Raamkalee Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Meditate on the Lord, Har, Har, O mind; don't forget Him, even for an instant.<br>
  Enshrine the Lord, Raam, Raam, Raam, Raam, within your heart and throat.<br>
  Enshrine within your heart the Primal Lord, Har, Har, the all-pervading, supreme, immaculate Lord God.<br>
  He sends fear far away; He is the Destroyer of sin; He eradicates the unbearable pains of the terrifying world-ocean.<br>
  Contemplate the Lord of the World, the Cherisher of the World, the Lord, the Virtuous Lord of the Universe.<br>
  Prays Nanak, joining the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy, remember the Lord, day and night. ||1||<br>
  His lotus feet are the support and anchor of His humble servants.<br>
  He takes the Naam, the Name of the Infinite Lord, as his wealth, property and treasure.<br>
  Those who have the treasure of the Lord's Name, enjoy the taste of the One Lord.<br>
  They meditate on the Infinite Lord with each and every breath, as their pleasure, joy and beauty.<br>
  The Naam, the Name of the Lord, is the Destroyer of sins, the only deed of redemption. The Naam drives out the fear of the Messenger of Death.<br>
  Prays Nanak, the support of His lotus feet is the capital of His humble servant. ||2||<br>
  Your Glorious Virtues are endless, O my Lord and Master; no one knows them all.<br>
  Seeing and hearing of Your wondrous plays, O Merciful Lord, Your devotees narrate them.<br>
  All beings and creatures meditate on You, O Primal Transcendent Lord, Master of men.<br>
  All beings are beggars; You are the One Giver, O Lord of the Universe, Embodiment of mercy.<br>
  He alone is holy, a Saint, a truly wise person, who is accepted by the Dear Lord.<br>
  Prays Nanak, they alone realize You, unto whom You show Mercy. ||3||<br>
  I am unworthy and without any master; I seek Your Sanctuary, Lord.<br>
  I am a sacrifice, a sacrifice, a sacrifice to the Divine Guru, who has implanted the Naam within me.<br>
  The Guru blessed me with the Naam; happiness came, and all my desires were fulfilled.<br>
  The fire of desire has been quenched, and peace and tranquility have come; after such a long separation, I have met my Lord again.<br>
  I have found ecstasy, pleasure and true intuitive poise, singing the great glories, the song of bliss of the Lord.<br>
  Prays Nanak, I have obtained the Name of God from the Perfect Guru. ||4||2||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Rise early each morning, and with the Saints, sing the melodious harmony, the unstruck sound current of the Shabad.<br>
  All sins and sufferings are erased, chanting the Lord's Name, under Guru's Instructions.<br>
  Dwell upon the Lord's Name, and drink in the Nectar; day and night, worship and adore Him.<br>
  The merits of Yoga, charity and religious rituals are obtained by grasping His lotus feet.<br>
  Loving devotion to the merciful, enticing Lord takes away all pain.<br>
  Prays Nanak, cross over the world-ocean, meditating on the Lord, your Lord and Master. ||1||<br>
  Meditation on the Lord of the Universe is an ocean of peace; Your devotees sing Your Glorious Praises, Lord.<br>
  Ecstasy, bliss and great happiness are obtained by grasping hold of the Guru's feet.<br>
  Meeting with the treasure of peace, their pains are taken away; granting His Grace, God protects them.<br>
  Those who grasp the Lord's feet - their fears and doubts run away, and they chant the Name of the Lord.<br>
  He thinks of the One Lord, and he sings of the One God; he gazes upon the One Lord alone.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 051</h2></center>
  Prays Nanak, God has granted His Grace, and I have found the Perfect True Guru. ||2||<br>
  Meet with the holy, humble servants of God; meeting with the Lord, listen to the Kirtan of His Praises.<br>
  God is the Merciful Master, the Lord of wealth; there is no end to His Virtues.<br>
  The Merciful Lord is the Dispeller of pain, the Giver of Sanctuary, the Eradicator of all evil.<br>
  Emotional attachment, sorrow, corruption and pain - chanting the Naam, the Name of the Lord, one is saved from these.<br>
  All beings are Yours, O my God; bless me with Your Mercy, that I may become the dust under the feet of all men.<br>
  Prays Nanak, O God, be kind to me, that I may chant Your Name, and live. ||3||<br>
  God saves His humble devotees, attaching them to His feet.<br>
  Twenty-four hours a day, they meditate in remembrance on their God; they meditae on the One Name.<br>
  Meditating on that God, they cross over the terrifying world-ocean, and their comings and goings cease.<br>
  They enjoy eternal peace and pleasure, singing the Kirtan of God's Praises; His Will seems so sweet to them.<br>
  All my desires are fulfilled, meeting with the Perfect True Guru.<br>
  Prays Nanak, God has blended me with Himself; I shall never suffer pain or sorrow again. ||4||3||<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl, Chhant.<br>
  Shalok:<br>
  In the Sanctuary of His lotus feet, I sing His Glorious Praises in ecstasy and bliss.<br>
  O Nanak, worship God in adoration, the Eradicator of misfortune. ||1||<br>
  Chhant:<br>
  God is the Eradicator of misfortune; there is none other than Him.<br>
  Forever and ever, remember the Lord in meditation; He is permeating the water, the land and the sky.<br>
  He is permeating and pervading the water, the land and the sky; do not forget Him from your mind, even for an instant.<br>
  Blessed was that day, when I grasped the Guru's feet; all virtues rest in the Lord of the Universe.<br>
  So serve Him day and night, O servant; whatever pleases Him, happens.<br>
  Nanak is a sacrifice to the Giver of peace; his mind and body are enlightened. ||1||<br>
  Shalok:<br>
  Meditating in remembrance on the Lord, the mind and body find peace; the thought of duality is dispelled.<br>
  Nanak takes the support of the Lord of the World, the Lord of the Universe, the Destroyer of troubles. ||1||<br>
  Chhant:<br>
  The Merciful Lord has eradicated my fears and troubles.<br>
  In ecstasy, I sing the Glorious Praises of the Lord; God is the Cherisher, the Master of the meek.<br>
  The Cherishing Lord is imperishable, the One and only Primal Lord; I am imbued with His Love.<br>
  When I placed my hands and forehead upon His Feet, He blended me with Himself; I became awake and aware forever, night and day.<br>
  My soul, body, household and home belong to Him, along with my body, youth, wealth and property.<br>
  Forever and ever, Nanak is a sacrifice to Him, who cherishes and nurtures all beings. ||2||<br>
  Shalok:<br>
  My tongue chants the Name of the Lord, and chants the Glorious Praises of the Lord of the Universe.<br>
  Nanak has grasped the sheltering support of the One Transcendent Lord, who shall save him in the end. ||1||<br>
  Chhant:<br>
  He is God, our Lord and Master, our Saving Grace. Grab hold of the hem of His robe.<br>
  Vibrate, and meditate on the Merciful Divine Lord in the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy; renounce your intellectual mind.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 052</h2></center>
  Seek the Support of the One Lord, and surrender your soul to Him; place your hopes only in the Sustainer of the World.<br>
  Those who are imbued with the Lord's Name, in the Saadh Sangat, cross over the terrifying world-ocean.<br>
  The corrupting sins of birth and death are eradicated, and no stain ever sticks to them again.<br>
  Nanak is a sacrifice to the Perfect Primal Lord; His marriage is eternal. ||3||<br>
  Shalok:<br>
  Righteous faith, wealth, sexual success and salvation; the Lord bestows these four blessings.<br>
  One who has such pre-ordained destiny upon his forehead, O Nanak, has all his desires fulfilled. ||1||<br>
  Chhant:<br>
  All my desires are fulfilled, meeting with my Immaculate, Sovereign Lord.<br>
  I am in ecstasy, O very fortunate ones; the Dear Lord has become manifest in my own home.<br>
  My Beloved has come to my home, because of my past actions; how can I count His Glories?<br>
  The Lord, the Giver of peace and intuition, is infinite and perfect; with what tongue can I describe His Glorious Virtues?<br>
  He hugs me close in His embrace, and merges me into Himself; there is no place of rest other than Him.<br>
  Nanak is forever a sacrifice to the Creator, who is contained in, and permeating all. ||4||4||<br>
  Raag Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Sing the melodious harmonies, O my companions, and meditate on the One Lord.<br>
  Serve your True Guru, O my companions, and you shall obtain the fruits of your mind's desires.<br>
  Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl, Ruti ~ The Seasons. Shalok:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Bow to the Supreme Lord God, and seek the dust of the feet of the Holy.<br>
  Cast out your self-conceit, and vibrate, meditate, on the Lord, Har, Har. O Nanak, God is all-pervading. ||1||<br>
  He is the Eradicator of sins, the Destroyer of fear, the Ocean of peace, the Sovereign Lord King.<br>
  Merciful to the meek, the Destroyer of pain: O Nanak, always meditate on Him. ||2||<br>
  Chhant:<br>
  Sing His Praises, O very fortunate ones, and the Dear Lord God shall bless you with His Mercy.<br>
  Blessed and auspicious is that season, that month, that moment, that hour, when you chant the Lord's Glorious Praises.<br>
  Blessed are those humble beings, who are imbued with love for His Praises, and who meditate single-mindedly on Him.<br>
  Their lives become fruitful, and they find that Lord God.<br>
  Donations to charities and religious rituals are not equal to meditation on the Lord, who destroys all sins.<br>
  Prays Nanak, meditating in remembrance on Him, I live; birth and death are finished for me. ||1||<br>
  Shalok:<br>
  Strive for the inaccessible and unfathomable Lord, and bow in humility to His lotus feet.<br>
  O Nanak, that sermon alone is pleasing to You, Lord, which inspires us to take the Support of the Name. ||1||<br>
  Seek the Sanctuary of the Saints, O friends; meditate in remembrance on your infinite Lord and Master.<br>
  The dried branch shall blossom forth in its greenery again, O Nanak, meditating on the Lord God. ||2||<br>
  Chhant:<br>
  The season of spring is delightful; the months of Chayt and Baisaakhi are the most pleasant months.<br>
  I have obtained the Dear Lord as my Husband, and my mind, body and breath have blossomed forth.<br>
  The eternal, unchanging Lord has come into my home as my Husband, O my companions; dwelling upon His lotus feet, I blossom forth in bliss.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 053</h2></center>
  The Lord of the Universe is beautiful, proficient, wise and all-knowing;<br>
  His Virtues are priceless. By great good fortune, I have found Him; my pain is dispelled, and my hopes are fulfilled.<br>
  Prays Nanak, I have entered Your Sanctuary, Lord, and my fear of death is eradicated. ||2||<br>
  Shalok:<br>
  Without the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy, one dies wandering around in confusion, performing all sorts of rituals.<br>
  O Nanak, all are bound by the attractive bonds of Maya, and the karmic record of past actions. ||1||<br>
  Those who are pleasing to God are united with Him; He separates others from Himself.<br>
  Nanak has entered the Sanctuary of God; His greatness is glorious! ||2||<br>
  Chhant:<br>
  In the summer season, in the months of Jayt'h and Asaarh, the heat is terrible, intense and severe.<br>
  The discarded bride is separated from His Love, and the Lord does not even look at her.<br>
  She does not see her Lord, and she dies with an aching sigh; she is defrauded and plundered by her great pride.<br>
  She flails around, like a fish out of water; attached to Maya, she is alienated from the Lord.<br>
  She sins, and so she is fearful of reincarnation; the Messenger of Death will surely punish her.<br>
  Prays Nanak, take me under Your sheltering support, Lord, and protect me; You are the Fulfiller of desire. ||3||<br>
  Shalok:<br>
  With loving faith, I am attached to my Beloved; I cannot survive without Him, even for an instant.<br>
  He is permeating and pervading my mind and body, O Nanak, with intuitive ease. ||1||<br>
  My Friend has taken me by the hand; He has been my best friend, lifetime after lifetime.<br>
  He has made me the slave of His feet; O Nanak, my consciousness is filled with love for God. ||2||<br>
  Chhant:<br>
  The rainy season is beautiful; the months of Saawan and Bhaadon bring bliss.<br>
  The clouds are low, and heavy with rain; the waters and the lands are filled with honey.<br>
  God is all-pervading everywhere; the nine treasures of the Lord's Name fill the homes of all hearts.<br>
  Meditating in remembrance on the Lord and Master, the Searcher of hearts, all one's ancestry is saved.<br>
  No blemish sticks to that being who remains awake and aware in the Love of the Lord; the Merciful Lord is forever forgiving.<br>
  Prays Nanak, I have found my Husband Lord, who is forever pleasing to my mind. ||4||<br>
  Shalok:<br>
  Thirsty with desire, I wander around; when will I behold the Lord of the World?<br>
  Is there any humble Saint, any friend, O Nanak, who can lead me to meet with God? ||1||<br>
  Without meeting Him, I have no peace or tranquility; I cannot survive for a moment, even for an instant.<br>
  Entering the Sanctuary of the Lord's Holy Saints, O Nanak, my desires are fulfilled. ||2||<br>
  Chhant:<br>
  In the cool, autumn season, in the months of Assu and Katik, I am thirsty for the Lord.<br>
  Searching for the Blessed Vision of His Darshan, I wander around wondering, when will I meet my Lord, the treasure of virtue?<br>
  Without my Beloved Husband Lord, I find no peace, and all my necklaces and bracelets become cursed.<br>
  So beautiful, so wise, so clever and knowing; still, without the breath, it is just a body.<br>
  I look here and there, in the ten directions; my mind is so thirsty to meet God!<br>
  Prays Nanak, shower Your Mercy upon me; unite me with Yourself, O God, O treasure of virtue. ||5||<br>
  Shalok:<br>
  The fire of desire is cooled and quenched; my mind and body are filled with peace and tranquility.<br>
  O Nanak, I have met my Perfect God; the illusion of duality is dispelled. ||1||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 054</h2></center>
  The Lord Himself sent His Holy Saints, to tell us that He is not far away.<br>
  O Nanak, doubt and fear are dispelled, chanting the Name of the all-pervading Lord. ||2||<br>
  Chhant:<br>
  In the cold season of Maghar and Poh, the Lord reveals Himself.<br>
  My burning desires were quenched, when I obtained the Blessed Vision of His Darshan; the fraudulent illusion of Maya is gone.<br>
  All my desires have been fulfilled, meeting the Lord face-to-face; I am His servant, I serve at His feet.<br>
  My necklaces, hair-ties, all decorations and adornments, are in singing the Glorious Praises of the unseen, mysterious Lord.<br>
  I long for loving devotion to the Lord of the Universe, and so the Messenger of Death cannot even see me.<br>
  Prays Nanak, God has united me with Himself; I shall never suffer separation from my Beloved again. ||6||<br>
  Shalok:<br>
  The happy soul bride has found the wealth of the Lord; her consciousness does not waver.<br>
  Joining together with the Saints, O Nanak, God, my Friend, has revealed Himself in my home. ||1||<br>
  With her Beloved Husband Lord, she enjoys millions of melodies, pleasures and joys.<br>
  The fruits of the mind's desires are obtained, O Nanak, chanting the Lord's Name. ||2||<br>
  Chhant:<br>
  The snowy winter season, the months of Maagh and Phagun, are pleasing and ennobling to the mind.<br>
  O my friends and companions, sing the songs of joy; my Husband Lord has come into my home.<br>
  My Beloved has come into my home; I meditate on Him in my mind. The bed of my heart is beautifully adorned.<br>
  The woods, the meadows and the three worlds have blossomed forth in their greenery; gazing upon the Blessed Vision of His Darshan, I am fascinated.<br>
  I have met my Lord and Master, and my desires are fulfilled; my mind chants His Immaculate Mantra.<br>
  Prays Nanak, I celebrate continuously; I have met my Husband Lord, the Lord of excellence. ||7||<br>
  Shalok:<br>
  The Saints are the helpers, the support of the soul; they carry us cross the terrifying world-ocean.<br>
  Know that they are the highest of all; O Nanak, they love the Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||1||<br>
  Those who know Him, cross over; they are the brave heroes, the heroic warriors.<br>
  Nanak is a sacrifice to those who meditate on the Lord, and cross over to the other shore. ||2||<br>
  Chhant:<br>
  His feet are exalted above all. They eradicate all suffering.<br>
  They destroy the pains of coming and going. They bring loving devotion to the Lord.<br>
  Imbued with the Lord's Love, one is intoxicated with intuitive peace and poise, and does not forget the Lord from his mind, even for an instant.<br>
  Shedding my self-conceit, I have entered the Sanctuary of His Feet; all virtues rest in the Lord of the Universe.<br>
  I bow in humility to the Lord of the Universe, the treasure of virtue, the Lord of excellence, our Primal Lord and Master.<br>
  Prays Nanak, shower me with Your Mercy, Lord; throughout the ages, You take the same form. ||8||1||6||8||<br>
  Raamkalee, First Mehl, Dakhanee, Ongkaar:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  From Ongkaar, the One Universal Creator God, Brahma was created.<br>
  He kept Ongkaar in his consciousness.<br>
  From Ongkaar, the mountains and the ages were created.<br>
  Ongkaar created the Vedas.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 055</h2></center>
  Ongkaar saves the world through the Shabad.<br>
  Ongkaar saves the Gurmukhs.<br>
  Listen to the Message of the Universal, Imperishable Creator Lord.<br>
  The Universal, Imperishable Creator Lord is the essence of the three worlds. ||1||<br>
  Listen, O Pandit, O religious scholar, why are you writing about worldly debates?<br>
  As Gurmukh, write only the Name of the Lord, the Lord of the World. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Sassa: He created the entire universe with ease; His One Light pervades the three worlds.<br>
  Become Gurmukh, and obtain the real thing; gather the gems and pearls.<br>
  If one understands, realizes and comprehends what he reads and studies, in the end he shall realize that the True Lord dwells deep within his nucleus.<br>
  The Gurmukh sees and contemplates the True Lord; without the True Lord, the world is false. ||2||<br>
  Dhadha: Those who enshrine Dharmic faith and dwell in the City of Dharma are worthy; their minds are steadfast and stable.<br>
  Dhadha: If the dust of their feet touches one's face and forehead, he is transformed from iron into gold.<br>
  Blessed is the Support of the Earth; He Himself is not born; His measure and speech are perfect and True.<br>
  Only the Creator Himself knows His own extent; He alone knows the Brave Guru. ||3||<br>
  In love with duality, spiritual wisdom is lost; the mortal rots away in pride, and eats poison.<br>
  He thinks that the sublime essence of the Guru's song is useless, and he does not like to hear it. He loses the profound, unfathomable Lord.<br>
  Through the Guru's Words of Truth, the Ambrosial Nectar is obtained, and the mind and body find joy in the True Lord.<br>
  He Himself is the Gurmukh, and He Himself bestows the Ambrosial Nectar; He Himself leads us to drink it in. ||4||<br>
  Everyone says that God is the One and only, but they are engrossed in egotism and pride.<br>
  Realize that the One God is inside and outside; understand this, that the Mansion of His Presence is within the home of your heart.<br>
  God is near at hand; do not think that God is far away. The One Lord permeates the entire universe.<br>
  There in One Universal Creator Lord; there is no other at all. O Nanak, merge into the One Lord. ||5||<br>
  How can you keep the Creator under your control? He cannot be seized or measured.<br>
  Maya has made the mortal insane; she has administered the poisonous drug of falsehood.<br>
  Addicted to greed and avarice, the mortal is ruined, and then later, he regrets and repents.<br>
  So serve the One Lord, and attain the state of Salvation; your comings and goings shall cease. ||6||<br>
  The One Lord is in all actions, colors and forms.<br>
  He manifests in many shapes through wind, water and fire.<br>
  The One Soul wanders through the three worlds.<br>
  One who understands and comprehends the One Lord is honored.<br>
  One who gathers in spiritual wisdom and meditation, dwells in the state of balance.<br>
  How rare are those who, as Gurmukh, attain the One Lord.<br>
  They alone find peace, whom the Lord blesses with His Grace.<br>
  In the Gurdwara, the Guru's Door, they speak and hear of the Lord. ||7||<br>
  His Light illuminates the ocean and the earth.<br>
  Throughout the three worlds, is the Guru, the Lord of the World.<br>
  The Lord reveals His various forms;<br>
  granting His Grace, He enters the home of the heart.<br>
  The clouds hang low, and the rain is pouring down.<br>
  The Lord embellishes and exalts with the Sublime Word of the Shabad.<br>
  One who knows the mystery of the One God,<br>
  is Himself the Creator, Himself the Divine Lord. ||8||<br>
  When the sun rises, the demons are slain;<br>
  the mortal looks upwards, and contemplates the Shabad.<br>
  The Lord is beyond the beginning and the end, beyond the three worlds.<br>
  He Himself acts, speaks and listens.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 056</h2></center>
  He is the Architect of Destiny; He blesses us with mind and body.<br>
  That Architect of Destiny is in my mind and mouth.<br>
  God is the Life of the world; there is no other at all.<br>
  O Nanak, imbued with the Naam, the Name of the Lord, one is honored. ||9||<br>
  One who lovingly chants the Name of the Sovereign Lord King,<br>
  fights the battle and conquers his own mind;<br>
  day and night, he remains imbued with the Lord's Love.<br>
  He is famous throughout the three worlds and the four ages.<br>
  One who knows the Lord, becomes like Him.<br>
  He becomes absolutely immaculate, and his body is sanctified.<br>
  His heart is happy, in love with the One Lord.<br>
  He lovingly centers his attention deep within upon the True Word of the Shabad. ||10||<br>
  Don't be angry - drink in the Ambrosial Nectar; you shall not remain in this world forever.<br>
  The ruling kings and the paupers shall not remain; they come and go, throughout the four ages.<br>
  Everyone says that they will remain, but none of them remain; unto whom should I offer my prayer?<br>
  The One Shabad, the Name of the Lord, will never fail you; the Guru grants honor and understanding. ||11||<br>
  My shyness and hesitation have died and gone, and I walk with my face unveiled.<br>
  The confusion and doubt from my crazy, insane mother-in-law has been removed from over my head.<br>
  My Beloved has summoned me with joyful caresses; my mind is filled with the bliss of the Shabad.<br>
  Imbued with the Love of my Beloved, I have become Gurmukh, and carefree. ||12||<br>
  Chant the jewel of the Naam, and earn the profit of the Lord.<br>
  Greed, avarice, evil and egotism;<br>
  slander, inuendo and gossip;<br>
  the self-willed manmukh is blind, foolish and ignorant.<br>
  For the sake of earning the profit of the Lord, the mortal comes into the world.<br>
  But he becomes a mere slave laborer, and is mugged by the mugger, Maya.<br>
  One who earns the profit of the Naam, with the capital of faith,<br>
  O Nanak, is truly honored by the True Supreme King. ||13||<br>
  The world is ruined on the path of Death.<br>
  No one has the power to erase Maya's influence.<br>
  If wealth visits the home of the lowliest clown,<br>
  seeing that wealth, all pay their respects to him.<br>
  Even an idiot is thought of as clever, if he is rich.<br>
  Without devotional worship, the world is insane.<br>
  The One Lord is contained among all.<br>
  He reveals Himself, unto those whom He blesses with His Grace. ||14||<br>
  Throughout the ages, the Lord is eternally established; He has no vengeance.<br>
  He is not subject to birth and death; He is not entangled in worldly affairs.<br>
  Whatever is seen, is the Lord Himself.<br>
  Creating Himself, He establishes Himself in the heart.<br>
  He Himself is unfathomable; He links people to their affairs.<br>
  He is the Way of Yoga, the Life of the World.<br>
  Living a righteous lifestyle, true peace is found.<br>
  Without the Naam, the Name of the Lord, how can anyone find liberation? ||15||<br>
  Without the Name, even one's own body is an enemy.<br>
  Why not meet the Lord, and take away the pain of your mind?<br>
  The traveller comes and goes along the highway.<br>
  What did he bring when he came, and what will he take away when he goes?<br>
  Without the Name, one loses everywhere.<br>
  The profit is earned, when the Lord grants understanding.<br>
  In merchandise and trade, the merchant is trading.<br>
  Without the Name, how can one find honor and nobility? ||16||<br>
  One who contemplates the Lord's Virtues is spiritually wise.<br>
  Through His Virtues, one receives spiritual wisdom.<br>
  How rare in this world, is the Giver of virtue.<br>
  The True way of life comes through contemplation of the Guru.<br>
  The Lord is inaccessible and unfathomable. His worth cannot be estimated.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 057</h2></center>
  They alone meet Him, whom the Lord causes to meet.<br>
  The virtuous soul bride continually contemplates His Virtues.<br>
  O Nanak, following the Guru's Teachings, one meets the Lord, the true friend. ||17||<br>
  Unfulfilled sexual desire and unresolved anger waste the body away,<br>
  as gold is dissolved by borax.<br>
  The gold is touched to the touchstone, and tested by fire;<br>
  when its pure color shows through, it is pleasing to the eye of the assayer.<br>
  The world is a beast, and arrogent Death is the butcher.<br>
  The created beings of the Creator receive the karma of their actions.<br>
  He who created the world, knows its worth.<br>
  What else can be said? There is nothing at all to say. ||18||<br>
  Searching, searching, I drink in the Ambrosial Nectar.<br>
  I have adopted the way of tolerance, and given my mind to the True Guru.<br>
  Everyone calls himself true and genuine.<br>
  He alone is true, who obtains the jewel throughout the four ages.<br>
  Eating and drinking, one dies, but still does not know.<br>
  He dies in an instant, when he realizes the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  His consciousness becomes permanently stable, and his mind accepts death.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, he realizes the Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||19||<br>
  The Profound Lord dwells in the sky of the mind, the Tenth Gate;<br>
  singing His Glorious Praises, one dwells in intuitive poise and peace.<br>
  He does not go to come, or come to go.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, he remains lovingly focused on the Lord.<br>
  The Lord of the mind-sky is inaccessible, independent and beyond birth.<br>
  The most worthy Samaadhi is to keep the consciousness stable, focused on Him.<br>
  Remembering the Lord's Name, one is not subject to reincarnation.<br>
  The Guru's Teachings are the most Excellent; all other ways lack the Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||20||<br>
  Wandering to countless doorsteps and homes, I have grown weary.<br>
  My incarnations are countless, without limit.<br>
  I have had so many mothers and fathers, sons and daughters.<br>
  I have had so many gurus and disciples.<br>
  Through a false guru, liberation is not found.<br>
  There are so many brides of the One Husband Lord - consider this.<br>
  The Gurmukh dies, and lives with God.<br>
  Searching in the ten directions, I found Him within my own home.<br>
  I have met Him; the True Guru has led me to meet Him. ||21||<br>
  The Gurmukh sings, and the Gurmukh speaks.<br>
  The Gurmukh evaluates the value of the Lord, and inspires others to evaluate Him as well.<br>
  The Gurmukh comes and goes without fear.<br>
  His filth is taken away, and his stains are burnt off.<br>
  The Gurmukh contemplates the sound current of the Naad for his Vedas.<br>
  The Gurmukh's cleansing bath is the performance of good deeds.<br>
  For the Gurmukh, the Shabad is the most excellent Ambrosial Nectar.<br>
  O Nanak, the Gurmukh crosses over. ||22||<br>
  The fickle consciousness does not remain stable.<br>
  The deer secretly nibbles at the green sprouts.<br>
  One who enshrines the Lord's lotus feet in his heart and consciousness<br>
  lives long, always remembering the Lord.<br>
  Everyone has worries and cares.<br>
  He alone finds peace, who thinks of the One Lord.<br>
  When the Lord dwells in the consciousness, and one is absorbed in the Lord's Name,<br>
  one is liberated, and returns home with honor. ||23||<br>
  The body falls apart, when one knot is untied.<br>
  Behold, the world is on the decline; it will be totally destroyed.<br>
  Only one who looks alike upon sunshine and shade<br>
  has his bonds shattered; he is liberated and returns home.<br>
  Maya is empty and petty; she has defrauded the world.<br>
  Such destiny is pre-ordained by past actions.<br>
  Youth is wasting away; old age and death hover above the head.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 058</h2></center>
  The body falls apart, like algae upon the water. ||24||<br>
  God Himself appears throughout the three worlds.<br>
  Throughout the ages, He is the Great Giver; there is no other at all.<br>
  As it pleases You, You protect and preserve us.<br>
  I ask for the Lord's Praises, which bless me with honor and credit.<br>
  Remaining awake and aware, I am pleasing to You, O Lord.<br>
  When You unite me with Yourself, then I am merged in You.<br>
  I chant Your Victorious Praises, O Life of the World.<br>
  Accepting the Guru's Teachings, one is sure to merge in the One Lord. ||25||<br>
  Why do you speak such nonsense, and argue with the world?<br>
  You shall die repenting, when you see your own insanity.<br>
  He is born, only to die, but he does not wish to live.<br>
  He comes hopeful, and then goes, without hope.<br>
  Regretting, repenting and grieving, he is dust mixing with dust.<br>
  Death does not chew up one who sings the Glorious Praises of the Lord.<br>
  The nine treasures are obtained through the Name of the Lord;<br>
  the Lord bestows intuitive peace and poise. ||26||<br>
  He speaks spiritual wisdom, and He Himself understands it.<br>
  He Himself knows it, and He Himself comprehends it.<br>
  One who takes the Words of the Guru into his very fiber,<br>
  is immaculate and holy, and is pleasing to the True Lord.<br>
  In the ocean of the Guru, there is no shortage of pearls.<br>
  The treasure of jewels is truly inexhaustible.<br>
  Do those deeds which the Guru has ordained.<br>
  Why are you chasing after the Guru's actions?<br>
  O Nanak, through the Guru's Teachings, merge in the True Lord. ||27||<br>
  Love is broken, when one speaks in defiance.<br>
  The arm is broken, when it is pulled from both sides.<br>
  Love breaks, when the speech goes sour.<br>
  The Husband Lord abandons and leaves behind the evil-minded bride.<br>
  The broken knot is tied again, through contemplation and meditation.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, one's affairs are resolved in one's own home.<br>
  One who earns the profit of the True Name, will not lose it again;<br>
  the Lord and Master of the three worlds is your best friend. ||28||<br>
  Control your mind, and keep it in its place.<br>
  The world is destroyed by conflict, regretting its sinful mistakes.<br>
  There is one Husband Lord, and all are His brides.<br>
  The false bride wears many costumes.<br>
  He stops her from going into the homes of others;<br>
  He summons her to the Mansion of His Presence, and no obstacles block her path.<br>
  She is embellished with the Word of the Shabad, and is loved by the True Lord.<br>
  She is the happy soul bride, who takes the Support of her Lord and Master. ||29||<br>
  Wandering and roaming around, O my companion, your beautiful robes are torn.<br>
  In jealousy, the body is not at peace; without the Fear of God, multitudes are ruined.<br>
  One who remains dead within her own home, through the Fear of God, is looked upon with favor by her all-knowing Husband Lord.<br>
  She maintains fear of her Guru, and chants the Name of the Fearless Lord.<br>
  Living on the mountain, I suffer such great thirst; when I see Him, I know that He is not far away.<br>
  My thirst is quenched, and I have accepted the Word of the Shabad. I drink my fill of the Ambrosial Nectar.<br>
  Everyone says, "Give! Give!" As He pleases, He gives.<br>
  Through the Gurdwara, the Guru's Door, He gives, and quenches the thirst. ||30||<br>
  Searching and seeking, I fell down and collapsed upon the bank of the river of life.<br>
  Those who are heavy with sin sink down, but those who are light swim across.<br>
  I am a sacrifice to those who meet the immortal and immeasurable Lord.<br>
  The dust of their feet brings emancipation; in their company, we are united in the Lord's Union.<br>
  I gave my mind to my Guru, and received the Immaculate Name.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 059</h2></center>
  I serve the One who gave me the Naam; I am a sacrifice to Him.<br>
  He who builds, also demolishes; there is no other than Him.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, I contemplate Him, and then my body does not suffer in pain. ||31||<br>
  No one is mine - whose gown should I grasp and hold? No one ever was, and no one shall ever be mine.<br>
  Coming and going, one is ruined, afflicted with the disease of dual-mindedness.<br>
  Those beings who lack the Naam, the Name of the Lord, collapse like pillars of salt.<br>
  Without the Name, how can they find release? They fall into hell in the end.<br>
  Using a limited number of words, we describe the unlimited True Lord.<br>
  The ignorant lack understanding. Without the Guru, there is no spiritual wisdom.<br>
  The separated soul is like the broken string of a guitar, which does not vibrate its sound.<br>
  God unites the separated souls with Himself, awakening their destiny. ||32||<br>
  The body is the tree, and the mind is the bird; the birds in the tree are the five senses.<br>
  They peck at the essence of reality, and merge with the One Lord. They are never trapped at all.<br>
  But the others fly away in a hurry, when they see the food.<br>
  Their feathers are clipped, and they are caught in the noose; through their mistakes, they are caught in disaster.<br>
  Without the True Lord, how can anyone find release? The jewel of the Lord's Glorious Praises comes by the karma of good actions.<br>
  When He Himself releases them, only then are they released. He Himself is the Great Master.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, they are released, when He Himself grants His Grace.<br>
  Glorious greatness rests in His Hands. He blesses those with whom He is pleased. ||33||<br>
  The soul trembles and shakes, when it loses its mooring and support.<br>
  Only the support of the True Lord brings honor and glory. Through it, one's works are never in vain.<br>
  The Lord is eternal and forever stable; the Guru is stable, and contemplation upon the True Lord is stable.<br>
  O Lord and Master of angels, men and Yogic masters, You are the support of the unsupported.<br>
  In all places and interspaces, You are the Giver, the Great Giver.<br>
  Wherever I look, there I see You, Lord; You have no end or limitation.<br>
  You are pervading and permeating the places and interspaces; reflecting upon the Word of the Guru's Shabad, You are found.<br>
  You give gifts even when they are not asked for; You are great, inaccessible and infinite. ||34||<br>
  O Merciful Lord, You are the embodiment of mercy; creating the Creation, You behold it.<br>
  Please shower Your Mercy upon me, O God, and unite me with Yourself. In an instant, You destroy and rebuild.<br>
  You are all-wise and all-seeing; You are the Greatest Giver of all givers.<br>
  He is the Eradicator of poverty, and the Destroyer of pain; the Gurmukh realizes spiritual wisdom and meditation. ||35||<br>
  Losing his wealth, he cries out in anguish; the fool's consciousness is engrossed in wealth.<br>
  How rare are those who gather the wealth of Truth, and love the Immaculate Naam, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  If by losing your wealth, you may become absorbed in the Love of the One Lord, then just let it go.<br>
  Dedicate your mind, and surrender your head; seek only the Support of the Creator Lord.<br>
  Worldly affairs and wanderings cease, when the mind is filled with the bliss of the Shabad.<br>
  Even one's enemies become friends, meeting with the Guru, the Lord of the Universe.<br>
  Wandering from forest to forest searching, you will find that those things are within the home of your own heart.<br>
  United by the True Guru, you shall remain united, and the pains of birth and death will be ended. ||36||<br>
  Through various rituals, one does not find release. Without virtue, one is sent to the City of Death.<br>
  One will not have this world or the next; committing sinful mistakes, one comes to regret and repent in the end.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 060</h2></center>
  He has neither spiritual wisdom or meditation; neither Dharmic faith mor meditation.<br>
  Without the Name, how can one be fearless? How can he understand egotistical pride?<br>
  I am so tired - how can I get there? This ocean has no bottom or end.<br>
  I have no loving companions, whom I can ask for help.<br>
  O Nanak, crying out, "Beloved, Beloved", we are united with the Uniter.<br>
  He who separated me, unites me again; my love for the Guru is infinite. ||37||<br>
  Sin is bad, but it is dear to the sinner.<br>
  He loads himself with sin, and expands his world through sin.<br>
  Sin is far away from one who understands himself.<br>
  He is not afflicted by sorrow or separation.<br>
  How can one avoid falling into hell? How can he cheat the Messenger of Death?<br>
  How can coming and going be forgotten? Falsehood is bad, and death is cruel.<br>
  The mind is enveloped by entanglements, and into entanglements it falls.<br>
  Without the Name, how can anyone be saved? They rot away in sin. ||38||<br>
  Again and again, the crow falls into the trap.<br>
  Then he regrets it, but what can he do now?<br>
  Even though he is trapped, he pecks at the food; he does not understand.<br>
  If he meets the True Guru, then he sees with his eyes.<br>
  Like a fish, he is caught in the noose of death.<br>
  Do not seek liberation from anyone else, except the Guru, the Great Giver.<br>
  Over and over again, he comes; over and over again, he goes.<br>
  Be absorbed in love for the One Lord, and remain lovingly focused on Him.<br>
  In this way you shall be saved, and you shall not fall into the trap again. ||39||<br>
  She calls out, "Brother, O brother - stay, O brother!" But he becomes a stranger.<br>
  Her brother departs for his own home, and his sister burns with the pain of separation.<br>
  In this world, her father's home, the daughter, the innocent soul bride, loves her Young Husband Lord.<br>
  If you long for your Husband Lord, O soul bride, then serve the True Guru with love.<br>
  How rare are the spiritually wise, who meet the True Guru, and truly understand.<br>
  All glorious greatness rests in the Lord and Master's Hands. He grants them, when He is pleased.<br>
  How rare are those who contemplate the Word of the Guru's Bani; they become Gurmukh.<br>
  This is the Bani of the Supreme Being; through it, one dwells within the home of his inner being. ||40||<br>
  Shattering and breaking apart, He creates and re-creates; creating, He shatters again. He builds up what He has demolished, and demolishes what He has built.<br>
  He dries up the pools which are full, and fills the dried tanks again. He is all-powerful and independent.<br>
  Deluded by doubt, they have gone insane; without destiny, what do they obtain?<br>
  The Gurmukhs know that God holds the string; wherever He pulls it, they must go.<br>
  Those who sing the Glorious Praises of the Lord, are forever imbued with His Love; they never again feel regret.<br>
  Bhabha: If someone seeks, and then becomes Gurmukh, then he comes to dwell in the home of his own heart.<br>
  Bhabha: The way of the terrifying world-ocean is treacherous. Remain free of hope, in the midst of hope, and you shall cross over.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, one comes to understand himself; in this way, he remains dead while yet alive. ||41||<br>
  Crying out for the wealth and riches of Maya, they die; but Maya does not go along with them.<br>
  The soul-swan arises and departs, sad and depressed, leaving its wealth behind.<br>
  The false mind is hunted by the Messenger of Death; it carries its faults along when it goes.<br>
  The mind turns inward, and merges with mind, when it is with virtue.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 061</h2></center>
  Crying out, "Mine, mine!", they have died, but without the Name, they find only pain.<br>
  So where are their forts, mansions, palaces and courts? They are like a short story.<br>
  O Nanak, without the True Name, the false just come and go.<br>
  He Himself is clever and so very beautiful; He Himself is wise and all-knowing. ||42||<br>
  Those who come, must go in the end; they come and go, regretting and repenting.<br>
  They will pass through 8.4 millions species; this number does not decrease or rise.<br>
  They alone are saved, who love the Lord.<br>
  Their worldly entanglements are ended, and Maya is conquered.<br>
  Whoever is seen, shall depart; who should I make my friend?<br>
  I dedicate my soul, and place my body and mind in offering before Him.<br>
  You are eternally stable, O Creator, Lord and Master; I lean on Your Support.<br>
  Conquered by virtue, egotism is killed; imbued with the Word of the Shabad, the mind rejects the world. ||43||<br>
  Neither the kings nor the nobles will remain; neither the rich nor the poor will remain.<br>
  When one's turn comes, no one can stay here.<br>
  The path is difficult and treacherous; the pools and mountains are impassable.<br>
  My body is filled with faults; I am dying of grief. Without virtue, how can I enter my home?<br>
  The virtuous take virtue, and meet God; how can I meet them with love?<br>
  If ony I could be like them, chanting and meditating within my heart on the Lord.<br>
  He is overflowing with faults and demerits, but virtue dwells within him as well.<br>
  Without the True Guru, he does not see God's Virtues; he does not chant the Glorious Virtues of God. ||44||<br>
  God's soldiers take care of their homes; their pay is pre-ordained, before they come into the world.<br>
  They serve their Supreme Lord and Master, and obtain the profit.<br>
  They renounce greed, avarice and evil, and forget them from their minds.<br>
  In the fortress of the body, they announce the victory of their Supreme King; they are never ever vanquished.<br>
  One who calls himself a servant of his Lord and Master, and yet speaks defiantly to Him,<br>
  shall forfeit his pay, and not be seated upon the throne.<br>
  Glorious greatness rests in the hands of my Beloved; He gives, according to the Pleasure of His Will.<br>
  He Himself does everything; who else should we address? No one else does anything. ||45||<br>
  I cannot conceive of any other, who could be seated upon the royal cushions.<br>
  The Supreme Man of men eradicates hell; He is True, and True is His Name.<br>
  I wandered around searching for Him in the forests and meadows; I contemplate Him within my mind.<br>
  The treasures of myriads of pearls, jewels and emeralds are in the hands of the True Guru.<br>
  Meeting with God, I am exalted and elevated; I love the One Lord single-mindedly.<br>
  O Nanak, one who lovingly meets with his Beloved, earns profit in the world hereafter.<br>
  He who created and formed the creation, made your form as well.<br>
  As Gurmukh, meditate on the Infinite Lord, who has no end or limitation. ||46||<br>
  Rharha: The Dear Lord is beautiful;<br>
  There is no other king, except Him.<br>
  Rharha: Listen to the spell, and the Lord will come to dwell in your mind.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, one finds the Lord; do not be deluded by doubt.<br>
  He alone is the true banker, who has the capital of the wealth of the Lord.<br>
  The Gurmukh is perfect - applaud him!<br>
  Through the beautiful Word of the Guru's Bani, the Lord is obtained; contemplate the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 062</h2></center>
  Self-conceit is eliminated, and pain is eradicated; the soul bride obtains her Husband Lord. ||47||<br>
  He hoards gold and silver, but this wealth is false and poisonous, nothing more than ashes.<br>
  He calls himself a banker, gathering wealth, but he is ruined by his dual-mindedness.<br>
  The truthful ones gather Truth; the True Name is priceless.<br>
  The Lord is immaculate and pure; through Him, their honor is true, and their speech is true.<br>
  You are my friend and companion, all-knowing Lord; You are the lake, and You are the swan.<br>
  I am a sacrifice to that being, whose mind is filled with the True Lord and Master.<br>
  Know the One who created love and attachment to Maya, the Enticer.<br>
  One who realizes the all-knowing Primal Lord, looks alike upon poison and nectar. ||48||<br>
  Without patience and forgiveness, countless hundreds of thousands have perished.<br>
  Their numbers cannot be counted; how could I count them? Bothered and bewildered, uncounted numbers have died.<br>
  One who realizes his Lord and Master is set free, and not bound by chains.<br>
  Through the Word of the Shabad, enter the Mansion of the Lord's Presence; you shall be blessed with patience, forgiveness, truth and peace.<br>
  Partake of the true wealth of meditation, and the Lord Himself shall abide within your body.<br>
  With mind, body and mouth, chant His Glorious Virtues forever; courage and composure shall enter deep within your mind.<br>
  Through egotism, one is distracted and ruined; other than the Lord, all things are corrupt.<br>
  Forming His creatures, He placed Himself within them; the Creator is unattached and infinite. ||49||<br>
  No one knows the mystery of the Creator of the World.<br>
  Whatever the Creator of the World does, is certain to occur.<br>
  For wealth, some meditate on the Lord.<br>
  By pre-ordained destiny, wealth is obtained.<br>
  For the sake of wealth, some become servants or thieves.<br>
  Wealth does not go along with them when they die; it passes into the hands of others.<br>
  Without Truth, honor is not obtained in the Court of the Lord.<br>
  Drinking in the subtle essence of the Lord, one is emancipated in the end. ||50||<br>
  Seeing and perceiving, O my companions, I am wonder-struck and amazed.<br>
  My egotism, which proclaimed itself in possessiveness and self-conceit, is dead. My mind chants the Word of the Shabad, and attains spiritual wisdom.<br>
  I am so tired of wearing all these necklaces, hair-ties and bracelets, and decorating myself.<br>
  Meeting with my Beloved, I have found peace; now, I wear the necklace of total virtue.<br>
  O Nanak, the Gurmukh attains the Lord, with love and affection.<br>
  Without the Lord, who has found peace? Reflect upon this in your mind, and see.<br>
  Read about the Lord, understand the Lord, and enshrine love for the Lord.<br>
  Chant the Lord's Name, and meditate on the Lord; hold tight to the Support of the Name of the Lord. ||51||<br>
  The inscription inscribed by the Creator Lord cannot be erased, O my companions.<br>
  He who created the universe, in His Mercy, installs His Feet within us.<br>
  Glorious greatness rests in the Hands of the Creator; reflect upon the Guru, and understand this.<br>
  This inscription cannot be challenged. As it pleases You, You care for me.<br>
  By Your Glance of Grace, I have found peace; O Nanak, reflect upon the Shabad.<br>
  The self-willed manmukhs are confused; they rot away and die. Only by reflecting upon the Guru can they be saved.<br>
  What can anyone say, about that Primal Lord, who cannot be seen?<br>
  I am a sacrifice to my Guru, who has revealed Him to me, within my own heart. ||52||<br>
  That Pandit, that religious scholar, is said to be well-educated, if he contemplates knowledge with intuitive ease.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 063</h2></center>
  Considering his knowledge, he finds the essence of reality, and lovingly focuses his attention on the Name of the Lord.<br>
  The self-willed manmukh sells his knowledge; he earns poison, and eats poison.<br>
  The fool does not think of the Word of the Shabad. He has no understanding, no comprehension. ||53||<br>
  That Pandit is called Gurmukh, who imparts understanding to his students.<br>
  Contemplate the Naam, the Name of the Lord; gather in the Naam, and earn the true profit in this world.<br>
  With the true notebook of the true mind, study the most sublime Word of the Shabad.<br>
  O Nanak, he alone is learned, and he alone is a wise Pandit, who wears the necklace of the Lord's Name. ||54||1||<br>
  Raamkalee, First Mehl, Sidh Gosht ~ Conversations With The Siddhas:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  The Siddhas formed an assembly; sitting in their Yogic postures, they shouted, "Salute this gathering of Saints."<br>
  I offer my salutation to the One who is true, infinite and incomparably beautiful.<br>
  I cut off my head, and offer it to Him; I dedicate my body and mind to Him.<br>
  O Nanak, meeting with the Saints, Truth is obtained, and one is spontaneously blessed with distinction. ||1||<br>
  What is the use of wandering around? Purity comes only through Truth.<br>
  Without the True Word of the Shabad, no one finds liberation. ||1||Pause||<br>
  "Who are you? What is your name? What is your way? What is your goal?<br>
  We pray that you will answer us truthfully; we are a sacrifice to the humble Saints.<br>
  Where is your seat? Where do you live, boy? Where did you come from, and where are you going?<br>
  Tell us, Nanak - the detached Siddhas wait to hear your reply. What is your path?"||2||<br>
  He dwells deep within the nucleus of each and every heart. This is my seat and my home. I walk in harmony with the Will of the True Guru.<br>
  I came from the Celestial Lord God; I go wherever He orders me to go. I am Nanak, forever under the Command of His Will.<br>
  I sit in the posture of the eternal, imperishable Lord. These are the Teachings I have received from the Guru.<br>
  As Gurmukh, I have come to understand and realize myself; I merge in the Truest of the True. ||3||<br>
  "The world-ocean is treacherous and impassable; how can one cross over?<br>
  Charpat the Yogi says, O Nanak, think it over, and give us your true reply."<br>
  What answer can I give to someone, who claims to understand himself?<br>
  I speak the Truth; if you have already crossed over, how can I argue with you? ||4||<br>
  The lotus flower floats untouched upon the surface of the water, and the duck swims through the stream;<br>
  with one's consciousness focused on the Word of the Shabad, one crosses over the terrifying world-ocean. O Nanak, chant the Naam, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  One who lives alone, as a hermit, enshrining the One Lord in his mind, remaining unaffected by hope in the midst of hope,<br>
  sees and inspires others to see the inaccessible, unfathomable Lord. Nanak is his slave. ||5||<br>
  "Listen, Lord, to our prayer. We seek your true opinion.<br>
  Don't be angry with us - please tell us: How can we find the Guru's Door?"<br>
  This fickle mind sits in its true home, O Nanak, through the Support of the Naam, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  The Creator Himself unites us in Union, and inspires us to love the Truth. ||6||<br>
  "Away from stores and highways, we live in the woods, among plants and trees.<br>
  For food, we take fruits and roots. This is the spiritual wisdom spoken by the renunciates.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 064</h2></center>
  We bathe at sacred shrines of pilgrimage, and obtain the fruits of peace; not even an iota of filth sticks to us.<br>
  Luhaareepaa, the disciple of Gorakh says, this is the Way of Yoga."||7||<br>
  In the stores and on the road, do not sleep; do not let your consciousness covet anyone else's home.<br>
  Without the Name, the mind has no firm support; O Nanak, this hunger never departs.<br>
  The Guru has revealed the stores and the city within the home of my own heart, where I intuitively carry on the true trade.<br>
  Sleep little, and eat little; O Nanak, this is the essence of wisdom. ||8||<br>
  "Wear the robes of the sect of Yogis who follow Gorakh; put on the ear-rings, begging wallet and patched coat.<br>
  Among the twelve schools of Yoga, ours is the highest; among the six schools of philosophy, ours is the best path.<br>
  This is the way to instruct the mind, so you will never suffer beatings again."<br>
  Nanak speaks: the Gurmukh understands; this is the way that Yoga is attained. ||9||<br>
  Let constant absorption in the Word of the Shabad deep within be your ear-rings; eradicate egotism and attachment.<br>
  Discard sexual desire, anger and egotism, and through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, attain true understanding.<br>
  For your patched coat and begging bowl, see the Lord God pervading and permeating everywhere; O Nanak, the One Lord will carry you across.<br>
  True is our Lord and Master, and True is His Name. Analyze it, and you shall find the Word of the Guru to be True. ||10||<br>
  Let your mind turn away in detachment from the world, and let this be your begging bowl. Let the lessons of the five elements be your cap.<br>
  Let the body be your meditation mat, and the mind your loin cloth.<br>
  Let truth, contentment and self-discipline be your companions.<br>
  O Nanak, the Gurmukh dwells on the Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||11||<br>
  "Who is hidden? Who is liberated?<br>
  Who is united, inwardly and outwardly?<br>
  Who comes, and who goes?<br>
  Who is permeating and pervading the three worlds?"||12||<br>
  He is hidden within each and every heart. The Gurmukh is liberated.<br>
  Through the Word of the Shabad, one is united, inwardly and outwardly.<br>
  The self-willed manmukh perishes, and comes and goes.<br>
  O Nanak, the Gurmukh merges in Truth. ||13||<br>
  "How is one placed in bondage, and consumed by the serpent of Maya?<br>
  How does one lose, and how does one gain?<br>
  How does one become immaculate and pure? How is the darkness of ignorance removed?<br>
  One who understands this essence of reality is our Guru."||14||<br>
  Man is bound by evil-mindedness, and consumed by Maya, the serpent.<br>
  The self-willed manmukh loses, and the Gurmukh gains.<br>
  Meeting the True Guru, darkness is dispelled.<br>
  O Nanak, eradicating egotism, one merges in the Lord. ||15||<br>
  Focused deep within, in perfect absorption,<br>
  the soul-swan does not fly away, and the body-wall does not collapse.<br>
  Then, one knows that his true home is in the cave of intuitive poise.<br>
  O Nanak, the True Lord loves those who are truthful. ||16||<br>
  "Why have you left your house and become a wandering Udaasee?<br>
  Why have you adopted these religious robes?<br>
  What merchandise do you trade?<br>
  How will you carry others across with you?"||17||<br>
  I became a wandering Udaasee, searching for the Gurmukhs.<br>
  I have adopted these robes seeking the Blessed Vision of the Lord's Darshan.<br>
  I trade in the merchandise of Truth.<br>
  O Nanak, as Gurmukh, I carry others across. ||18||<br>
  "How have you changed the course of your life?<br>
  With what have you linked your mind?<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 065</h2></center>
  How have you subdued your hopes and desires?<br>
  How have you found the Light deep within your nucleus?<br>
  Without teeth, how can you eat iron?<br>
  Give us your true opinion, Nanak."||19||<br>
  Born into the House of the True Guru, my wandering in reincarnation ended.<br>
  My mind is attached and attuned to the unstruck sound current.<br>
  Through the Word of the Shabad, my hopes and desires have been burnt away.<br>
  As Gurmukh, I found the Light deep within the nucleus of my self.<br>
  Eradicating the three qualities, one eats iron.<br>
  O Nanak, the Emancipator emancipates. ||20||<br>
  "What can you tell us about the beginning? In what home did the absolute dwell then?<br>
  What are the ear-rings of spiritual wisdom? Who dwells in each and every heart?<br>
  How can one avoid the attack of death? How can one enter the home of fearlessness?<br>
  How can one know the posture of intuition and contentment, and overcome one's adversaries?"<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, egotism and corruption are conquered, and then one comes to dwell in the home of the self within.<br>
  One who realizes the Shabad of the One who created the creation - Nanak is his slave. ||21||<br>
  "Where did we come from? Where are we going? Where will we be absorbed?<br>
  One who reveals the meaning of this Shabad is the Guru, who has no greed at all.<br>
  How can one find the essence of the unmanifest reality? How does one become Gurmukh, and enshrine love for the Lord?<br>
  He Himself is consciousness, He Himself is the Creator; share with us, Nanak, your wisdom."<br>
  By His Command we come, and by His Command we go; by His Command, we merge in absorption.<br>
  Through the Perfect Guru, live the Truth; through the Word of the Shabad, the state of dignity is attained. ||22||<br>
  We can only express a sense of wonder about the beginning. The absolute abided endlessly deep within Himself then.<br>
  Consider freedom from desire to be the ear-rings of the Guru's spiritual wisdom. The True Lord, the Soul of all, dwells within each and every heart.<br>
  Through the Guru's Word, one merges in the absolute, and intuitively receives the immaculate essence.<br>
  O Nanak, that Sikh who seeks and finds the Way does not serve any other.<br>
  Wonderful and amazing is His Command; He alone realizes His Command and knows the true way of life of His creatures.<br>
  One who eradicates his self-conceit becomes free of desire; he alone is a Yogi, who enshrines the True Lord deep within. ||23||<br>
  From His state of absolute existence, He assumed the immaculate form; from formless, He assumed the supreme form.<br>
  By pleasing the True Guru, the supreme status is obtained, and one is absorbed in the True Word of the Shabad.<br>
  He knows the True Lord as the One and only; he sends his egotism and duality far away.<br>
  He alone is a Yogi, who realizes the Word of the Guru's Shabad; the lotus of the heart blossoms forth within.<br>
  If one remains dead while yet alive, then he understands everything; he knows the Lord deep within himself, who is kind and compassionate to all.<br>
  O Nanak, he is blessed with glorious greatness; he realizes himself in all beings. ||24||<br>
  We emerge from Truth, and merge into Truth again. The pure being merges into the One True Lord.<br>
  The false come, and find no place of rest; in duality, they come and go.<br>
  This coming and going in reincarnation is ended through the Word of the Guru's Shabad; the Lord Himself analyzes and grants His forgiveness.<br>
  One who suffers from the disease of duality, forgets the Naam, the source of nectar.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 066</h2></center>
  He alone understands, whom the Lord inspires to understand. Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, one is liberated.<br>
  O Nanak, the Emancipator emancipates one who drives out egotism and duality. ||25||<br>
  The self-willed manmukhs are deluded, under the shadow of death.<br>
  They look into the homes of others, and lose.<br>
  The manmukhs are confused by doubt, wandering in the wilderness.<br>
  Having lost their way, they are plundered; they chant their mantras at cremation grounds.<br>
  They do not think of the Shabad; instead, they utter obscenities.<br>
  O Nanak, those who are attuned to the Truth know peace. ||26||<br>
  The Gurmukh lives in the Fear of God, the True Lord.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Bani, the Gurmukh refines the unrefined.<br>
  The Gurmukh sings the immaculate, Glorious Praises of the Lord.<br>
  The Gurmukh attains the supreme, sanctified status.<br>
  The Gurmukh meditates on the Lord with every hair of his body.<br>
  O Nanak, the Gurmukh merges in Truth. ||27||<br>
  The Gurmukh is pleasing to the True Guru; this is contemplation on the Vedas.<br>
  Pleasing the True Guru, the Gurmukh is carried across.<br>
  Pleasing the True Guru, the Gurmukh receives the spiritual wisdom of the Shabad.<br>
  Pleasing the True Guru, the Gurmukh comes to know the path within.<br>
  The Gurmukh attains the unseen and infinite Lord.<br>
  O Nanak, the Gurmukh finds the door of liberation. ||28||<br>
  The Gurmukh speaks the unspoken wisdom.<br>
  In the midst of his family, the Gurmukh lives a spiritual life.<br>
  The Gurmukh lovingly meditates deep within.<br>
  The Gurmukh obtains the Shabad, and righteous conduct.<br>
  He knows the mystery of the Shabad, and inspires others to know it.<br>
  O Nanak, burning away his ego, he merges in the Lord. ||29||<br>
  The True Lord fashioned the earth for the sake of the Gurmukhs.<br>
  There, he set in motion the play of creation and destruction.<br>
  One who is filled with the Word of the Guru's Shabad enshrines love for the Lord.<br>
  Attuned to the Truth, he goes to his home with honor.<br>
  Without the True Word of the Shabad, no one receives honor.<br>
  O Nanak, without the Name, how can one be absorbed in Truth? ||30||<br>
  The Gurmukh obtains the eight miraculous spiritual powers, and all wisdom.<br>
  The Gurmukh crosses over the terrifying world-ocean, and obtains true understanding.<br>
  The Gurmukh knows the ways of truth and untruth.<br>
  The Gurmukh knows worldliness and renunciation.<br>
  The Gurmukh crosses over, and carries others across as well.<br>
  O Nanak, the Gurmukh is emancipated through the Shabad. ||31||<br>
  Attuned to the Naam, the Name of the Lord, egotism is dispelled.<br>
  Attuned to the Naam, they remain absorbed in the True Lord.<br>
  Attuned to the Naam, they contemplate the Way of Yoga.<br>
  Attuned to the Naam, they find the door of liberation.<br>
  Attuned to the Naam, they understand the three worlds.<br>
  O Nanak, attuned to the Naam, eternal peace is found. ||32||<br>
  Attuned to the Naam, they attain Sidh Gosht - conversation with the Siddhas.<br>
  Attuned to the Naam, they practice intense meditation forever.<br>
  Attuned to the Naam, they live the true and excellent lifestyle.<br>
  Attuned to the Naam, they contemplate the Lord's virtues and spiritual wisdom.<br>
  Without the Name, all that is spoken is useless.<br>
  O Nanak, attuned to the Naam, their victory is celebrated. ||33||<br>
  Through the Perfect Guru, one obtains the Naam, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  The Way of Yoga is to remain absorbed in Truth.<br>
  The Yogis wander in the twelve schools of Yoga; the Sannyaasis in six and four.<br>
  One who remains dead while yet alive, through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, finds the door of liberation.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 067</h2></center>
  Without the Shabad, all are attached to duality. Contemplate this in your heart, and see.<br>
  O Nanak, blessed and very fortunate are those who keep the True Lord enshrined in their hearts. ||34||<br>
  The Gurmukh obtains the jewel, lovingly focused on the Lord.<br>
  The Gurmukh intuitively recognizes the value of this jewel.<br>
  The Gurmukh practices Truth in action.<br>
  The mind of the Gurmukh is pleased with the True Lord.<br>
  The Gurmukh sees the unseen, when it pleases the Lord.<br>
  O Nanak, the Gurmukh does not have to endure punishment. ||35||<br>
  The Gurmukh is blessed with the Name, charity and purification.<br>
  The Gurmukh centers his meditation on the celestial Lord.<br>
  The Gurmukh obtains honor in the Court of the Lord.<br>
  The Gurmukh obtains the Supreme Lord, the Destroyer of fear.<br>
  The Gurmukh does good deeds, an inspires others to do so.<br>
  O Nanak, the Gurmukh unites in the Lord's Union. ||36||<br>
  The Gurmukh understands the Simritees, the Shaastras and the Vedas.<br>
  The Gurmukh knows the secrets of each and every heart.<br>
  The Gurmukh eliminates hate and envy.<br>
  The Gurmukh erases all accounting.<br>
  The Gurmukh is imbued with love for the Lord's Name.<br>
  O Nanak, the Gurmukh realizes his Lord and Master. ||37||<br>
  Without the Guru, one wanders, coming and going in reincarnation.<br>
  Without the Guru, one's work is useless.<br>
  Without the Guru, the mind is totally unsteady.<br>
  Without the Guru, one is unsatisfied, and eats poison.<br>
  Without the Guru, one is stung by the poisonous snake of Maya, and dies.<br>
  O Nanak without the Guru, all is lost. ||38||<br>
  One who meets the Guru is carried across.<br>
  His sins are erased, and he is emancipated through virtue.<br>
  The supreme peace of liberation is attained, contemplating the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  The Gurmukh is never defeated.<br>
  In the store of the body, this mind is the merchant;<br>
  O Nanak, it deals intuitively in Truth. ||39||<br>
  The Gurmukh is the bridge, built by the Architect of Destiny.<br>
