  The demons of passion which plundered Sri Lanka - the body - have been conquered.<br>
  Ram Chand - the mind - has slaughtered Raawan - pride;<br>
  the Gurmukh understands the secret revealed by Babheekhan.<br>
  The Gurmukh carries even stones across the ocean.<br>
  The Gurmukh saves millions of people. ||40||<br>
  The comings and goings in reincarnation are ended for the Gurmukh.<br>
  The Gurmukh is honored in the Court of the Lord.<br>
  The Gurmukh distinguishes the true from the false.<br>
  The Gurmukh focuses his meditation on the celestial Lord.<br>
  In the Court of the Lord, the Gurmukh is absorbed in His Praises.<br>
  O Nanak, the Gurmukh is not bound by bonds. ||41||<br>
  The Gurmukh obtains the Name of the Immaculate Lord.<br>
  Through the Shabad, the Gurmukh burns away his ego.<br>
  The Gurmukh sings the Glorious Praises of the True Lord.<br>
  The Gurmukh remains absorbed in the True Lord.<br>
  Through the True Name, the Gurmukh is honored and exalted.<br>
  O Nanak, the Gurmukh understands all the worlds. ||42||<br>
  "What is the root, the source of all? What teachings hold for these times?<br>
  Who is your guru? Whose disciple are you?<br>
  What is that speech, by which you remain unattached?<br>
  Listen to what we say, O Nanak, you little boy.<br>
  Give us your opinion on what we have said.<br>
  How can the Shabad carry us across the terrifying world-ocean?"||43||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 068</h2></center>
  From the air came the beginning. This is the age of the True Guru's Teachings.<br>
  The Shabad is the Guru, upon whom I lovingly focus my consciousness; I am the chaylaa, the disciple.<br>
  Speaking the Unspoken Speech, I remain unattached.<br>
  O Nanak, throughout the ages, the Lord of the World is my Guru.<br>
  I contemplate the sermon of the Shabad, the Word of the One God.<br>
  The Gurmukh puts out the fire of egotism. ||44||<br>
  "With teeth of wax, how can one chew iron?<br>
  What is that food, which takes away pride?<br>
  How can one live in the palace, the home of snow, wearing robes of fire?<br>
  Where is that cave, within which one may remain unshaken?<br>
  Who should we know to be pervading here and there?<br>
  What is that meditation, which leads the mind to be absorbed in itself?"||45||<br>
  Eradicating egotism and individualism from within,<br>
  and erasing duality, the mortal becomes one with God.<br>
  The world is difficult for the foolish, self-willed manmukh;<br>
  practicing the Shabad, one chews iron.<br>
  Know the One Lord, inside and out.<br>
  O Nanak, the fire is quenched, through the Pleasure of the True Guru's Will. ||46||<br>
  Imbued with the True Fear of God, pride is taken away;<br>
  realize that He is One, and contemplate the Shabad.<br>
  With the True Shabad abiding deep within the heart,<br>
  the body and mind are cooled and soothed, and colored with the Lord's Love.<br>
  The fire of sexual desire, anger and corruption is quenched.<br>
  O Nanak, the Beloved bestows His Glance of Grace. ||47||<br>
  "The moon of the mind is cool and dark; how is it enlightened?<br>
  How does the sun blaze so brilliantly?<br>
  How can the constant watchful gaze of Death be turned away?<br>
  By what understanding is the honor of the Gurmukh preserved?<br>
  Who is the warrior, who conquers Death?<br>
  Give us your thoughtful reply, O Nanak."||48||<br>
  Giving voice to the Shabad, the moon of the mind is illuminated with infinity.<br>
  When the sun dwells in the house of the moon, the darkness is dispelled.<br>
  Pleasure and pain are just the same, when one takes the Support of the Naam, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  He Himself saves, and carries us across.<br>
  With faith in the Guru, the mind merges in Truth,<br>
  and then, prays Nanak, one is not consumed by Death. ||49||<br>
  The essence of the Naam, the Name of the Lord, is known to be the most exalted and excellent of all.<br>
  Without the Name, one is afflicted by pain and death.<br>
  When one's essence merges into the essence, the mind is satisfied and fulfilled.<br>
  Duality is gone, and one enters into the home of the One Lord.<br>
  The breath blows across the sky of the Tenth Gate and vibrates.<br>
  O Nanak, the mortal then intuitively meets the eternal, unchanging Lord. ||50||<br>
  The absolute Lord is deep within; the absolute Lord is outside us as well. The absolute Lord totally fills the three worlds.<br>
  One who knows the Lord in the fourth state, is not subject to virtue or vice.<br>
  One who knows the mystery of God the Absolute, who pervades each and every heart, knows the Primal Being, the Immaculate Divine Lord.<br>
  That humble being who is imbued with the Immaculate Naam,<br>
  O Nanak, is himself the Primal Lord, the Architect of Destiny. ||51||<br>
  "Everyone speaks of the Absolute Lord, the unmanifest void.<br>
  How can one find this absolute void?<br>
  Who are they, who are attuned to this absolute void?"<br>
  They are like the Lord, from whom they originated.<br>
  They are not born, they do not die; they do not come and go.<br>
  O Nanak, the Gurmukhs instruct their minds. ||52||<br>
  By practicing control over the nine gates, one attains perfect control over the Tenth Gate.<br>
  There, the unstruck sound current of the absolute Lord vibrates and resounds.<br>
  Behold the True Lord ever-present, and merge with Him.<br>
  The True Lord is pervading and permeating each and every heart.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 069</h2></center>
  The hidden Bani of the Word is revealed.<br>
  O Nanak, the True Lord is revealed and known. ||53||<br>
  Meeting with the Lord through intuition and love, peace is found.<br>
  The Gurmukh remains awake and aware; he does not fall sleep.<br>
  He enshrines the unlimited, absolute Shabad deep within.<br>
  Chanting the Shabad, he is liberated, and saves others as well.<br>
  Those who practice the Guru's Teachings are attuned to the Truth.<br>
  O Nanak, those who eradicate their self-conceit meet with the Lord; they do not remain separated by doubt. ||54||<br>
  "Where is that place, where evil thoughts are destroyed?<br>
  The mortal does not understand the essence of reality; why must he suffer in pain?"<br>
  No one can save one who is tied up at Death's door.<br>
  Without the Shabad, no one has any credit or honor.<br>
  "How can one obtain understanding and cross over?"<br>
  O Nanak, the foolish self-willed manmukh does not understand. ||55||<br>
  Evil thoughts are erased, contemplating the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  Meeting with the True Guru, the door of liberation is found.<br>
  The self-willed manmukh does not understand the essence of reality, and is burnt to ashes.<br>
  His evil-mindedness separates him from the Lord, and he suffers.<br>
  Accepting the Hukam of the Lord's Command, he is blessed with all virtues and spiritual wisdom.<br>
  O Nanak, he is honored in the Court of the Lord. ||56||<br>
  One who possesses the merchandise, the wealth of the True Name,<br>
  crosses over, and carries others across with him as well.<br>
  One who intuitively understands, and is attuned to the Lord, is honored.<br>
  No one can estimate his worth.<br>
  Wherever I look, I see the Lord permeating and pervading.<br>
  O Nanak, through the Love of the True Lord, one crosses over. ||57||<br>
  "Where is the Shabad said to dwell? What will carry us across the terrifying world-ocean?<br>
  The breath, when exhaled, extends out ten finger lengths; what is the support of the breath?<br>
  Speaking and playing, how can one be stable and steady? How can the unseen be seen?"<br>
  Listen, O master; Nanak prays truly. Instruct your own mind.<br>
  The Gurmukh is lovingly attuned to the True Shabad. Bestowing His Glance of Grace, He unites us in His Union.<br>
  He Himself is all-knowing and all-seeing. By perfect destiny, we merge in Him. ||58||<br>
  That Shabad dwells deep within the nucleus of all beings. God is invisible; wherever I look, there I see Him.<br>
  The air is the dwelling place of the absolute Lord. He has no qualities; He has all qualities.<br>
  When He bestows His Glance of Grace, the Shabad comes to abide within the heart, and doubt is eradicated from within.<br>
  The body and mind become immaculate, through the Immaculate Word of His Bani. Let His Name be enshrined in your mind.<br>
  The Shabad is the Guru, to carry you across the terrifying world-ocean. Know the One Lord alone, here and hereafter.<br>
  He has no form or color, shadow or illusion; O Nanak, realize the Shabad. ||59||<br>
  O reclusive hermit, the True, Absolute Lord is the support of the exhaled breath, which extends out ten finger lengths.<br>
  The Gurmukh speaks and churns the essence of reality, and realizes the unseen, infinite Lord.<br>
  Eradicating the three qualities, he enshrines the Shabad within, and then, his mind is rid of egotism.<br>
  Inside and out, he knows the One Lord alone; he is in love with the Name of the Lord.<br>
  He understands the Sushmana, Ida and Pingala, when the unseen Lord reveals Himself.<br>
  O Nanak, the True Lord is above these three energy channels. Through the Word, the Shabad of the True Guru, one merges with Him. ||60||<br>
  "The air is said to be the soul of the mind. But what does the air feed on?<br>
  What is the way of the spiritual teacher, and the reclusive hermit? What is the occupation of the Siddha?"<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 070</h2></center>
  Without the Shabad, the essence does not come, O hermit, and the thirst of egotism does not depart.<br>
  Imbued with the Shabad, one finds the ambrosial essence, and remains fulfilled with the True Name.<br>
  "What is that wisdom, by which one remains steady and stable? What food brings satisfaction?"<br>
  O Nanak, when one looks upon pain and pleasure alike, through the True Guru, then he is not consumed by Death. ||61||<br>
  If one is not imbued with the Lord's Love, nor intoxicated with His subtle essence,<br>
  without the Word of the Guru's Shabad, he is frustrated, and consumed by his own inner fire.<br>
  He does not preserve his semen and seed, and does not chant the Shabad.<br>
  He does not control his breath; he does not worship and adore the True Lord.<br>
  But one who speaks the Unspoken Speech, and remains balanced,<br>
  O Nanak, attains the Lord, the Supreme Soul. ||62||<br>
  By Guru's Grace, one is attuned to the Lord's Love.<br>
  Drinking in the Ambrosial Nectar, he is intoxicated with the Truth.<br>
  Contemplating the Guru, the fire within is put out.<br>
  Drinking in the Ambrosial Nectar, the soul settles in peace.<br>
  Worshipping the True Lord in adoration, the Gurmukh crosses over the river of life.<br>
  O Nanak, after deep contemplation, this is understood. ||63||<br>
  "Where does this mind-elephant live? Where does the breath reside?<br>
  Where should the Shabad reside, so that the wanderings of the mind may cease?"<br>
  When the Lord blesses one with His Glance of Grace, he leads him to the True Guru. Then, this mind dwells in its own home within.<br>
  When the individual consumes his egotism, he becomes immaculate, and his wandering mind is restrained.<br>
  "How can the root, the source of all be realized? How can the soul know itself? How can the sun enter into the house of the moon?"<br>
  The Gurmukh eliminates egotism from within; then, O Nanak, the sun naturally enters into the home of the moon. ||64||<br>
  When the mind becomes steady and stable, it abides in the heart, and then the Gurmukh realizes the root, the source of all.<br>
  The breath is seated in the home of the navel; the Gurmukh searches, and finds the essence of reality.<br>
  This Shabad permeates the nucleus of the self, deep within, in its own home; the Light of this Shabad pervades the three worlds.<br>
  Hunger for the True Lord shall consume your pain, and through the True Lord, you shall be satisfied.<br>
  The Gurmukh knows the unstruck sound current of the Bani; how rare are those who understand.<br>
  Says Nanak, one who speaks the Truth is dyed in the color of Truth, which will never fade away. ||65||<br>
  "When this heart and body did not exist, where did the mind reside?<br>
  When there was no support of the navel lotus, then in which home did the breath reside?<br>
  When there was no form or shape, then how could anyone lovingly focus on the Shabad?<br>
  When there was no dungeon formed from egg and sperm, who could measure the Lord's value and extent?<br>
  When color, dress and form could not be seen, how could the True Lord be known?"<br>
  O Nanak, those who are attuned to the Naam, the Name of the Lord, are detached. Then and now, they see the Truest of the True. ||66||<br>
  When the heart and the body did not exist, O hermit, then the mind resided in the absolute, detached Lord.<br>
  When there was no support of the lotus of the navel, the breath remained in its own home, attuned to the Lord's Love.<br>
  When there was no form or shape or social class, then the Shabad, in its essence, resided in the unmanifest Lord.<br>
  When the world and the sky did not even exist, the Light of the Formless Lord filled the three worlds.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 071</h2></center>
  Color, dress and form were contained in the One Lord; the Shabad was contained in the One, Wondrous Lord.<br>
  Without the True Name, no one can become pure; O Nanak, this is the Unspoken Speech. ||67||<br>
  "How, in what way, was the world formed, O man? And what disaster will end it?"<br>
  In egotism, the world was formed, O man; forgetting the Naam, it suffers and dies.<br>
  One who becomes Gurmukh contemplates the essence of spiritual wisdom; through the Shabad, he burns away his egotism.<br>
  His body and mind become immaculate, through the Immaculate Bani of the Word. He remains absorbed in Truth.<br>
  Through the Naam, the Name of the Lord, he remains detached; he enshrines the True Name in his heart.<br>
  O Nanak, without the Name, Yoga is never attained; reflect upon this in your heart, and see. ||68||<br>
  The Gurmukh is one who reflects upon the True Word of the Shabad.<br>
  The True Bani is revealed to the Gurmukh.<br>
  The mind of the Gurmukh is drenched with the Lord's Love, but how rare are those who understand this.<br>
  The Gurmukh dwells in the home of the self, deep within.<br>
  The Gurmukh realizes the Way of Yoga.<br>
  O Nanak, the Gurmukh knows the One Lord alone. ||69||<br>
  Without serving the True Guru, Yoga is not attained;<br>
  without meeting the True Guru, no one is liberated.<br>
  Without meeting the True Guru, the Naam cannot be found.<br>
  Without meeting the True Guru, one suffers in terrible pain.<br>
  Without meeting the True Guru, there is only the deep darkness of egotistical pride.<br>
  O Nanak, without the True Guru, one dies, having lost the opportunity of this life. ||70||<br>
  The Gurmukh conquers his mind by subduing his ego.<br>
  The Gurmukh enshrines Truth in his heart.<br>
  The Gurmukh conquers the world; he knocks down the Messenger of Death, and kills it.<br>
  The Gurmukh does not lose in the Court of the Lord.<br>
  The Gurmukh is united in God's Union; he alone knows.<br>
  O Nanak, the Gurmukh realizes the Word of the Shabad. ||71||<br>
  This is the essence of the Shabad - listen, you hermits and Yogis. Without the Name, there is no Yoga.<br>
  Those who are attuned to the Name, remain intoxicated night and day; through the Name, they find peace.<br>
  Through the Name, everything is revealed; through the Name, understanding is obtained.<br>
  Without the Name, people wear all sorts of religious robes; the True Lord Himself has confused them.<br>
  The Name is obtained only from the True Guru, O hermit, and then, the Way of Yoga is found.<br>
  Reflect upon this in your mind, and see; O Nanak, without the Name, there is no liberation. ||72||<br>
  You alone know Your state and extent, Lord; What can anyone say about it?<br>
  You Yourself are hidden, and You Yourself are revealed. You Yourself enjoy all pleasures.<br>
  The seekers, the Siddhas, the many gurus and disciples wander around searching for You, according to Your Will.<br>
  They beg for Your Name, and You bless them with this charity. I am a sacrifice to the Blessed Vision of Your Darshan.<br>
  The eternal imperishable Lord God has staged this play; the Gurmukh understands it.<br>
  O Nanak, He extends Himself throughout the ages; there is no other than Him. ||73||1||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 072</h2></center>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Vaar Of Raamkalee, Third Mehl,<br>
  To Be Sung To The Tune Of 'Jodha And Veera Poorbaanee':<br>
  Shalok, Third Mehl:<br>
  The True Guru is the field of intuitive wisdom. One who is inspired to love Him,<br>
  plants the seed of the Name there. The Name sprouts up, and he remains absorbed in the Name.<br>
  But this egotism is the seed of skepticism; it has been uprooted.<br>
  It is not planted there, and it does not sprout; whatever God grants us, we eat.<br>
  When water mixes with water, it cannot be separated again.<br>
  O Nanak, the Gurmukh is wonderful; come, poeple, and see!<br>
  But what can the poor people see? They do not understand.<br>
  He alone sees, whom the Lord causes to see; the Lord comes to dwell in his mind. ||1||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  The self-willed manmukh is the field of sorrow and suffering. He plains sorrow, and eats sorrow.<br>
  In sorrow he is born, and in sorrow he dies. Acting in egotism, his life passes away.<br>
  He does not understand the coming and going of reincarnation; the blind man acts in blindness.<br>
  He does not know the One who gives, but he is attached to what is given.<br>
  O Nanak, he acts according to his pre-ordained destiny. He cannot do anything else. ||2||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  Meeting the True Guru, everlasting peace is obtained. He Himself leads us to meet Him.<br>
  This is the true meaning of peace, that one becomes immaculate within oneself.<br>
  The doubt of ignorance is eradicated, and spiritual wisdom is obtained.<br>
  Nanak comes to gaze upon the One Lord alone; wherever he looks, there He is. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  The True Lord created His throne, upon which He sits.<br>
  He Himself is everything; this is what the Word of the Guru's Shabad says.<br>
  Through His almighty creative power, He created and fashioned the mansions and hotels.<br>
  He made the two lamps, the sun and the moon; He formed the perfect form.<br>
  He Himself sees, and He Himself hears; meditate on the Word of the Guru's Shabad. ||1||<br>
  Waaho! Waaho! Hail, hail, O True King! True is Your Name. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Shalok:<br>
  Kabeer, I have ground myself into henna paste.<br>
  O my Husband Lord, You took no notice of me; You never applied me to Your feet. ||1||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  O Nanak, my Husband Lord keeps me like henna paste; He blesses me with His Glance of Grace.<br>
  He Himself grinds me, and He Himself rubs me; He Himself applies me to His feet.<br>
  This is the cup of love of my Lord and Master; He gives it as He chooses. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  You created the world with its variety; by the Hukam of Your Command, it comes, goes, and merges again in You.<br>
  You Yourself see, and blossom forth; there is no one else at all.<br>
  As it pleases You, You keep me. Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, I understand You.<br>
  You are the strength of all. As it pleases You, You lead us on.<br>
  There is no other as great as You; unto whom should I speak and talk? ||2||<br>
  Shalok, Third Mehl:<br>
  Deluded by doubt, I wandered over the whole world. Searching, I became frustrated.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 073</h2></center>
  My Husband Lord has not blessed me with peace and tranquility; what will work with Him?<br>
  By Guru's Grace, I meditate on the Lord; I enshrine Him deep within my heart.<br>
  O Nanak, seated in his her own home, she finds her Husband Lord, when the Creator Lord grants His Grace. ||1||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  Chasing after worldly affairs, the day is wasted, and the night passes in sleep.<br>
  Speaking lies, one eats poison; the self-willed manmukh departs, crying out in pain.<br>
  The Mesenger of Death holds his club over the mortal's head; in the love of duality, he loses his honor.<br>
  He never even thinks of the Name of the Lord; over and over again, he comes and goes in reincarnation.<br>
  But if, by Guru's Grace, the Lord's Name comes to dwell in his mind, then the Messenger of Death will not strike him down with his club.<br>
  Then, O Nanak, he merges intuitively into the Lord, receiving His Grace. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  Some are linked to His Praises, when the Lord blesses them with the Guru's Teachings.<br>
  Some are blessed with the Name of the eternal, unchanging True Lord.<br>
  Water, air and fire, by His Will, worship Him.<br>
  They are held in the Fear of God; He has formed the perfect form.<br>
  The Hukam, the Command of the One Lord is all-pervasive; accepting it, peace is found. ||3||<br>
  Shalok:<br>
  Kabeer, such is the touchstone of the Lord; the false cannot even touch it.<br>
  He alone passes this test of the Lord, who remains dead while yet alive. ||1||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  How can this mind be conquered? How can it be killed?<br>
  If one does not accept the Word of the Shabad, egotism does not depart.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, egotism is eradicated, and then, one is Jivan Mukta - liberated while yet alive.<br>
  O Nanak, one whom the Lord forgives is united with Him, and then no obstacles block his way. ||2||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  Everyone can say that they are dead while yet alive; how can they be liberated while yet alive?<br>
  If someone restrains himself through the Fear of God, and takes the medicine of the Love of God,<br>
  night and day, he sings the Glorious Praises of the Lord. In celestial peace and poise, he crosses over the poisonous, terrifying world-ocean, through the Naam, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  O Nanak, the Gurmukh finds the Lord; he is blessed with His Glance of Grace. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  God created the love of duality, and the three modes which pervade the universe.<br>
  He created Brahma, Vishnu and Shiva, who act according to His Will.<br>
  The Pandits, the religious scholars, and the astrologers study their books, but they do not understand contemplation.<br>
  Everything is Your play, O True Creator Lord.<br>
  As it pleases You, You bless us with forgiveness, and merge us in the True Word of the Shabad. ||4||<br>
  Shalok, Third Mehl:<br>
  The man of false mind practices falsehood.<br>
  He runs after Maya, and yet pretends to be a man of disciplined meditation.<br>
  Deluded by doubt, he visits all the sacred shrines of pilgrimage.<br>
  How can such a man of disciplined meditation attain the supreme status?<br>
  By Guru's Grace, one lives the Truth.<br>
  O Nanak, such a man of disciplined meditation attains liberation. ||1||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  He alone is a man of disciplined meditation, who practices this self-discipline.<br>
  Meeting with the True Guru, he contemplates the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  Serving the True Guru - this is the only acceptable disciplined meditation.<br>
  O Nanak, such a man of disciplined meditation is honored in the Court of the Lord. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  He created the night and the day, for the activities of the world.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 074</h2></center>
  Following the Guru's Teachings, one's heart is illumined, and the darkness is dispelled.<br>
  By the Hukam of His Command, He creates everything; He pervades and permeates all the woods and meadows.<br>
  He Himself is everything; the Gurmukh constantly chants the Lord's Name.<br>
  Through the Shabad, understanding comes; the True Lord Himself inspires us to understand. ||5||<br>
  Shalok, Third Mehl:<br>
  He is not called a renunciate, whose consciousness is filled with doubt.<br>
  Donations to him bring proportionate rewards.<br>
  He hungers for the supreme status of the Fearless, Immaculate Lord;<br>
  O Nanak, how rare are those who offer him this food. ||1||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  They are not called renunciates, who take food in the homes of others.<br>
  For the sake of their bellies, they wear various religious robes.<br>
  They alone are renunciates, O Nanak, who enter into their own souls.<br>
  They seek and find their Husband Lord; they dwell within the home of their own inner self. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  They sky and the earth are separate, but the True Lord supports them from within.<br>
  True are all those homes and gates, within which the True Name is enshrined.<br>
  The Hukam of the True Lord's Command is effective everywhere. The Gurmukh merges in the True Lord.<br>
  He Himself is True, and True is His throne. Seated upon it, He administers true justice.<br>
  The Truest of the True is all-pervading everywhere; the Gurmukh sees the unseen. ||6||<br>
  Shalok, Third Mehl:<br>
  In the world-ocean, the Infinite Lord abides. The false come and go in reincarnation.<br>
  One who walks according to his own will, suffers terrible punishment.<br>
  All things are in the world-ocean, but they are obtained only by the karma of good actions.<br>
  O Nanak, he alone obtains the nine treasures, who walks in the Will of the Lord. ||1||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  One who intuitively serves the True Guru, loses his life in egotism.<br>
  His tongue does not taste the sublime essence of the Lord, and his heart-lotus does not blossom forth.<br>
  The self-willed manmukh eats poison and dies; he is ruined by love and attachment to Maya.<br>
  Without the Name of the One Lord, his life is cursed, and his home is cursed as well.<br>
  When God Himself bestows His Glance of Grace, then one becomes the slave of His slaves.<br>
  And then, night and day, he serves the True Guru, and never leaves His side.<br>
  As the lotus flower floats unaffected in the water, so does he remain detached in his own household.<br>
  O servant Nanak, the Lord acts, and inspires everyone to act, according to the Pleasure of His Will. He is the treasure of virtue. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  For thirty-six ages, there was utter darkness. Then, the Lord revealed Himself.<br>
  He Himself created the entire universe. He Himself blessed it with understanding.<br>
  He created the Simritees and the Shaastras; He calculates the accounts of virtue and vice.<br>
  He alone understands, whom the Lord inspires to understand and to be pleased with the True Word of the Shabad.<br>
  He Himself is all-pervading; He Himself forgives, and unites with Himself. ||7||<br>
  Shalok, Third Mehl:<br>
  This body is all blood; without blood, the body cannot exist.<br>
  Those who are attuned to their Lord - their bodies are not filled with the blood of greed.<br>
  In the Fear of God, the body becomes thin, and the blood of greed passes out of the body.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 075</h2></center>
  As fire purifies metal, so does the Fear of the Lord eradicate the filth of evil-mindedness.<br>
  O Nanak, beautiful are those humble beings, who are imbued with the Lord's Love. ||1||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  In Raamkalee, I have enshrined the Lord in my mind; thus I have been embellished.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, my heart-lotus has blossomed forth; the Lord blessed me with the treasure of devotional worship.<br>
  My doubt was dispelled, and I woke up; the darkness of ignorance was dispelled.<br>
  She who is in love with her Lord, is the most infinitely beautiful.<br>
  Such a beautiful, happy soul-bride enjoys her Husband Lord forever.<br>
  The self-willed manmukhs do not know how to decorate themselves; wasting their whole lives, they depart.<br>
  Those who decorate themselves without devotional worship to the Lord, are continually reincarnated to suffer.<br>
  They do not obtain respect in this world; the Creator Lord alone knows what will happen to them in the world hereafter.<br>
  O Nanak, the True Lord is the One and only; duality exists only in the world.<br>
  He Himself enjoins them to good and bad; they do only that which the Creator Lord causes them to do. ||2||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  Without serving the True Guru, tranquility is not obtained. It cannot be found anywhere else.<br>
  No matter how much one may long for it, without the karma of good actions, it cannot be found.<br>
  Those whose inner beings are filled with greed and corruption, are ruined through the love of duality.<br>
  The cycle of birth and death is not ended, and filled with egotism, they suffer in pain.<br>
  Those who focus their consciousness on the True Guru, do not remain unfulfilled.<br>
  They are not summoned by the Messenger of Death, and they do not suffer in pain.<br>
  O Nanak, the Gurmukh is saved, merging in the True Word of the Shabad. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  He Himself remains unattached forever; all others run after worldly affairs.<br>
  He Himself is eternal, unchanging and unmoving; the others continue coming and going in reincarnation.<br>
  Meditating on the Lord forever and ever, the Gurmukh finds peace.<br>
  He dwells in the home of his own inner being, absorbed in the Praise of the True Lord.<br>
  The True Lord is profound and unfathomable; through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, He is understood. ||8||<br>
  Shalok, Third Mehl:<br>
  Meditate on the True Name; the True Lord is all-pervading.<br>
  O Nanak, one who realizes the Hukam of the Lord's Command, obtains the fruit of Truth.<br>
  One who merely mouths the words, does not understand the Hukam of the True Lord's Command.<br>
  O Nanak, one who accepts the Will of the Lord is His devotee. Without accepting it, he is the falsest of the false. ||1||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  The self-willed manmukhs do not know what they are saying. They are filled with sexual desire, anger and egotism.<br>
  They do not understand right places and wrong places; they are filled with greed and corruption.<br>
  They come, and sit and talk for their own purposes. The Messenger of Death strikes them down.<br>
  Hereafter, they are called to account in the Court of the Lord; the false ones are struck down and humiliated.<br>
  How can this filth of falsehood be washed off? Can anyone think about this, and find the way?<br>
  If one meets with the True Guru, He implants the Naam, the Name of the Lord within; all his sins are destroyed.<br>
  Let all bow in humility to that humble being who chants the Naam, and worships the Naam in adoration.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 076</h2></center>
  The Naam washes off the filth of falsehood; chanting the Naam, one becomes truthful.<br>
  O servant Nanak, wondrous are the plays of the Lord, the Giver of life. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  You are the Great Giver; no other is as great as You. Unto whom should I speak and talk?<br>
  By Guru's Grace, I find You; You eradicate egotism from within.<br>
  You are beyond sweet and salty flavors; True is Your glorious greatness.<br>
  You bless those whom You forgive, and unite them with Yourself.<br>
  You have placed the Ambrosial Nectar deep within the heart; the Gurmukh drinks it in. ||9||<br>
  Shalok, Third Mehl:<br>
  The stories of one's ancestors make the children good children.<br>
  They accept what is pleasing to the Will of the True Guru, and act accordingly.<br>
  Go and consult the Simritees, the Shaastras, the writings of Vyaas, Suk Dayv, Naarad, and all those who preach to the world.<br>
  Those, whom the True Lord attaches, are attached to the Truth; they contemplate the True Name forever.<br>
  O Nanak, their coming into the world is approved; they redeem all their ancestors. ||1||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  The disciples whose teacher is blind, act blindly as well.<br>
  They walk according to their own wills, and continually speak falsehood and lies.<br>
  They practice falsehood and deception, and endlessly slander others.<br>
  Slandering others, they drown themselves, and drown all their generations as well.<br>
  O Nanak, whatever the Lord links them to, to that they are linked; what can the poor creatures do? ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  He keeps all under His Gaze; He created the entire Universe.<br>
  He has linked some to falsehood and deception; these self-willed manmukhs are plundered.<br>
  The Gurmukhs meditate on the Lord forever; their inner beings are filled with love.<br>
  Those who have the treasure of virtue, chant the Praises of the Lord.<br>
  O Nanak, meditate on the Naam, and the Glorious Praises of the True Lord. ||10||<br>
  Shalok, First Mehl:<br>
  Men of charity gather wealth by committing sins, and then give it away in donations to charity.<br>
  Their spiritual teachers go to their homes to instruct them.<br>
  The woman loves the man only for his wealth;<br>
  they come and go as they please.<br>
  No one obeys the Shaastras or the Vedas.<br>
  Everyone worships himself.<br>
  Becoming judges, they sit and administer justice.<br>
  They chant on their malas, and call upon God.<br>
  They accept bribes, and block justice.<br>
  If someone asks them, they read quotations from their books.<br>
  The Muslim scriptures are in their ears and in their hearts.<br>
  They plunder the people, and engage in gossip and flattery.<br>
  They anoint their kitchens to try to become pure.<br>
  Behold, such is the Hindu.<br>
  The Yogi, with matted hair and ashes on his body, has become a householder.<br>
  The children weep in front of him and behind him.<br>
  He does not attain Yoga - he has lost his way.<br>
  Why does he apply ashes to his forehead?<br>
  O Nanak, this is the sign of the Dark Age of Kali Yuga;<br>
  everyone says that he himself knows. ||1||<br>
  First Mehl:<br>
  The Hindu comes to the house of a Hindu.<br>
  He puts the sacred thread around his neck and reads the scriptures.<br>
  He puts on the thread, but does evil deeds.<br>
  His cleansings and washings will not be approved.<br>
  The Muslim glorifies his own faith.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 077</h2></center>
  Without the Guru or a spiritual teacher, no one is accepted.<br>
  They may be shown the way, but only a few go there.<br>
  Without the karma of good actions, heaven is not attained.<br>
  The Way of Yoga is demonstrated in the Yogi's monastery.<br>
  They wear ear-rings to show the way.<br>
  Wearing ear-rings, they wander around the world.<br>
  The Creator Lord is everywhere.<br>
  There are as many travellers as there are beings.<br>
  When one's death warrant is issued, there is no delay.<br>
  One who knows the Lord here, realizes Him there as well.<br>
  Others, whether Hindu or Muslim, are just babbling.<br>
  Everyone's account is read in the Court of the Lord;<br>
  without the karma of good actions, no one crosses over.<br>
  One who speaks the True Name of the True Lord,<br>
  O Nanak, is not called to account hereafter. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  The fortress of the body is called the Mansion of the Lord.<br>
  The rubies and gems are found within it; the Gurmukh chants the Name of the Lord.<br>
  The body, the Mansion of the Lord, is very beautiful, when the Name of the Lord, Har, Har, is implanted deep within.<br>
  The self-willed manmukhs ruin themselves; they boil continuously in attachment to Maya.<br>
  The One Lord is the Master of all. He is found only by perfect destiny. ||11||<br>
  Shalok, First Mehl:<br>
  There is no Truth in suffering, there is no Truth in comfort. There is no Truth in wandering like animals through the water.<br>
  There is no Truth in shaving one's head; there is no Truth is studying the scriptures or wandering in foreign lands.<br>
  There is no Truth in trees, plants or stones, in mutilating oneself or suffering in pain.<br>
  There is no Truth in binding elephants in chains; there is no Truth in grazing cows.<br>
  He alone grants it, whose hands hold spritual perfection; he alone receives it, unto whom it is given.<br>
  O Nanak, he alone is blessed with glorious greatness, whose heart is filled with the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  God says, all hearts are mine, and I am in all hearts. Who can explain this to one who is confused?<br>
  Who can confuse that being, unto whom I have shown the Way?<br>
  And who can show the Path to that being whom I have confused since the beginning of time? ||1||<br>
  First Mehl:<br>
  He alone is a householder, who restrains his passions<br>
  and begs for meditation, austerity and self-discipline.<br>
  He gives donations to charity with his body;<br>
  such a householder is as pure as the water of the Ganges.<br>
  Says Eeshar, the Lord is the embodiment of Truth.<br>
  The supreme essence of reality has no shape or form. ||2||<br>
  First Mehl:<br>
  He alone is a detached hermit, who burns away his self-conceit.<br>
  He begs for suffering as his food.<br>
  In the city of the heart, he begs for charity.<br>
  Such a renunciate ascends to the City of God.<br>
  Says Gorakh, God is the embodiment of Truth;<br>
  the supreme essence of reality has no shape or form. ||3||<br>
  First Mehl:<br>
  He alone is an Udasi, a shaven-headed renunciate, who embraces renunciation.<br>
  He sees the Immaculate Lord dwelling in both the upper and lower regions.<br>
  He balances the sun and the moon energies.<br>
  The body-wall of such an Udasi does not collapse.<br>
  Says Gopi Chand, God is the embodiment of Truth;<br>
  the supreme essence of reality has no shape or form. ||4||<br>
  First Mehl:<br>
  He alone is a Paakhandi, who cleanses his body of filth.<br>
  The fire of his body illuminates God within.<br>
  He does not waste his energy in wet dreams.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 078</h2></center>
  Such a Paakhandi does not grow old or die.<br>
  Says Charpat, God is the embodiment of Truth;<br>
  the supreme essence of reality has no shape or form. ||5||<br>
  First Mehl:<br>
  He alone is a Bairaagi, who turns himself toward God.<br>
  In the Tenth Gate, the sky of the mind, he erects his pillar.<br>
  Night and day, he remains in deep inner meditation.<br>
  Such a Bairaagi is just like the True Lord.<br>
  Says Bhart'har, God is the embodiment of Truth;<br>
  the supreme essence of reality has no shape or form. ||6||<br>
  First Mehl:<br>
  How is evil eradicated? How can the true way of life be found?<br>
  What is the use of piercing the ears, or begging for food?<br>
  Throughout existence and non-existence, there is only the Name of the One Lord.<br>
  What is that Word, which holds the heart in its place?<br>
  When you look alike upon sunshine and shade,<br>
  says Nanak, then the Guru will speak to you.<br>
  The students follow the six systems.<br>
  They are neither worldly people, nor detached renunciates.<br>
  One who remains absorbed in the Formless Lord<br>
  - why should he go out begging? ||7||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  That alone is said to be the Lord's temple, where the Lord is known.<br>
  In the human body, the Guru's Word is found, when one understands that the Lord, the Supreme Soul, is in all.<br>
  Don't look for Him outside your self. The Creator, the Architect of Destiny, is within the home of your own heart.<br>
  The self-willed manmukh does not appreciate the value of the Lord's temple; they waste away and lose their lives.<br>
  The One Lord is pervading in all; through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, He can be found. ||12||<br>
  Shalok, Third Mehl:<br>
  Only a fool listens to the words of the fool.<br>
  What are the signs of the fool? What does the fool do?<br>
  A fool is stupid; he dies of egotism.<br>
  His actions always bring him pain; he lives in pain.<br>
  If someone's beloved friend falls into the pit, what can be used to pull him out?<br>
  One who becomes Gurmukh contemplates the Lord, and remains detached.<br>
  Chanting the Lord's Name, he saves himself, and he carries across those who are drowning as well.<br>
  O Nanak, he acts in accordance with the Will of God; he endures whatever he is given. ||1||<br>
  First Mehl:<br>
  Says Nanak, listen, O mind, to the True Teachings.<br>
  Opening His ledger, God will call you to account.<br>
  Those rebels who have unpaid accounts shall be called out.<br>
  Azraa-eel, the Angel of Death, shall be appointed to punish them.<br>
  They will find no way to escape coming and going in reincarnation; they are trapped in the narrow path.<br>
  Falsehood will come to an end, O Nanak, and Truth will prevail in the end. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  The body and everything belongs to the Lord; the Lord Himself is all-pervading.<br>
  The Lord's value cannot be estimated; nothing can be said about it.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, one praises the Lord, imbued with feelings of devotion.<br>
  The mind and body are totally rejuvenated, and egotism is eradicated.<br>
  Everything is the play of the Lord. The Gurmukh understands this. ||13||<br>
  Shalok, First Mehl:<br>
  Branded with a thousand marks of disgrace, Indra cried in shame.<br>
  Paras Raam returned home crying.<br>
  Ajai cried and wept, when he was made to eat the manure he had given, pretending it was charity.<br>
  Such is the punishment received in the Court of the Lord.<br>
  Rama wept when he was sent into exile,<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 079</h2></center>
  and separated from Sita and Lakhshman.<br>
  The ten-headed Raawan, who stole away Sita with the beat of his tambourine, wept when he lost Sri Lanka.<br>
  The Paandavas once lived in the Presence of the Lord; they were made slaves, and wept.<br>
  Janmayjaa wept, that he had lost his way.<br>
  One mistake, and he became a sinner.<br>
  The Shaykhs, Pirs and spiritual teachers weep;<br>
  at the very last instant, they suffer in agony.<br>
  The kings weep - their ears are cut;<br>
  they go begging from house to house.<br>
  The miser weeps; he has to leave behind the wealth he has gathered.<br>
  The Pandit, the religious scholar, weeps when his learning is gone.<br>
  The young woman weeps because she has no husband.<br>
  O Nanak, the whole world is suffering.<br>
  He alone is victorious, who believes in the Lord's Name.<br>
  No other action is of any account. ||1||<br>
  Second Mehl:<br>
  Meditation, austerity and everything come through belief in the Lord's Name. All other actions are useless.<br>
  O Nanak, believe in the One who is worth believing in. By Guru's Grace, he is realized. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  The union of the body and the soul-swan was pre-ordained by the Creator Lord.<br>
  He is hidden, and yet pervading all. He is revealed to the Gurmukh.<br>
  Singing the Glorious Praises of the Lord, and chanting His Praises, one merges in His Glories.<br>
  True is the True Word of the Guru's Bani. One unites in Union with the True Lord.<br>
  He Himself is everything; He Himself grants glorious greatness. ||14||<br>
  Shalok, Second Mehl:<br>
  O Nanak, the blind man may go to appraise the jewels,<br>
  but he will not know their value; he will return home after exposing his ignorance. ||1||<br>
  Second Mehl:<br>
  The Jeweller has come, and opened up the bag of jewels.<br>
  The merchandise and the merchant are merged together.<br>
  They alone purchase the gem, O Nanak, who have virtue in their purse.<br>
  Those who do not appreciate the value of the jewels, wander like blind men in the world. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  The fortress of the body has nine gates; the tenth gate is kept hidden.<br>
  The rigid door is not open; only through the Word of the Guru's Shabad can it be opened.<br>
  The unstruck sound current resounds and vibrates there. The Word of the Guru's Shabad is heard.<br>
  Deep within the nucleus of the heart, the Divine Light shines forth. Through devotional worship, one meets the Lord.<br>
  The One Lord is pervading and permeating all. He Himself created the creation. ||15||<br>
  Shalok, Second Mehl:<br>
  He is truly blind, who follows the way shown by the blind man.<br>
  O Nanak, why should the one who can see, get lost?<br>
  Do not call them blind, who have no eyes in their face.<br>
  They alone are blind, O Nanak, who wander away from their Lord and Master. ||1||<br>
  Second Mehl:<br>
  One whom the Lord has made blind - the Lord can make him see again.<br>
  He acts only as he knows, although he may be spoken to a hundred times.<br>
  Where the real thing is not seen, self-conceit prevails there - know this well.<br>
  O Nanak, how can the purshaser purchase the real thing, if he cannot recognize it? ||2||<br>
  Second Mehl:<br>
  How can someone be called blind, if he was made blind by the Lord's Command?<br>
  O Nanak, one who does not understand the Hukam of the Lord's Command should be called blind. ||3||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 080</h2></center>
  Pauree:<br>
  Deep within the body is the fortress of the Lord, and all lands and countries.<br>
  He Himself sits in primal, profound Samaadhi; He Himself is all-pervading.<br>
  He Himself created the Universe, and He Himself remains hidden within it.<br>
  Serving the Guru, the Lord is known, and the Truth is revealed.<br>
  He is True, the Truest of the True; the Guru has imparted this understanding. ||16||<br>
  Shalok, First Mehl:<br>
  Night is the summer season, and day is the winter season; sexual desire and anger are the two fields planted.<br>
  Greed prepares the soil, and the seed of falsehood is planted; attachment and love are the farmer and hired hand.<br>
  Contemplation is the plow, and corruption is the harvest; this is what one earns and eats, according to the Hukam of the Lord's Command.<br>
  O Nanak, when one is called to give his account, he will be barren and infertile. ||1||<br>
  First Mehl:<br>
  Make the Fear of God the farm, purity the water, truth and contentment the cows and bulls,<br>
  humility the plow, consciousness the plowman, remembrance the preparation of the soil, and union with the Lord the planting time.<br>
  Let the Lord's Name be the seed, and His Forgiving Grace the harvest. Do this, and the whole world will seem false.<br>
  O Nanak, if He bestows His Merciful Glance of Grace, then all your separation will be ended. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  The self-willed manmukh is trapped in the darkness of emotional attachment; in the love of duality he speaks.<br>
  The love of duality brings pain forever; he churns the water endlessly.<br>
  The Gurmukh meditates on the Naam, the Name of the Lord; he churns, and obtains the essence of reality.<br>
  The Divine Light illuminates his heart deep within; he seeks the Lord, and obtains Him.<br>
  He Himself deludes in doubt; no one can comment on this. ||17||<br>
  Shalok, Second Mehl:<br>
  O Nanak, don't be anxious; the Lord will take care of you.<br>
  He created the creatures in water, and He gives them their nourishment.<br>
  There are no stores open there, and no one farms there.<br>
  No business is ever transacted there, and no one buys or sells.<br>
  Animals eat other animals; this is what the Lord has given them as food.<br>
  He created them in the oceans, and He provides for them as well.<br>
  O Nanak, don't be anxious; the Lord will take care of you. ||1||<br>
  First Mehl:<br>
  O Nanak, this soul is the fish, and death is the hungry fisherman.<br>
  The blind man does not even think of this. And suddenly, the net is cast.<br>
  O Nanak, his consciousness is unconscious, and he departs, bound by anxiety.<br>
  But if the Lord bestows His Glance of Grace, then He unites the soul with Himself. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  They are true, forever true, who drink in the sublime essence of the Lord.<br>
  The True Lord abides in the mind of the Gurmukh; He strikes the true bargain.<br>
  Everything is in the home of the self within; only the very fortunate obtain it.<br>
  The hunger within is conquered and overcome, singing the Glorious Praises of the Lord.<br>
  He Himself unites in His Union; He Himself blesses them with understanding. ||18||<br>
  Shalok, First Mehl:<br>
  The cotton is ginned, woven and spun;<br>
  the cloth is laid out, washed and bleached white.<br>
  The tailor cuts it with his scissors, and sews it with his thread.<br>
  Thus, the torn and tattered honor is sewn up again, through the Lord's Praise, O Nanak, and one lives the true life.<br>
  Becoming worn, the cloth is torn; with needle and thread it is sewn up again.<br>
  It will not last for a month, or even a week. It barely lasts for an hour, or even a moment.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 081</h2></center>
  But the Truth does not grow old; and when it is stitched, it is never torn again.<br>
  O Nanak, the Lord and Master is the Truest of the True. While we meditate on Him, we see Him. ||1||<br>
  First Mehl:<br>
  The knife is Truth, and its steel is totally True.<br>
  Its workmanship is incomparably beautiful.<br>
  It is sharpened on the grindstone of the Shabad.<br>
  It is placed in the scabbard of virtue.<br>
  If the Shaykh is killed with that,<br>
  then the blood of greed will spill out.<br>
  One who is slaughtered in this ritualistic way, will be attached to the Lord.<br>
  O Nanak, at the Lord's door, he is absorbed into His Blessed Vision. ||2||<br>
  First Mehl:<br>
  A beautiful dagger hangs by your waist, and you ride such a beautiful horse.<br>
  But don't be too proud; O Nanak, you may fall head first to the ground. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  They alone walk as Gurmukh, who receive the Shabad in the Sat Sangat, the True Congregation.<br>
  Meditating on the True Lord, they become truthful; they carry in their robes the supplies of the Lord's wealth.<br>
  The devotees look beautiful, singing the Praises of the Lord; following the Guru's Teachings, they become stable and unchanging.<br>
  They enshrine the jewel of contemplation within their minds, and the most sublime Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  He Himself unites in His Union; He Himself grants glorious greatness. ||19||<br>
  Shalok, Third Mehl:<br>
  Everyone is filled with hope; hardly anyone is free of hope.<br>
  O Nanak, blessed is the birth of one, who remains dead while yet alive. ||1||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  Nothing is in the hands of hope. How can one become free of hope?<br>
  What can this poor being do? The Lord Himself creates confusion. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  Cursed is the life in this world, without the True Name.<br>
  God is the Great Giver of givers. His wealth is permanent and unchanging.<br>
  That humble being is immaculate, who worships the Lord with each and every breath.<br>
  With your tongue, vibrate the One Inaccessible Lord, the Inner-knower, the Searcher of hearts.<br>
  He is all-pervading everywhere. Nanak is a sacrifice to Him. ||20||<br>
  Shalok, First Mehl:<br>
  The union between the lake of the True Guru, and the swan of the soul, was pre-ordained from the very beginning, by the Pleasure of the Lord's Will.<br>
  The diamonds are in this lake; they are the food of the swans.<br>
  The cranes and the ravens may be very wise, but they do not remain in this lake.<br>
  They do not find their food there; their food is different.<br>
  Practicing Truth, the True Lord is found. False is the pride of the false.<br>
  O Nanak, they alone meet the True Guru, who are so pre-destined by the Lord's Command. ||1||<br>
  First Mehl:<br>
  My Lord and Master is immaculate, as are those who think of Him.<br>
  O Nanak, serve Him, who gives to you forever and ever.<br>
  O Nanak, serve Him; by serving Him, sorrow is dispelled.<br>
  Faults and demerits vanish, and virtues take their place; peace comes to dwell in the mind. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  He Himself is all-pervading; He Himself is absorbed in the profound state of Samaadhi.<br>
  He Himself instructs; the Gurmukh is satisfied and fulfilled.<br>
  Some, He causes to wander in the wilderness, while others are committed to His devotional worship.<br>
  He alone understands, whom the Lord causes to understand; He Himself attaches mortals to His Name.<br>
  O Nanak, meditating on the Naam, the Name of the Lord, true greatness is obtained. ||21||1||<br>
  Sudh||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 082</h2></center>
  Vaar Of Raamkalee, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Shalok, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  As I have heard of the True Guru, so I have seen Him.<br>
  He re-unites the separated ones with God; He is the Mediator at the Court of the Lord.<br>
  He implants the Mantra of the Lord's Name, and eradicates the illness of egotism.<br>
  O Nanak, he alone meets the True Guru, who has such union pre-ordained. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  If the One Lord is my Friend, then all are my friends. If the One Lord is my enemy, then all fight with me.<br>
  The Perfect Guru has shown me that, without the Name, everything is useless.<br>
  The faithless cynics and the evil people wander in reincarnation; they are attached to other tastes.<br>
  Servant Nanak has realized the Lord God, by the Grace of the Guru, the True Guru. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  The Creator Lord created the Creation.<br>
  He Himself is the perfect Banker; He Himself earns His profit.<br>
  He Himself made the expansive Universe; He Himself is imbued with joy.<br>
  The value of God's almighty creative power cannot be estimated.<br>
  He is inaccessible, unfathomable, endless, the farthest of the far.<br>
  He Himself is the greatest Emperor; He Himself is His own Prime Minister.<br>
  No one knows His worth, or the greatness of His resting place.<br>
  He Himself is our True Lord and Master. He reveals Himself to the Gurmukh. ||1||<br>
  Shalok, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Listen, O my beloved friend: please show me the True Guru.<br>
  I dedicate my mind to Him; I keep Him continually enshrined within my heart.<br>
  Without the One and Only True Guru, life in this world is cursed.<br>
  O servant Nanak, they alone meet the True Guru, with whom He constantly abides. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Deep within me is the longing to meet You; how can I find You, God?<br>
  I will search for someone, some friend, who will unite me with my Beloved.<br>
  The Perfect Guru has united me with Him; wherever I look, there He is.<br>
  Servant Nanak serves that God; there is no other as great as He is. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  He is the Great Giver, the Generous Lord; with what mouth can I praise Him?<br>
  In His Mercy, He protects, preserves and sustains us.<br>
  No one is under anyone else's control; He is the One Support of all.<br>
  He cherishes all as His children, and reaches out with His hand.<br>
  He stages His joyous plays, which no one understands at all.<br>
  The all-powerful Lord gives His Support to all; I am a sacrifice to Him.<br>
  Night and day, sing the Praises of the One who is worthy of being praised.<br>
  Those who fall at the Guru's Feet, enjoy the sublime essence of the Lord. ||2||<br>
  Shalok, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  He has widened the narrow path for me, and preserved my integrity, along with that of my family.<br>
  He Himself has arranged and resolved my affairs. I dwell upon that God forever.<br>
  God is my mother and father; He hugs me close in His embrace, and cherishes me, like His tiny baby.<br>
  All beings and creatures have become kind and compassionate to me. O Nanak, the Lord has blessed me with His Glance of Grace. ||1||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 083</h2></center>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  To ask for any other than You, Lord, is the most miserable of miseries.<br>
  Please bless me with Your Name, and make me content; may the hunger of my mind be satisfied.<br>
  The Guru has made the woods and meadows green again. O Nanak, is it any wonder that He blesses human beings as well? ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  Such is that Great Giver; may I never forget Him from my mind.<br>
  I cannot survive without Him, for an instant, for a moment, for a second.<br>
  Inwardly and outwardly, He is with us; how can we hide anything from Him?<br>
  One whose honor He Himself has preserved, crosses over the terrifying world-ocean.<br>
  He alone is a devotee, a spiritual teacher, and a disciplined pratictioner of meditation, whom the Lord has so blessed.<br>
  He alone is perfect and renowned as supreme, whom the Lord has blessed with His power.<br>
  He alone endures the unendurable, whom the Lord inspires to endure it.<br>
  And he alone meets the True Lord, within whose mind the Guru's Mantra is implanted. ||3||<br>
  Shalok, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Blessed are those beautiful Ragas which, when chanted, quench all thirst.<br>
  Blessed are those beautiful people who, as Gurmukh, chant the Name of the Lord.<br>
  I am a sacrifice to those who single-mindedly worship and adore the One Lord.<br>
  I yearn for the dust of their feet; by His Grace, it is obtained.<br>
  I am a sacrifice to those who are imbued with love for the Lord of the Universe.<br>
  I tell them the state of my soul, and pray that I may be united with the Sovereign Lord King, my Friend.<br>
  The Perfect Guru has united me with Him, and the pains of birth and death have departed.<br>
  Servant Nanak has found the inaccessible, infinitely beautiful Lord, and he will not go anywhere else. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Blessed is that time, blessed is that hour, blessed is that second, excellent is that instant;<br>
  blessed is that day, and that opportunity, when I gazed upon the Blessed Vision of the Guru's Darshan.<br>
  The mind's desires are fulfilled, when the inaccessible, unfathomable Lord is obtained.<br>
  Egotism and emotional attachment are eradicated, and one leans only on the Support of the True Name.<br>
  O servant Nanak, one who is committed to the Lord's service - the whole world is saved along with him. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  How rare are those who are blessed to praise the Lord, in devotional worship.<br>
  Those who are blessed with the Lord's treasures are not called to give their account again.<br>
  Those who are imbued with His Love are absorbed in ecstasy.<br>
  They take the Support of the One Name; the One Name is their only food.<br>
  For their sake, the world eats and enjoys.<br>
  Their Beloved Lord belongs to them alone.<br>
  The Guru comes and meets them; they alone know God.<br>
  I am a sacrifice to those who are pleasing to their Lord and Master. ||4||<br>
  Shalok, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  My friendship is with the One Lord alone; I am in love with the One Lord alone.<br>
  The Lord is my only friend; my companionship is with the One Lord alone.<br>
  My conversation is with the One Lord alone; He never frowns, or turns His face away.<br>
  He alone knows the state of my soul; He never ignores my love.<br>
  He is my only counselor, all-powerful to destroy and create.<br>
  The Lord is my only Giver. He places His hand upon the heads of the generous in the world.<br>
  I take the Support of the One Lord alone; He is all-powerful, over the heads of all.<br>
  The Saint, the True Guru, has united me with the Lord. He placed His hand on my forehead.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 084</h2></center>
  The Guru led me to meet the greatest Lord and Master; He saved the whole world.<br>
  The desires of the mind are fulfilled; I have attained my pre-destined Union with God.<br>
  Nanak has obtained the True Name; He enjoys the enjoyments forever. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Friendship with the self-willed manmukhs is an alliance with Maya.<br>
  As we watch, they run away; they never stand firm.<br>
  As long as they get food and clothing, they stick around.<br>
  But on that day when they receive nothing, then they start to curse.<br>
  The self-willed manmukhs are ignorant and blind; they do not know the secrets of the soul.<br>
  The false bond does not last; it is like stones joined with mud.<br>
  The blind do not understand themselves; they are engrossed in false worldly entanglements.<br>
  Entangled in false attachments, they pass their lives in egotism and self-conceit.<br>
  But that being, whom the Lord has blessed with His Mercy from the very beginning, does perfect deeds, and accumulates good karma.<br>
  O servant Nanak, those humble beings alone are saved, who enter the Sanctuary of the True Guru. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  Those who are imbued with the Lord's Vision, speak the Truth.<br>
  How can I obtain the dust of those who realize their Lord and Master?<br>
  The mind, stained by corruption, becomes pure by associating with them.<br>
  One sees the Mansion of the Lord's Presence, when the door of doubt is opened.<br>
  That one, unto whom the Mansion of the Lord's Presence is revealed, is never pushed or shoved.<br>
  My mind and body are enraptured, when the Lord blesses me, even for an instant, with His Glance of Grace.<br>
  The nine treasures, and the treasure of the Naam are obtained by commitment to the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  He alone is blessed with the dust of the feet of the Saints, upon whose forehead such pre-ordained desiny is inscribed. ||5||<br>
  Shalok, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  O deer-eyed bride, I speak the Truth, which shall save you.<br>
  Listen to these beautiful words, O beauteous bride; your Beloved Lord is your mind's only support.<br>
  You have fallen in love with an evil person; tell me - show me why!<br>
  I lack nothing, and I am not sad or depressed; I have no deficiency at all.<br>
  I abandoned and lost my fascinating and beautiful Husband Lord; in this evil-mindedness, I have lost my good fortune.<br>
  I am not mistaken, and I am not confused; I have no egotism, and commit no offense.<br>
  As You have linked me, so I am linked; listen to my true message.<br>
  She alone is the blessed soul-bride, and she alone is fortunate, upon whom the Husband Lord has showered His Mercy.<br>
  Her Husband Lord takes away all her faults and mistakes; hugging her close in His embrace, He embellishes her.<br>
  The unfortunate soul-bride makes this prayer: O Nanak, when will my turn come?<br>
  All the blessed soul-brides celebrate and make merry; bless me as well with a night of bliss, O Lord. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Why do you waver, O my mind? The Lord is the Fulfiller of hopes and desires.<br>
  Meditate on the True Guru, the Primal Being; He is the Destroyer of all pains.<br>
  Worship and adore the Lord's Name, O my mind; all sins and corruption shall be washed away.<br>
  Those who are blessed with such pre-ordained destiny, are in love with the Formless Lord.<br>
  They abandon the tastes of Maya, and gather in the infinite wealth of the Naam.<br>
  Twenty-four hours a day, they are lovingly absorbed in the One Lord; they surrender and accept the Will of the Infinite Lord.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 085</h2></center>
  Servant Nanak begs for this one gift: please bless me, Lord, with the Blessed Vision of Your Darshan; my mind is in love with You. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  One who is conscious of You finds everlasting peace.<br>
  One who is conscious of You does not suffer at the hands of the Messenger of Death.<br>
  One who is conscious of You is not anxious.<br>
  One who has the Creator as his Friend - all his affairs are resolved.<br>
  One who is conscious of You is renowned and respected.<br>
  One who is conscious of You becomes very wealthy.<br>
  One who is conscious of You has a great family.<br>
  One who is conscious of You saves his ancestors. ||6||<br>
  Shalok, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Blind inwardly, and blind outwardly, he sings falsely, falsely.<br>
  He washes his body, and draws ritual marks on it, and totally runs after wealth.<br>
  But the filth of his egotism is not removed from within, and over and over again, he comes and goes in reincarnation.<br>
  Engulfed in sleep, and tormented by frustrated sexual desire, he chants the Lord's Name with his mouth.<br>
  He is called a Vaishnav, but he is bound to deeds of egotism; by threshing only husks, what rewards can be obtained?<br>
  Sitting among the swans, the crane does not become one of them; sitting there, he keeps staring at the fish.<br>
  And when the gathering of swans looks and sees, they realize that they can never form an alliance with the crane.<br>
  The swans peck at the diamonds and pearls, while the crane chases after frogs.<br>
  The poor crane flies away, so that his secret will not be exposed.<br>
  Whatever the Lord attaches one to, to that he is attached. Who is to blame, when the Lord wills it so?<br>
  The True Guru is the lake, overflowing with pearls. One who meets the True Guru obtains them.<br>
  The Sikh-swans gather at the lake, according to the Will of the True Guru.<br>
  The lake is filled with the wealth of these jewels and pearls; they are spent and consumed, but they never run out.<br>
  The swan never leaves the lake; such is the Pleasure of the Creator's Will.<br>
  O servant Nanak, one who has such pre-ordained destiny inscribed upon his forehead - that Sikh comes to the Guru.<br>
  He saves himself, and saves all his generations as well; he emancipates the whole world. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  He is called a Pandit, a religious scholar, and yet he wanders along many pathways. He is as hard as uncooked beans.<br>
  He is filled with attachment, and constantly engrossed in doubt; his body cannot hold still.<br>
  False is his coming, and false is his going; he is continually on the lookout for Maya.<br>
  If someone speaks the truth, then he is aggravated; he is totally filled with anger.<br>
  The evil fool is engrossed in evil-mindedness and false intellectualizations; his mind is attached to emotional attachment.<br>
  The deceiver abides with the five deceivers; it is a gathering of like minds.<br>
  And when the Jeweller, the True Guru, appraises him, then he is exposed as mere iron.<br>
  Mixed and mingled with others, he was passed off as genuine in many places; but now, the veil has been lifted, and he stands naked before all.<br>
  One who comes to the Sanctuary of the True Guru, shall be transformed from iron into gold.<br>
  The True Guru has no anger or vengeance; He looks upon son and enemy alike. Removing faults and mistakes, He purifies the human body.<br>
  O Nanak, one who has such pre-ordained destiny inscribed upon his forehead, is in love with the True Guru.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 086</h2></center>
  The Word of the Perfect True Guru's Bani is Ambrosial Nectar; it dwells in the heart of one who is blessed by the Guru's Mercy.<br>
  His coming and going in reincarnation is ended; forever and ever, he is at peace. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  He alone understands You, Lord, with whom You are pleased.<br>
  He alone is approved in the Court of the Lord, with whom You are pleased.<br>
  Egotism is eradicated, when You bestow Your Grace.<br>
  Sins are erased, when You are thoroughly pleased.<br>
  One who has the Lord Master on his side, becomes fearless.<br>
  One who is blessed with Your Mercy, becomes truthful.<br>
  One who is blessed with Your Kindness, is not touched by fire.<br>
  You are forever Merciful to those who are receptive to the Guru's Teachings. ||7||<br>
  Shalok, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Please grant Your Grace, O Merciful Lord; please forgive me.<br>
  Forever and ever, I chant Your Name; I fall at the feet of the True Guru.<br>
  Please, dwell within my mind and body, and end my sufferings.<br>
  Please give me Your hand, and save me, that fear may not afflict me.<br>
  May I sing Your Glorious Praises day and night; please commit me to this task.<br>
  Associating with the humble Saints, the disease of egotism is eradicated.<br>
  The One Lord and Master is all-pervading, permeating everywhere.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, I have truly found the Truest of the True.<br>
  Please bless me with Your Kindness, O Kind Lord, and bless me with Your Praises.<br>
  Gazing upon the Blessed Vision of Your Darshan, I am in ecstasy; this is what Nanak loves. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Meditate on the One Lord within your mind, and enter the Sanctuary of the One Lord alone.<br>
  Be in love with the One Lord; there is no other at all.<br>
  Beg from the One Lord, the Great Giver, and you will be blessed with everything.<br>
  In your mind and body, with each breath and morsel of food, meditate on the One and only Lord God.<br>
  The Gurmukh obtains the true treasure, the Ambrosial Naam, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  Very fortunate are those humble Saints, within whose minds the Lord has come to abide.<br>
  He is pervading and permeating the water, the land and the sky; there is no other at all.<br>
  Meditating on the Naam, and chanting the Naam, Nanak abides in the Will of his Lord and Master. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  One who has You as his Saving Grace - who can kill him?<br>
  One who has You as his Saving Grace conquers the three worlds.<br>
  One who has You on his side - his face is radiant and bright.<br>
  One who has You on his side, is the purest of the Pure.<br>
  One who is blessed with Your Grace is not called to give his account.<br>
  One with whom You are pleased, obtains the nine treasures.<br>
  One who has You on his side, God - unto whom is he subservient?<br>
  One who is blessed with Your Kind Mercy is dedicated to Your worship. ||8||<br>
  Shalok, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Be Merciful, O my Lord and Master, that I may pass my life in the Society of the Saints.<br>
  Those who forget You are born only to die and be reincarnated again; their sufferings will never end. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Meditate in remembrance within your heart on the True Guru, whether you are on the most difficult path, on the mountain or by the river bank.<br>
  Chanting the Name of the Lord, Har, Har, no one shall block your way. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 087</h2></center>
  Where You are, Almighty Lord, there is no one else.<br>
  There, in the fire of the mother's womb, You protected us.<br>
  Hearing Your Name, the Messenger of Death runs away.<br>
  The terrifying, treacherous, impassible world-ocean is crossed over, through the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  Those who feel thirst for You, take in Your Ambrosial Nectar.<br>
  This is the only act of goodness in this Dark Age of Kali Yuga, to sing the Glorious Praises of the Lord of the Universe.<br>
  He is Merciful to all; He sustains us with each and every breath.<br>
  Those who come to You with love and faith are never turned away empty-handed. ||9||<br>
  Shalok, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Those whom You bless with the Support of Your Name, O Supreme Lord God, do not know any other.<br>
  Inaccessible, Unfathomable Lord and Master, All-powerful True Great Giver:<br>
  You are eternal and unchanging, without vengeance and True; True is the Darbaar of Your Court.<br>
  Your worth cannot be described; You have no end or limitation.<br>
  To forsake God, and ask for something else, is all corruption and ashes.<br>
  They alone find peace, and they are the true kings, whose dealings are true.<br>
  Those who are in love with God's Name, intuitively enjoy the essence of peace.<br>
  Nanak worships and adores the One Lord; he seeks the dust of the Saints. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Singing the Kirtan of the Lord's Praises, bliss, peace and rest are obtained.<br>
  Forsake other clever tricks, O Nanak; only through the Name will you be saved. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  No one can bring You under control, by despising the world.<br>
  No one can bring You under control, by studying the Vedas.<br>
  No one can bring You under control, by bathing at the holy places.<br>
  No one can bring You under control, by wandering all over the world.<br>
  No one can bring You under control, by any clever tricks.<br>
  No one can bring You under control, by giving huge donations to charities.<br>
  Everyone is under Your power, O inaccessible, unfathomable Lord.<br>
  You are under the control of Your devotees; You are the strength of Your devotees. ||10||<br>
  Shalok, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The Lord Himself is the true physician.<br>
  These physicians of the world only burden the soul with pain.<br>
  The Word of the Guru's Shabad is Ambrosial Nectar; it is so delicious to eat.<br>
  O Nanak, one whose mind is filled with this Nectar - all his pains are dispelled. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  By the Hukam of Lord's Command, they move about; by the Lord's Command, they remain still.<br>
  By His Hukam, they endure pain and pleasure alike.<br>
  By His Hukam, they chant the Naam, the Name of the Lord, day and night.<br>
  O Nanak, he alone does so, who is blessed.<br>
  By the Hukam of the Lord's Command, they die; by the Hukam of His Command, they live.<br>
  By His Hukam, they become tiny, and huge.<br>
  By His Hukam, they receive pain, happiness and bliss.<br>
  By His Hukam, they chant the Guru's Mantra, which always works.<br>
  By His Hukam, coming and going in reincarnation cease,<br>
  O Nanak, when He links them to His devotional worship. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  I am a sacrifice to that musician who is Your servant, O Lord.<br>
  I am a sacrifice to that musician who sings the Glorious Praises of the Infinite Lord.<br>
  Blessed, blessed is that musician, for whom the Formless Lord Himself longs.<br>
  Very fortunate is that musician who comes to the gate of the Court of the True Lord.<br>
  That musician meditates on You, Lord, and praises You day and night.<br>
  He begs for the Ambrosial Naam, the Name of the Lord, and will never be defeated.<br>
  His clothes and his food are true, and he enshrines love for the Lord within.<br>
  Praiseworthy is that musician who loves God. ||11||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 088</h2></center>
  Shalok, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The Bani of the Guru's Word is Ambrosial Nectar; its taste is sweet. The Name of the Lord is Ambrosial Nectar.<br>
  Meditate in remembrance on the Lord in your mind, body and heart; twenty-four hours a day, sing His Glorious Praises.<br>
  Listen to these Teachings, O Sikhs of the Guru. This is the true purpose of life.<br>
  This priceless human life will be made fruitful; embrace love for the Lord in your mind.<br>
  Celestial peace and absolute bliss come when one meditates on God - suffering is dispelled.<br>
  O Nanak, chanting the Naam, the Name of the Lord, peace wells up, and one obtains a place in the Court of the Lord. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  O Nanak, meditate on the Naam, the Name of the Lord; this is the Teaching imparted by the Perfect Guru.<br>
  In the Lord's Will, they practice meditation, austerity and self-discipline; in the Lord's Will, they are released.<br>
  In the Lord's Will, they are made to wander in reincarnation; in the Lord's Will, they are forgiven.<br>
  In the Lord's Will, pain and pleasure are experienced; in the Lord's Will, actions are performed.<br>
  In the Lord's Will, clay is fashioned into form; in the Lord's Will, His Light is infused into it.<br>
  In the Lord's Will, enjoyments are enjoyed; in the Lord's Will, these enjoyments are denied.<br>
  In the Lord's Will, they are incarnated in heaven and hell; in the Lord's Will, they fall to the ground.<br>
  In the Lord's Will, they are committed to His devotional worship and Praise; O Nanak, how rare are these! ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  Hearing, hearing of the glorious greatness of the True Name, I live.<br>
  Even ignorant beasts and goblins can be saved, in an instant.<br>
  Day and night, chant the Name, forever and ever.<br>
  The most horrible thirst and hunger is satisfied through Your Name, O Lord.<br>
  Disease, sorrow and pain run away, when the Name dwells within the mind.<br>
  He alone attains his Beloved, who loves the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  The worlds and solar systems are saved by the Infinite Lord.<br>
  Your glory is Yours alone, O my Beloved True Lord. ||12||<br>
  Shalok, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  I abandoned and lost my Beloved Friend, O Nanak; I was fooled by the transitory color of the safflower, which fades away.<br>
  I did not know Your value, O my Friend; without You, I am not worth even half a shell. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  My mother-in-law is my enemy, O Nanak; my father-in-law is argumentative and my brother-in-law burns me at every step.<br>
  They can all just play in the dust, when You are my Friend, O Lord. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  You relieve the pains of those, within whose consciousness You dwell, O Lord.<br>
  Those, within whose consciousness You dwell, never lose.<br>
  One who meets the Perfect Guru will surely be saved.<br>
  One who is attached to Truth, contemplates Truth.<br>
  One, into whose hands the treasure comes, stops searching.<br>
  He alone is known as a devotee, who loves the One Lord.<br>
  He is the dust under the feet of all; he is the lover of the Lord's feet.<br>
  Everything is Your wonderful play; the whole creation is Yours. ||13||<br>
  Shalok, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  I have totally discarded praise and slander, O Nanak; I have forsaken and abandoned everything.<br>
  I have seen that all relationships are false, and so I have grasped hold of the hem of Your robe, Lord. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  I wandered and wandered and went crazy, O Nanak, in countless foreign lands and pathways.<br>
  But then, I slept in peace and comfort, when I met the Guru, and found my Friend. ||2||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 089</h2></center>
  Pauree:<br>
  When I forget You, I endure all pains and afflictions.<br>
  Making thousands of efforts, they are still not eliminated.<br>
  One who forgets the Name, is known as a poor person.<br>
  One who forgets the Name, wanders in reincarnation.<br>
  One who does not remember his Lord and Master, is punished by the Messenger of Death.<br>
  One who does not remember his Lord and Master, is judged to be a sick person.<br>
  One who does not remember his Lord and Master, is egotistical and proud.<br>
  One who forgets the Name is miserable in this world. ||14||<br>
  Shalok, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  I have not seen any other like You. You alone are pleasing to Nanak's mind.<br>
  I am a dedicated, devoted sacrifice to that friend, that mediator, who leads me to recognize my Husband Lord. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Beautiful are those feet which walk towards You; beautiful is that head which falls at Your Feet.<br>
  Beautiful is that mouth which sings Your Praises; beautiful is that soul which seeks Your Sanctuary. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  Meeting the Lord's brides, in the True Congregation, I sing the songs of joy.<br>
  The home of my heart is now held steady, and I shall not go out wandering again.<br>
  Evil-mindedness has been dispelled, along with sin and my bad reputation.<br>
  I am well-known as being calm and good-natured; my heart is filled with Truth.<br>
  Inwardly and outwardly, the One and only Lord is my way.<br>
  My mind is thirsty for the Blessed Vision of His Darshan. I am a slave at His feet.<br>
  I am glorified and embellished, when my Lord and Master enjoys me.<br>
  I meet Him through my blessed destiny, when it is pleasing to His Will. ||15||<br>
  Shalok, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  All virtues are Yours, Dear Lord; You bestow them upon us. I am unworthy - what can I achieve, O Nanak?<br>
  There is no other Giver as great as You. I am a beggar; I beg from You forever. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  My body was wasting away, and I was depressed. The Guru, my Friend, has encouraged and consoled me.<br>
