  I sleep in total peace and comfort; I have conquered the whole world. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  The Darbaar of Your Court is glorious and great. Your holy throne is True.<br>
  You are the Emperor over the heads of kings. Your canopy and chauree (fly-brush) are permanent and unchanging.<br>
  That alone is true justice, which is pleasing to the Will of the Supreme Lord God.<br>
  Even the homeless receive a home, when it is pleasing to the Will of the Supreme Lord God.<br>
  Whatever the Creator Lord does, is a good thing.<br>
  Those who recognize their Lord and Master, are seated in the Court of the Lord.<br>
  True is Your Command; no one can challenge it.<br>
  O Merciful Lord, Cause of causes, Your creative power is all-powerful. ||16||<br>
  Shalok, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Hearing of You, my body and mind have blossomed forth; chanting the Naam, the Name of the Lord, I am flushed with life.<br>
  Walking on the Path, I have found cool tranquility deep within; gazing upon the Blessed Vision of the Guru's Darshan, I am enraptured. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  I have found the jewel within my heart.<br>
  I was not charged for it; the True Guru gave it to me.<br>
  My search has ended, and I have become stable.<br>
  O Nanak, I have conquered this priceless human life. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  One who has such good karma inscribed upon his forehead, is committed to the Lord's service.<br>
  One whose heart lotus blossoms forth upon meeting the Guru, remains awake and aware, night and day.<br>
  All doubt and fear run away from one who is in love with the Lord's lotus feet.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 090</h2></center>
  He conquers his soul, following the Guru's Teachings, and attains the Imperishable Lord.<br>
  He alone keeps up in this Dark Age of Kali Yuga, who meditates on the Supreme Lord God.<br>
  In the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy, he is immaculate, as if he has bathed at the sixty-eight sacred shrines of pilgrimage.<br>
  He alone is a man of good fortune, who has met with God.<br>
  Nanak is a sacrifice to such a one, whose destiny is so great! ||17||<br>
  Shalok, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  When the Husband Lord is within the heart, then Maya, the bride, goes outside.<br>
  When one's Husband Lord is outside of oneself, then Maya, the bride, is supreme.<br>
  Without the Name, one wanders all around.<br>
  The True Guru shows us that the Lord is with us.<br>
  Servant Nanak merges in the Truest of the True. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Making all sorts of efforts, they wander around; but they do not make even one effort.<br>
  O Nanak, how rare are those who understand the effort which saves the world. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  The greatest of the great, infinite is Your dignity.<br>
  Your colors and hues are so numerous; no one can know Your actions.<br>
  You are the Soul within all souls; You alone know everything.<br>
  Everything is under Your control; Your home is beautiful.<br>
  Your home is filled with bliss, which resonates and resounds throughout Your home.<br>
  Your honor, majesty and glory are Yours alone.<br>
  You are overflowing with all powers; wherever we look, there You are.<br>
  Nanak, the slave of Your slaves, prays to You alone. ||18||<br>
  Shalok, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Your streets are covered with canopies; under them, the traders look beautiful.<br>
  O Nanak, he alone is truly a banker, who buys the infinite commodity. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Kabeer, no one is mine, and I belong to no one.<br>
  I am absorbed in the One, who created this creation. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  The Lord is the most beautiful fruit tree, bearing fruits of Ambrosial Nectar.<br>
  My mind longs to meet Him; how can I ever find Him?<br>
  He has no color or form; He is inaccessible and unconquerable.<br>
  I love Him with all my soul; He opens the door for me.<br>
  I shall serve you forever, if you tell me of my Friend.<br>
  I am a sacrifice, a dedicated, devoted sacrifice to Him.<br>
  The Beloved Saints tell us, to listen with our consciousness.<br>
  One who has such pre-ordained destiny, O slave Nanak, is blessed with the Ambrosial Name by the True Guru. ||19||<br>
  Shalok, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Kabeer, the earth belongs to the Holy, but the thieves have come and now sit among them.<br>
  The earth does not feel their weight; even they profit. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Kabeer, for the sake of the rice, the husks are beaten and threshed.<br>
  When one sits in the company of evil people, then he will be called to account by the Righteous Judge of Dharma. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  He Himself has the greatest family; He Himself is all alone.<br>
  He alone knows His own worth.<br>
  He Himself, by Himself, created everything.<br>
  Only He Himself can describe His own creation.<br>
  Blessed is Your place, where You dwell, Lord.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 091</h2></center>
  Blessed are Your devotees, who see You, O True Lord.<br>
  He alone praises You, who is blessed by Your Grace.<br>
  One who meets the Guru, O Nanak, is immaculate and sanctified. ||20||<br>
  Shalok, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Fareed, this world is beautiful, but there is a thorny garden within it.<br>
  Those who are blessed by their spiritual teacher are not even scratched. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Fareed, blessed is the life, with such a beautiful body.<br>
  How rare are those who are found to love their Beloved Lord. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  He alone obtains meditation, austerities, self-discipline, compassion and Dharmic faith, whom the Lord so blesses.<br>
  He alone meditates on the Naam, the Name of the Lord, whose fire the Lord puts out.<br>
  The Inner-knower, the Searcher of hearts, the Inaccessible Primal Lord, inspires us to look upon all with an impartial eye.<br>
  With the support of the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy, one falls in love with God.<br>
  One's faults are eradicated, and one's face becomes radiant and bright; through the Lord's Name, one crosses over.<br>
  The fear of birth and death is removed, and he is not reincarnated again.<br>
  God lifts him up and pulls him out of the deep, dark pit, and attaches him to the hem of His robe.<br>
  O Nanak, God forgives him, and holds him close in His embrace. ||21||<br>
  Shalok, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  One who loves God is imbued with the deep crimson color of His love.<br>
  O Nanak, such a person is rarely found; the value of such a humble person can never be estimated. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The True Name has pierced the nucleus of my self deep within. Outside, I see the True Lord as well.<br>
  O Nanak, He is pervading and permeating all places, the forests and the meadows, the three worlds, and every hair. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  He Himself created the Universe; He Himself imbues it.<br>
  He Himself is One, and He Himself has numerous forms.<br>
  He Himself is within all, and He Himself is beyond them.<br>
  He Himself is known to be far away, and He Himself is right here.<br>
  He Himself is hidden, and He Himself is revealed.<br>
  No one can estimate the value of Your Creation, Lord.<br>
  You are deep and profound, unfathomable, infinite and invaluable.<br>
  O Nanak, the One Lord is all-pervading. You are the One and only. ||22||1||2||<br>
  Sudh||<br>
  Vaar Of Raamkalee, Uttered By Satta And Balwand The Drummer:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  One who chants the Name of the Almighty Creator - how can his words be judged?<br>
  His divine virtues are the true sisters and brothers; through them, the gift of supreme status is obtained.<br>
  Nanak established the kingdom; He built the true fortress on the strongest foundations.<br>
  He installed the royal canopy over Lehna's head; chanting the Lord's Praises, He drank in the Ambrosial Nectar.<br>
  The Guru implanted the almighty sword of the Teachings to illuminate his soul.<br>
  The Guru bowed down to His disciple, while Nanak was still alive.<br>
  The King, while still alive, applied the ceremonial mark to his forehead. ||1||<br>
  Nanak proclaimed Lehna's succession - he earned it.<br>
  They shared the One Light and the same way; the King just changed His body.<br>
  The immaculate canopy waves over Him, and He sits on the throne in the Guru's shop.<br>
  He does as the Guru commands; He tasted the tasteless stone of Yoga.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 092</h2></center>
  The Langar - the Kitchen of the Guru's Shabad has been opened, and its supplies never run short.<br>
  Whatever His Master gave, He spent; He distributed it all to be eaten.<br>
  The Praises of the Master were sung, and the Divine Light descended from the heavens to the earth.<br>
  Gazing upon You, O True King, the filth of countless past lives is washed away.<br>
  The Guru gave the True Command; why should we hesitate to proclaim this?<br>
  His sons did not obey His Word; they turned their backs on Him as Guru.<br>
  These evil-hearted ones became rebellious; they carry loads of sin on their backs.<br>
  Whatever the Guru said, Lehna did, and so he was installed on the throne.<br>
  Who has lost, and who has won? ||2||<br>
  He who did the work, is accepted as Guru; so which is better - the thistle or the rice?<br>
  The Righteous Judge of Dharma considered the arguments and made the decision.<br>
  Whatever the True Guru says, the True Lord does; it comes to pass instantaneously.<br>
  Guru Angad was proclaimed, and the True Creator confirmed it.<br>
  Nanak merely changed his body; He still sits on the throne, with hundreds of branches reaching out.<br>
  Standing at His door, His followers serve Him; by this service, their rust is scraped off.<br>
  He is the Dervish - the Saint, at the door of His Lord and Master; He loves the True Name, and the Bani of the Guru's Word.<br>
  Balwand says that Khivi, the Guru's wife, is a noble woman, who gives soothing, leafy shade to all.<br>
  She distributes the bounty of the Guru's Langar; the kheer - the rice pudding and ghee, is like sweet ambrosia.<br>
  The faces of the Guru's Sikhs are radiant and bright; the self-willed manmukhs are pale, like straw.<br>
  The Master gave His approval, when Angad exerted Himself heroically.<br>
  Such is the Husband of mother Khivi; He sustains the world. ||3||<br>
  It is as if the Guru made the Ganges flow in the opposite direction, and the world wonders: what has he done?<br>
  Nanak, the Lord, the Lord of the World, spoke the words out loud.<br>
  Making the mountain his churning stick, and the snake-king his churning string, He has churned the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  From it, He extracted the fourteen jewels, and illuminated the world.<br>
  He revealed such creative power, and touched such greatness.<br>
  He raised the royal canopy to wave over the head of Lehna, and raised His glory to the skies.<br>
  His Light merged into the Light, and He blended Him into Himself.<br>
  Guru Nanak tested His Sikhs and His sons, and everyone saw what happened.<br>
  When Lehna alone was found to be pure, then He was set on the throne. ||4||<br>
  Then, the True Guru, the son of Pheru, came to dwell at Khadoor.<br>
  Meditation, austerities and self-discipline rest with You, while the others are filled with excessive pride.<br>
  Greed ruins mankind, like the green algae in the water.<br>
  In the Guru's Court, the Divine Light shines in its creative power.<br>
  You are the cooling peace, whose depth cannot be found.<br>
  You are overflowing with the nine treasures, and the treasure of the Naam, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  Whoever slanders You will be totally ruined and destroyed.<br>
  People of the world can see only what is near at hand, but You can see far beyond.<br>
  Then the True Guru, the son of Pheru, came to dwell at Khadoor. ||5||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 093</h2></center>
  The same mark on the forehead, the same throne, and the same Royal Court.<br>
  Just like the father and grandfather, the son is approved.<br>
  He took the thousand-headed serpent as his churning string, and with the force of devotional love, he churned the ocean of the world with his churning stick, the Sumayr mountain.<br>
  He extracted the fourteen jewels, and brought forth the Divine Light.<br>
  He made intuition his horse, and chastity his saddle.<br>
  He placed the arrow of the Lord's Praise in the bow of Truth.<br>
  In this Dark Age of Kali Yuga, there was only pitch darkness. Then, He rose like the sun to illuminate the darkness.<br>
  He farms the field of Truth, and spreads out the canopy of Truth.<br>
  Your kitchen always has ghee and flour to eat.<br>
  You understand the four corners of the universe; in your mind, the Word of the Shabad is approved and supreme.<br>
  You eliminate the comings and goings of reincarnation, and bestow the insignia of Your Glance of Grace.<br>
  You are the Avataar, the Incarnation of the all-knowing Primal Lord.<br>
  You are not pushed or shaken by the storm and the wind; you are like the Sumayr Mountain.<br>
  You know the inner state of the soul; You are the Knower of knowers.<br>
  How can I praise You, O True Supreme King, when You are so wise and all-knowing?<br>
  Those blessings granted by the Pleasure of the True Guru - please bless Satta with those gifts.<br>
  Seeing Nanak's canopy waving over Your head, everyone was astonished.<br>
  The same mark on the forehead, the same throne, and the same Royal Court.<br>
  Just like the father and grandfather, the son is approved. ||6||<br>
  Blessed, blessed is Guru Raam Daas; He who created You, has also exalted You.<br>
  Perfect is Your miracle; the Creator Lord Himself has installed You on the throne.<br>
  The Sikhs and all the Congregation recognize You as the Supreme Lord God, and bow down to You.<br>
  You are unchanging, unfathomable and immeasurable; You have no end or limitation.<br>
  Those who serve You with love - You carry them across.<br>
  Greed, envy, sexual desire, anger and emotional attachment - You have beaten them and driven them out.<br>
  Blessed is Your place, and True is Your magnificent glory.<br>
  You are Nanak, You are Angad, and You are Amar Daas; so do I recognize You.<br>
  When I saw the Guru, then my mind was comforted and consoled. ||7||<br>
  The four Gurus enlightened the four ages; the Lord Himself assumed the fifth form.<br>
  He created Himself, and He Himself is the supporting pillar.<br>
  He Himself is the paper, He Himself is the pen, and He Himself is the writer.<br>
  All His followers come and go; He alone is fresh and new.<br>
  Guru Arjun sits on the throne; the royal canopy waves over the True Guru.<br>
  From east to west, He illuminates the four directions.<br>
  Those self-willed manmukhs who do not serve the Guru die in shame.<br>
  Your miracles increase two-fold, even four-fold; this is the True Lord's true blessing.<br>
  The four Gurus enlightened the four ages; the Lord Himself assumed the fifth form. ||8||1||<br>
  Raamkalee, The Word Of The Devotees.<br>
  Kabeer Jee:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Make your body the vat, and mix in the yeast. Let the Word of the Guru's Shabad be the molasses.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 094</h2></center>
  Cut up desire, sexuality, anger, pride and envy, and let them be the fermenting bark. ||1||<br>
  Is there any Saint, with intuitive peace and poise deep within, unto whom I might offer my meditation and austerities as payment?<br>
  I dedicate my body and mind to whoever gives me even a drop of this wine from such a vat. ||1||Pause||<br>
  I have made the fourteen worlds the furnace, and I have burnt my body with the fire of God.<br>
  My mudra - my hand-gesture, is the pipe; tuning into the celestial sound current within, the Shushmanaa - the central spinal channel, is my cooling pad. ||2||<br>
  Pilgrimages, fasting, vows, purifications, self-discipline, austerities and breath control through the sun and moon channels - all these I pledge.<br>
  My focused consciousness is the cup, and the Ambrosial Nectar is the pure juice. I drink in the supreme, sublime essence of this juice. ||3||<br>
  The pure stream constantly trickles forth, and my mind is intoxicated by this sublime essence.<br>
  Says Kabeer, all other wines are trivial and tasteless; this is the only true, sublime essence. ||4||1||<br>
  Make spiritual wisdom the molasses, meditation the flowers, and the Fear of God the fire enshrined in your mind.<br>
  The Shushmanaa, the central spinal channel, is intuitively balanced, and the drinker drinks in this wine. ||1||<br>
  O hermit Yogi, my mind is intoxicated.<br>
  When that wine rises up, one tastes the sublime essence of this juice, and sees across the three worlds. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Joining the two channels of the breath, I have lit the furnace, and I drink in the supreme, sublime essence.<br>
  I have burnt both sexual desire and anger, and I have been emancipated from the world. ||2||<br>
  The light of spiritual wisdom enlightens me; meeting with the Guru, the True Guru, I have obtained this understanding.<br>
  Slave Kabeer is intoxicated with that wine, which never wears off. ||3||2||<br>
  You are my Sumayr Mountain, O my Lord and Master; I have grasped Your Support.<br>
  You do not shake, and I do not fall. You have preserved my honor. ||1||<br>
  Now and then, here and there, You, only You.<br>
  By Your Grace, I am forever in peace. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Relying upon You, I can live even in the cursed place of Magahar; You have put out the fire of my body.<br>
  First, I obtained the Blessed Vision of Your Darshan in Magahar; then, I came to dwell at Benares. ||2||<br>
  As is Magahar, so is Benares; I see them as one and the same.<br>
  I am poor, but I have obtained this wealth of the Lord; the proud are bursting with pride, and die. ||3||<br>
  One who takes pride in himself is stuck with thorns; no one can pull them out.<br>
  Here, he cries bitterly, and hereafter, he burns in the most hideous hell. ||4||<br>
  What is hell, and what is heaven? The Saints reject them both.<br>
  I have no obligation to either of them, by the Grace of my Guru. ||5||<br>
  Now, I have mounted to the throne of the Lord; I have met the Lord, the Sustainer of the World.<br>
  The Lord and Kabeer have become one. No one can tell them apart. ||6||3||<br>
  I honor and obey the Saints, and punish the wicked; this is my duty as God's police officer.<br>
  Day and night, I wash Your feet, Lord; I wave my hair as the chauree, to brush away the flies. ||1||<br>
  I am a dog at Your Court, Lord.<br>
  I open my snout and bark before it. ||1||Pause||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 095</h2></center>
  In my past life, I was Your servant; now, I cannot leave You.<br>
  The celestial sound current resounds at Your Door. Your insignia is stamped upon my forehead. ||2||<br>
  Those who are branded with Your brand fight bravely in battle; those without Your brand run away.<br>
  One who becomes a Holy person, appreciates the value of devotional worship to the Lord. The Lord places him in His treasury. ||3||<br>
  In the fortress is the chamber; by contemplative meditation it becomes the supreme chamber.<br>
  The Guru has blessed Kabeer with the commodity, saying, "Take this commodity; cherish it and keep it secure."||4||<br>
  Kabeer gives it to the world, but he alone receives it, upon whose forehead such destiny is recorded.<br>
  Permanent is the marriage, of one who receives this ambrosial essence. ||5||4||<br>
  O Brahmin, how can you forget the One, from whose mouth the Vedas and the Gayitri prayer issured forth?<br>
  The whole world falls at His feet; why don't you chant the Name of that Lord, O Pandit? ||1||<br>
  Why, O my Brahmin, do you not chant the Lord's Name?<br>
  If you don't chant the Lord's Name, O Pandit, you will only suffer in hell. ||1||Pause||<br>
  You think that you are high, but you take food from the houses of the lowly; you fill up your belly by forcibly practicing your rituals.<br>
  On the fourteenth day, and the night of the new moon, you go out begging; even though you hold the lamp in your hands, still, you fall into the pit. ||2||<br>
  You are a Brahmin, and I am only a weaver from Benares. How can I compare to you?<br>
  Chanting the Lord's Name, I have been saved; relying on the Vedas, O Brahmin, you shall drown and die. ||3||5||<br>
  There is a single tree, with countless branches and twigs; its flowers and leaves are filled with its juice.<br>
  This world is a garden of Ambrosial Nectar. The Perfect Lord created it. ||1||<br>
  I have come to know the story of my Sovereign Lord.<br>
  How rare is that Gurmukh who knows, and whose inner being is illumined by the Lord's Light. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The bumble bee, addicted to the nectar of the twelve-petalled flowers, enshrines it in the heart.<br>
  He holds his breath suspended in the sixteen-petalled sky of the Akaashic Ethers, and beats his wings in esctasy. ||2||<br>
  In the profound void of intuitive Samaadhi, the one tree rises up; it soaks up the water of desire from the ground.<br>
  Says Kabeer, I am the servant of those who have seen this celestial tree. ||3||6||<br>
  Make silence your ear-rings, and compassion your wallet; let meditation be your begging bowl.<br>
  Sew this body as your patched coat, and take the Lord's Name as your support. ||1||<br>
  Practice such Yoga, O Yogi.<br>
  As Gurmukh, enjoy meditation, austerities and self-discipline. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Apply the ashes of wisdom to your body; let your horn be your focused consciousness.<br>
  Become detached, and wander through the city of your body; play the harp of your mind. ||2||<br>
  Enshrine the five tatvas - the five elements, within your heart; let your deep meditative trance be undisturbed.<br>
  Says Kabeer, listen, O Saints: make righteousness and compassion your garden. ||3||7||<br>
  For what purpose were you created and brought into the world? What rewards have you received in this life?<br>
  God is the boat to carry you across the terrifying world-ocean; He is the Fulfiller of the mind's desires. You have not centered your mind on Him, even for an instant. ||1||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 096</h2></center>
  O Lord of the Universe, I am such a sinner!<br>
  God gave me body and soul, but I have not practiced loving devotional worship to Him. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Others' wealth, others' bodies, others' wives, others' slander and others' fights - I have not given them up.<br>
  For the sake of these, coming and going in reincarnation happens over and over again, and this story never ends. ||2||<br>
  That house, in which the Saints speak of the Lord - I have not visited it, even for an instant.<br>
  Drunkards, thieves, and evil-doers - I constantly dwell with them. ||3||<br>
  Sexual desire, anger, the wine of Maya, and envy - these are what I collect within myself.<br>
  Compassion, righteousness, and service to the Guru - these do not visit me, even in my dreams. ||4||<br>
  He is merciful to the meek, compassionate and benevolent, the Lover of His devotees, the Destroyer of fear.<br>
  Says Kabeer, please protect Your humble servant from disaster; O Lord, I serve only You. ||5||8||<br>
  Remembering Him in meditation, the door of liberation is found.<br>
  You shall go to heaven, and not return to this earth.<br>
  In the home of the Fearless Lord, the celestial trumpets resound.<br>
  The unstruck sound current will vibrate and resonate forever. ||1||<br>
  Practice such meditative remembrance in your mind.<br>
  Without this meditative remembrance, liberation will never be found. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Remembering Him in meditation, you will meet with no obstruction.<br>
  You will be liberated, and the great load will be taken away.<br>
  Bow in humility within your heart,<br>
  and you will not have to be reincarnated over and over again. ||2||<br>
  Remember Him in meditation, celebrate and be happy.<br>
  God has placed His lamp deep within you, which burns without any oil.<br>
  That lamp makes the world immortal;<br>
  it conquers and drives out the poisons of sexual desire and anger. ||3||<br>
  Remembering Him in meditation, you shall obtain salvation.<br>
  Wear that meditative remembrance as your necklace.<br>
  Practice that meditative remembrance, and never let it go.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, you shall cross over. ||4||<br>
  Remembering Him in meditation, you shall not be obligated to others.<br>
  You shall sleep in your mansion, in blankets of silk.<br>
  Your soul shall blossom forth in happiness, on this comfortable bed.<br>
  So drink in this meditative remembrance, night and day. ||5||<br>
  Remembering Him in meditation, your troubles will depart.<br>
  Remembering Him in meditation, Maya will not bother you.<br>
  Meditate, meditate in remembrance on the Lord, Har, Har, and sing His Praises in your mind.<br>
  This meditative remembrance is obtained from the True Guru. ||6||<br>
  Forever and ever, remember Him, day and night,<br>
  while standing up and sitting down, with every breath and morsel of food.<br>
  While awake and asleep, enjoy the essence of this meditative remembrance.<br>
  The Lord's meditative remembrance is obtained by good destiny. ||7||<br>
  Remembering Him in meditation, you shall not be loaded down.<br>
  Make this meditative remembrance of the Lord's Name your Support.<br>
  Says Kabeer, He has no limits;<br>
  no tantras or mantras can be used against Him. ||8||9||<br>
  Raamkalee, Second House, The Word Of Kabeer Jee:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Maya, the Trapper, has sprung her trap.<br>
  The Guru, the Liberated One, has put out the fire.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 097</h2></center>
  When I came to understand this mind, from the tips of my toes to the crown of my head,<br>
  then I took my cleansing bath, deep within my self. ||1||<br>
  The mind, the master of the breath, abides in the state of supreme bliss.<br>
  There is no death, no re-birth, and no aging for me now. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Turning away from materialism, I have found intuitive support.<br>
  I have entered into the sky of the mind, and opened the Tenth Gate.<br>
  The chakras of the coiled Kundalini energy have been opened,<br>
  and I have met my Sovereign Lord King without fear. ||2||<br>
  My attachment to Maya has been eradicated;<br>
  the moon energy has devoured the sun energy.<br>
  When I was focused and merged into the all-pervading Lord,<br>
  then the unstruck sound current began to vibrate. ||3||<br>
  The Speaker has spoken, and proclaimed the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  The hearer has heard, and enshrined it in the mind.<br>
  Chanting to the Creator, one crosses over.<br>
  Says Kabeer, this is the essence. ||4||1||10||<br>
  The moon and the sun are both the embodiment of light.<br>
  Within their light, is God, the incomparable. ||1||<br>
  O spiritual teacher, contemplate God.<br>
  In this light is contained the expanse of the created universe. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Gazing upon the diamond, I humbly salute this diamond.<br>
  Says Kabeer, the Immaculate Lord is indescribable. ||2||2||11||<br>
  People of the world, remain awake and aware. Even though you are awake, you are being robbed, O Siblings of Destiny.<br>
  While the Vedas stand guard watching, the Messenger of Death carries you away. ||1||Pause||<br>
  He thinks that the bitter nimm fruit is a mango, and the mango is a bitter nimm. He imagines the ripe banana on the thorny bush.<br>
  He thinks that the ripe coconut hangs on the barren simmal tree; what a stupid, idiotic fool he is! ||1||<br>
  The Lord is like sugar, spilled onto the sand; the elephant cannot pick it up.<br>
  Says Kabeer, give up your ancestry, social status and honor; be like the tiny ant - pick up and eat the sugar. ||2||3||12||<br>
  The Word Of Naam Dayv Jee, Raamkalee, First House:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  The boy takes paper, cuts it and makes a kite, and flies it in the sky.<br>
  Talking with his friends, he still keeps his attention on the kite string. ||1||<br>
  My mind has been pierced by the Name of the Lord,<br>
  like the goldsmith, whose attention is held by his work. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The young girl in the city takes a pitcher, and fills it with water.<br>
  She laughs, and plays, and talks with her friends, but she keeps her attention focused on the pitcher of water. ||2||<br>
  The cow is let loose, out of the mansion of the ten gates, to graze in the field.<br>
  It grazes up to five miles away, but keeps its attention focused on its calf. ||3||<br>
  Says Naam Dayv, listen, O Trilochan: the child is laid down in the cradle.<br>
  Its mother is at work, inside and outside, but she holds her child in her thoughts. ||4||1||<br>
  There are countless Vedas, Puraanas and Shaastras; I do not sing their songs and hymns.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 098</h2></center>
  In the imperishable realm of the Formless Lord, I play the flute of the unstruck sound current. ||1||<br>
  Becoming detached, I sing the Lord's Praises.<br>
  Imbued with the unattached, unstruck Word of the Shabad, I shall go to the home of the Lord, who has no ancestors. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Then, I shall no longer control the breath through the energy channels of the Ida, Pingala and Shushmanaa.<br>
  I look upon both the moon and the sun as the same, and I shall merge in the Light of God. ||2||<br>
  I do not go to see sacred shrines of pilgrimage, or bathe in their waters; I do not bother any beings or creatures.<br>
  The Guru has shown me the sixty-eight places of pilgrimage within my own heart, where I now take my cleansing bath. ||3||<br>
  I do not pay attention to anyone praising me, or calling me good and nice.<br>
  Says Naam Dayv, my consciousness is imbued with the Lord; I am absorbed in the profound state of Samaadhi. ||4||2||<br>
  When there was no mother and no father, no karma and no human body,<br>
  when I was not and you were not, then who came from where? ||1||<br>
  O Lord, no one belongs to anyone else.<br>
  We are like birds perched on a tree. ||1||Pause||<br>
  When there was no moon and no sun, then water and air were blended together.<br>
  When there were no Shaastras and no Vedas, then where did karma come from? ||2||<br>
  Control of the breath and positioning of the tongue, focusing at the third eye and wearing malas of tulsi beads, are all obtained through Guru's Grace.<br>
  Naam Dayv prays, this is the supreme essence of reality; the True Guru has inspired this realization. ||3||3||<br>
  RAAMKALEE, SECOND HOUSE:<br>
  Someone may practice austerities at Benares, or die upside-down at a sacred shrine ofpilgrimage, or burn his body in fire, or rejuvenate his body to life almost forever;<br>
  he may perform the horse-sacrifice ceremony, or give donations of gold covered over, but none of these is equal to the worship of the Lord's Name. ||1||<br>
  O hypocrite, renounce and abandon your hypocrisy; do not practice deception.<br>
  Constantly, continually, chant the Name of the Lord. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Someone may go to the Ganges or the Godaavari, or to the Kumbha festival, or bathe at Kaydaar Naat'h, or make donations of thousands of cows at Gomti;<br>
  he may make millions of pilgrimages to sacred shrines, or freeze his body in the Himalayas; still, none of these is equal to the worship of the Lord's Name. ||2||<br>
  Someone may give away horses and elephants, or women on their beds, or land; he may give such gifts over and over again.<br>
  He may purify his soul, and give away in charity his body weight in gold; none of these is equal to the worship of the Lord's Name. ||3||<br>
  Do not harbor anger in your mind, or blame the Messenger of Death; instead, realize the immaculate state of Nirvaanaa.<br>
  My Sovereign Lord King is Raam Chandra, the Son of the King Dasrat'h; prays Naam Dayv, I drink in the Ambrosial Nectar. ||4||4||<br>
  Raamkalee, The Word Of Ravi Daas Jee:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  They read and reflect upon all the Names of God; they listen, but they do not see the Lord, the embodiment of love and intuition.<br>
  How can iron be transformed into gold, unless it touches the Philosopher's Stone? ||1||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 22 - Raag Raamkalee - Part 099</h2></center>
  O Divine Lord, the knot of skepticism cannot be untied.<br>
  Sexual desire, anger, Maya, intoxication and jealousy - these five have combined to plunder the world. ||1||Pause||<br>
  I am a great poet, of noble heritage; I am a Pandit, a religious scholar, a Yogi and a Sannyaasi;<br>
  I am a spiritual teacher, a warrior and a giver - such thinking never ends. ||2||<br>
  Says Ravi Daas, no one understands; they all run around, deluded like madmen.<br>
  The Lord's Name is my only Support; He is my life, my breath of life, my wealth. ||3||1||<br>
  Raamkalee, The Word Of Baynee Jee:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  The energy channels of the Ida, Pingala and Shushmanaa: these three dwell in one place.<br>
  This is the true place of confluence of the three sacred rivers: this is where my mind takes its cleansing bath. ||1||<br>
  O Saints, the Immaculate Lord dwells there;<br>
  how rare are those who go to the Guru, and understand this.<br>
  The all-pervading immaculate Lord is there. ||1||Pause||<br>
  What is the insignia of the Divine Lord's dwelling?<br>
  The unstruck sound current of the Shabad vibrates there.<br>
  There is no moon or sun, no air or water there.<br>
  The Gurmukh becomes aware, and knows the Teachings. ||2||<br>
  Spiritual wisdom wells up, and evil-mindedness departs;<br>
  the nucleus of the mind sky is drenched with Ambrosial Nectar.<br>
  One who knows the secret of this device,<br>
  meets the Supreme Divine Guru. ||3||<br>
  The Tenth Gate is the home of the inaccessible, infinite Supreme Lord.<br>
  Above the store is a niche, and within this niche is the commodity. ||4||<br>
  One who remains awake, never sleeps.<br>
  The three qualities and the three worlds vanish, in the state of Samaadhi.<br>
  He takes the Beej Mantra, the Seed Mantra, and keeps it in his heart.<br>
  Turning his mind away from the world, he focuses on the cosmic void of the absolute Lord. ||5||<br>
  He remains awake, and he does not lie.<br>
  He keeps the five sensory organs under his control.<br>
  He cherishes in his consciousness the Guru's Teachings.<br>
  He dedicates his mind and body to the Lord's Love. ||6||<br>
  He considers his hands to be the leaves and branches of the tree.<br>
  He does not lose his life in the gamble.<br>
  He plugs up the source of the river of evil tendencies.<br>
  Turning away from the west, he makes the sun rise in the east.<br>
  He bears the unbearable, and the drops trickle down within;<br>
  then, he speaks with the Lord of the world. ||7||<br>
  The four-sided lamp illuminates the Tenth Gate.<br>
  The Primal Lord is at the center of the countless leaves.<br>
  He Himself abides there with all His powers.<br>
  He weaves the jewels into the pearl of the mind. ||8||<br>
  The lotus is at the forehead, and the jewels surround it.<br>
  Within it is the Immaculate Lord, the Master of the three worlds.<br>
  The Panch Shabad, the five primal sounds, resound and vibrate their in their purity.<br>
  The chauris - the fly brushes wave, and the conch shells blare like thunder.<br>
  The Gurmukh tramples the demons underfoot with his spiritual wisdom.<br>
  Baynee longs for Your Name, Lord. ||9||1||<br>
